<p><b><a href="/wiki/July" title="July">July</a></b> <b><a href="/wiki/2011" title="2011">2011</a></b> was the seventh month of that common year. The month, which began on a <a href="/wiki/Friday" title="Friday">Friday</a>, ended on a <a href="/wiki/Sunday" title="Sunday">Sunday</a> after 31 days.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_holidays">International holidays</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/July_2011&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: International holidays">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>(See Holidays and observances, on sidebar at right, below)</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portal:Current_events"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Portal:Current events</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/July_2011&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Portal:Current events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>This is an <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events/How_to_archive_the_portal" title="Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal">archived version</a> of Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Current events Portal</a> from July 2011.</i></p>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background-color:transparent">
<tr>
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div id="2011_July_1"></div>
<div id="2011_July_01"></div>
<table class="vevent" style="width:100%; margin:7px 0px; padding:2px; background-color:white; border:1px #cef2e0 solid;">
<tr>
<td>
<table cellspacing="0" class="plainlinks" style="background-color:#cef2e0" width="100%">
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 1, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-01</span>)</span> (Friday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_1&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_1&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Office_of_the_High_Commissioner_for_Human_Rights" title="Office of the High Commissioner for Human Rights">Office of the High Commissioner for Human Rights</a> claims the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Congo</a> government troops <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_rape" title="War rape">raped</a> 121 women between June 11 and 13 then pillaged their villages. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/un-reports-that-121-women-raped-by-congo-troops-in-restive-east/2011/07/01/AG5UiGtH_story.html?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>:
<ul>
<li>Hundreds of thousands of people protest against the regime nationwide as the crackdown against civilians continues. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-13988701" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The death toll is reported to be at least 11 in Syria today. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/20117112504223572.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Rebels withdraw from the town of <a href="/wiki/Bir_al-Ghanam" title="Bir al-Ghanam">Bir al-Ghanam</a>, 80km south of <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a> after coming under rocket attack from forces loyal to <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/commoditiesNews/idAFLDE7600JZ20110701" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>, speaking via an audio message broadcast to a square in central <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>, calls on <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> to stop its bombing campaign or he will target European "homes, offices, families". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-13997322" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201171181812716313.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Members at the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> summit in <a href="/wiki/Equatorial_Guinea" title="Equatorial Guinea">Equatorial Guinea</a> express annoyance at <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a>'s intervention in Libya over fears that it is only making the situation worse. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/20117171321504965.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_uprising" title="2011 Bahraini uprising">2011 Bahraini uprising</a>: Some <a href="/wiki/Expatriate" title="Expatriate">expatriate</a> <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrainis</a> are sent "loyalty pledges" in light of the uprising. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43590958" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_uprising" title="2011 Yemeni uprising">2011 Yemeni uprising</a>: Demonstrations are held in the capital <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a> and across the country, while protesters in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ta%27izz" title="Ta'izz">Ta'izz</a> chant slogans against a possible <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabian</a> intervention, "Tell Saudi Arabia that Yemen is a republic" and "Yemen is not Bahrain", in reference to Saudi Arabia's suppression of the Bahraini uprising. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201171141613329512.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II" title="Freedom Flotilla II">Freedom Flotilla II</a>:
<ul>
<li>Activists increase their guard of the remaining boats bound for Gaza following the alleged sabotage of other boats. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Israel/Article.aspx?id=227547" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/indepth/features/2011/07/201171142616817763.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greek</a> authorities prevented a US-flagged vessel, <i><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II#Ships" title="Freedom Flotilla II">The Audacity of Hope</a></i>, carrying dozens of U.S. activists, from departing for the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza Strip</a>, towing it back to the port of <a href="/wiki/Perama" title="Perama">Perama</a> after commandos, reportedly carrying weapons, intercept it. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201171143845732109.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Israel/Article.aspx?id=227600" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Albert_II,_Prince_of_Monaco" title="Albert II, Prince of Monaco">Albert II, Prince of Monaco</a> weds <a href="/wiki/Charlene,_Princess_of_Monaco" title="Charlene, Princess of Monaco">Charlene Wittstock</a>, the Olympic swimmer, at the royal palace; Wittstock becomes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Monegasque_consorts" title="List of Monegasque consorts">Her Serene Highness, Princess</a> Charlene. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-13973248" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Bank_of_Moscow" title="Bank of Moscow">Bank of Moscow</a></i>, the fifth largest bank in Russia, in record <a href="/wiki/Bailout" title="Bailout">bailout</a> of $14 billion, after the discovery that almost a third of the bank's <a href="/wiki/Asset" title="Asset">assets</a> are "problematic," the <a href="/wiki/Central_Bank_of_Russia" title="Central Bank of Russia">Central Bank of Russia</a> said.<a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-13999509" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.themoscowtimes.com/business/article/bank-of-moscow-gets-record-bailout/439955.html" rel="nofollow">(Moscow Times)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_Japan" title="Bank of Japan">Bank of Japan</a> survey shows that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Business_confidence" title="Business confidence">business confidence</a> has fallen markedly since the <a href="/wiki/2011_T%C5%8Dhoku_earthquake_and_tsunami" title="2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami">2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/japan-central-bank-survey-shows-business-confidence-down-sharply-after-tsunami/2011/06/30/AGP5kksH_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Manufacturing activity in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> is at its lowest level in more than two years after three successive months of falls indicating a continued slowdown. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304450604576418570501579448.html?mod=googlenews_wsj" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/home/asia" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The towns of <a href="/wiki/Colman,_South_Dakota" title="Colman, South Dakota">Colman</a> and <a href="/wiki/Flandreau,_South_Dakota" title="Flandreau, South Dakota">Flandreau</a> in the US state of <a href="/wiki/South_Dakota" title="South Dakota">South Dakota</a> are hit by a heavy storm resulting in the loss of power for several days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.argusleader.com/article/20110701/ARGUS911/110701049/Argus-911-update-Colman-Flandreau-may-lack-power-days" rel="nofollow">(Argus Leader)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Yonhap" title="Yonhap">Yonhap</a> News Agency reports that <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> is tightening border controls with <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> to stop defections. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/01/0200000000AEN20110701002800315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> takes over the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Presidency_of_the_European_Union" title="Presidency of the European Union">Presidency</a> of <a href="/wiki/Presidency_of_the_Council_of_the_European_Union" title="Presidency of the Council of the European Union">the Council of</a> the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> for six months. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-13985064" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> court declares books and brochures by <a href="/wiki/Scientology" title="Scientology">Scientology</a> founder <a href="/wiki/L._Ron_Hubbard" title="L. Ron Hubbard">L. Ron Hubbard</a> as "extremist", banning them from distribution in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.themoscowtimes.com/news/article/scientology-literature-declared-extremist/439845.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Moscow Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jUJK_3YqRLgnDtnGzEF_rEp2lkDQ?docId=f4bd741df1ca4130a85405f1cbda5ca2" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Australian_Federal_Police" title="Australian Federal Police">Australian Federal Police</a> charges six senior executives, all former employees of two companies owned by the <a href="/wiki/Reserve_Bank_of_Australia" title="Reserve Bank of Australia">Reserve Bank of Australia</a>, Securency and Note Printing Australia, in relation to alleged bribery of officials in <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> and <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/business/securency-bosses-arrested-20110701-1gtr8.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/more-news/six-people-linked-to-note-maker-securency-arrest-for-alleged-bribery/story-fn7x8me2-1226085465195" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald-Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>Dominique Strauss-Kahn
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> reports that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dominique_Strauss-Kahn_sexual_assault_case" title="Dominique Strauss-Kahn sexual assault case">sexual assault case</a> against former <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> head <a href="/wiki/Dominique_Strauss-Kahn" title="Dominique Strauss-Kahn">Dominique Strauss-Kahn</a> is on the verge of collapse due to concerns over the credibility of the alleged victim's testimony. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/01/nyregion/strauss-kahn-case-seen-as-in-jeopardy.html/?_r=1&amp;smid=tw-nytimes" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A judge releases him from house arrest as prosecutors said that the maid had made false statements. <a class="external text" href="http://www.montrealgazette.com/news/Strauss+Kahn+dines+York+after+release/5037332/story.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Montreal Gazette</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110701-strauss-kahn-released-house-arrest-amid-doubts-about-accuser" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chosunilbo" title="Chosunilbo">Chosunilbo</a></i> newspaper in <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> reports that <a href="/wiki/Kim_Pyong-il" title="Kim Pyong-il">Kim Pyong-il</a>, the half-brother of current <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a>, is under house arrest in <a href="/wiki/Pyongyang" title="Pyongyang">Pyongyang</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.kyodonews.jp/news/2011/07/100379.html" rel="nofollow">(Kyodo News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Italy" title="Law enforcement in Italy">Italian police</a> arrest the <a href="/wiki/Mafia" title="Mafia">Mafia</a> boss of <a href="/wiki/Corleone" title="Corleone">Corleone</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sicily" title="Sicily">Sicily</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110701-italian-police-arrest-corleone-mafia-boss" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Danish_people" title="Danish people">Danish</a> drug company <a href="/wiki/Lundbeck" title="Lundbeck">Lundbeck</a> restricts use of its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nembutal" title="Nembutal">Nembutal</a> drug to stop its use in <a href="/wiki/Lethal_injection" title="Lethal injection">lethal injections</a> in some US states. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110701-danish-firm-prevent-use-drug-executions" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Sixth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Sixth Circuit">A US Federal Appeals Court</a> overturns the <a href="/wiki/Michigan_Civil_Rights_Initiative" title="Michigan Civil Rights Initiative">Michigan Civil Rights Initiative</a> banning the use of race and gender preferences in college admissions and government hiring and contracting in the US state of Michigan. <a class="external text" href="http://detnews.com/article/20110701/SCHOOLS/107010416/State-to-fight-ruling-against-ban-on-race-in-college-admissions#ixzz1QtJdL7BL" rel="nofollow">(<i>Detroit News</i>)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">British Conservative</a> peer and leader of <a href="/wiki/Essex_County_Council" title="Essex County Council">Essex County Council</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paul_White,_Baron_Hanningfield" title="Paul White, Baron Hanningfield">Lord Hanningfield</a> is jailed for nine months for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Parliamentary_expenses_scandal" title="United Kingdom Parliamentary expenses scandal">fiddling his parliamentary expenses</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-13989329" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> president <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> makes his first speech since receiving treatment for cancer in <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14351508" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> celebrates the 144th anniversary of the enactment of its <a href="/wiki/Constitution_Act,_1867" title="Constitution Act, 1867">Constitution Act</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/story/2011/07/01/will-kate-visit-day2.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a></li>
<li>The government of the <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">Minnesota</a> is to shut down as a result of a budget dispute between <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic</a> <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Minnesota" title="Governor of Minnesota">Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Mark_Dayton" title="Mark Dayton">Mark Dayton</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minnesota_State_Legislature" title="Minnesota State Legislature">Legislature</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/politics/statelocal/124824189.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Star-Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5i-wB7Drzy1MfhL8_VpcVTMC6g3-Q?docId=49f917e92379476e971a48626e8a3520" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.politico.com/news/stories/0611/58107.html" rel="nofollow">(Politico)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> votes in <a href="/wiki/Moroccan_constitutional_referendum,_2011" title="Moroccan constitutional referendum, 2011">a constitutional referendum</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/20117154535570851.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">British Labour Party</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Iain_McKenzie" title="Iain McKenzie">Iain McKenzie</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Inverclyde_by-election,_2011" title="Inverclyde by-election, 2011">Inverclyde by-election</a> with a majority reduced from 14,416 in 2010 to 5,838. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-scotland-glasgow-west-13980594" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Leon_Panetta" title="Leon Panetta">Leon Panetta</a> is sworn in as the new <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Defense" title="United States Secretary of Defense">United States Secretary of Defense</a>, succeeding <a href="/wiki/Robert_Gates" title="Robert Gates">Robert Gates</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-13998664" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a>, owners in the <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North American</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">National Basketball Association</a> commence a <a href="/wiki/Lockout_(industry)" title="Lockout (industry)">lockout</a> after failing to reach a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Collective_bargaining_agreement" title="Collective bargaining agreement">collective bargaining agreement</a> with players. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/AP56ea7d680e854fe7bba310256d0bd49a.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Nadal" title="Rafael Nadal">Rafael Nadal</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Andy_Murray" title="Andy Murray">Andy Murray</a> in the semi-final of <a href="/wiki/2011_Wimbledon_Championships" title="2011 Wimbledon Championships">Wimbledon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/tennis/13991175.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>According to <i>The Daily Telegraph</i>, the <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> army invades <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>, taking control of the southeastern town of Al-<a href="/wiki/Kufra" title="Kufra">Kufra</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/libya/8611199/Sudanese-army-seizes-southern-Libyan-town.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>Libyan rebel leaders welcome an <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> offer to open talks with the Government in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a> without the direct involvement of <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14003786?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Syria" title="List of heads of state of Syria">President of Syria</a> <a href="/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad" title="Bashar al-Assad">Bashar al-Assad</a> sacks <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ahmad_Khaled_Abdel_Aziz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ahmad Khaled Abdel Aziz (page does not exist)">Ahmad Khaled Abdel Aziz</a>, the governor of the city of <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a>, after mass anti-government demonstrations occurred there yesterday. <a class="external text" href="http://gulfnews.com/news/region/syria/assad-sacks-governor-of-syrian-flashpoint-city-hama-state-tv-1.831577" rel="nofollow">(<i>Gulf News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sana.sy/eng/21/2011/07/02/355963.htm" rel="nofollow">(Syrian Arab News Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14000995" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011729129878700.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Moroccan_protests" title="2011 Moroccan protests">2011 Moroccan protests</a>: Demonstrations are called for following <a href="/wiki/Moroccan_constitutional_referendum,_2011" title="Moroccan constitutional referendum, 2011">a constitutional referendum</a> on greater freedoms held yesterday. <a class="external text" href="http://ca.reuters.com/article/topNews/idCATRE76019220110702?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somali</a> and <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> forces make gains against <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabaab</a> rebels in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/20117242810884556.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>11 members of one family are killed by a roadside bomb in southern <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> while traveling to <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/07/201172761852532.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Albert_II,_Prince_of_Monaco" title="Albert II, Prince of Monaco">Albert II, Prince of Monaco</a> marries <a href="/wiki/Charlene,_Princess_of_Monaco" title="Charlene, Princess of Monaco">Charlene Wittstock</a>, the Olympic swimmer, again, this time in a religious ceremony attended by 3,500 guests, including royalty and celebrities. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-13999817" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_sovereign_debt_crisis" title="European sovereign debt crisis">European sovereign debt crisis</a>: <a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">Eurozone</a> finance ministers agree to give a further €12 billion over the next two weeks to <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> as it fights bankruptcy. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14003788" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/201172205557387368.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Civil_Aviation_Safety_Authority" title="Civil Aviation Safety Authority">Civil Aviation Safety Authority</a> grounds all <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tiger_Airways" title="Tiger Airways">Tiger Airways</a> flights in the country until July 9 due to a range of safety concerns. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-national/casa-says-it-lost-confidence-in-tiger-20110702-1gvs0.html" rel="nofollow">(AAP via <i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>3 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coal_mine" title="Coal mine">coal miners</a> are killed and 40 others are trapped in separate incidents in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsday.com/news/nation/40-miners-trapped-3-dead-in-china-s-disasters-1.3000085" rel="nofollow">(AP via Newsday - <i>sub. req.</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/china/2011-07/03/content_12823951.htm" rel="nofollow">(China Daily)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_people" title="Mexican people">Mexican</a> authorities have confirmed 11 deaths from <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Arlene_(2011)" title="Tropical Storm Arlene (2011)">Tropical Storm Arlene</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/news/world/2011-07-02-mexico-tropical-storm-arlene_n.htm" rel="nofollow">(AP via USA Today)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ExxonMobil" title="ExxonMobil">ExxonMobil</a> workers attempt to contain an <a href="/wiki/Oil_spill" title="Oil spill">oil spill</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Yellowstone_River" title="Yellowstone River">Yellowstone River</a> in the US state of <a href="/wiki/Montana" title="Montana">Montana</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/greenspace/2011/07/exxon-pipeline-spill-on-yellowstone-river.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>228 people are arrested during a large demonstration in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> amid frustration with government policies and rising property prices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gjkwi6jd9oNLwY-iSVLqg_Kxzcsw?docId=CNG.34a11628a7892b6c861a8ffb743aafa7.391" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/07/02/idINIndia-58049320110702" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> jails a <a href="/wiki/Tibet" title="Tibet">Tibetan</a> writer for editing a banned magazine regarding <a href="/wiki/2008_Tibetan_unrest" title="2008 Tibetan unrest">unrest in 2008</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jzZQCl0IStRvLQas7a_zg26B_GfA?docId=CNG.34a11628a7892b6c861a8ffb743aafa7.631" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/02/us-china-tibet-writer-idUSTRE7610GJ20110702" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14001956" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President of Brazil</a> and current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_Brazil" title="Senate of Brazil">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/Itamar_Franco" title="Itamar Franco">Itamar Franco</a> dies of complications from <a href="/wiki/Leukemia" title="Leukemia">leukemia</a>; seven days of mourning are declared by current president <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/americas/07/02/brazil.former.president/index.html?eref=edition_americas" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14004407" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Campaigning closes ahead of <a href="/wiki/Thai_general_election,_2011" title="Thai general election, 2011">Thailand's general election</a> tomorrow. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/video/asia-pacific/2011/07/20117251016934132.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II" title="Freedom Flotilla II">Freedom Flotilla II</a>: Greek port authorities arrest the captain of the US-flagged vessel <i><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II#Ships" title="Freedom Flotilla II">The Audacity of Hope</a></i>, the latest incident to befall the flotilla following two counts of alleged sabotage and the towing back to port of this ship yesterday. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201172143643709749.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Israel/Article.aspx?id=227581" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a> sign the first accords between the two nations since Kosovo's declaration of independence three years ago. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/201172202625940367.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Petra_Kvitov%C3%A1" title="Petra Kvitová">Petra Kvitová</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Maria_Sharapova" title="Maria Sharapova">Maria Sharapova</a> to win the <a href="/wiki/2011_Wimbledon_Championships" title="2011 Wimbledon Championships">Wimbledon championship</a> in <a href="/wiki/2011_Wimbledon_Championships_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_Singles" title="2011 Wimbledon Championships – Women's Singles">women's singles</a>. It is Kvitová's first <a href="/wiki/Grand_Slam_(tennis)" title="Grand Slam (tennis)">Grand Slam</a> victory. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/tennis/14002512.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/sport/2011/jul/02/wimbledon-2011-petra-kvitova-profile" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li>Dozens of people are arrested and <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> is used during Independence Day celebrations in <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> after a "clapping" protest. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/201173184516320207.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14006365" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Police and protesters clash in <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> over a gas exploration deal with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ConocoPhilips" title="ConocoPhilips">ConocoPhilips</a>; 150 people are detained. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14006936" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bdnews24.com/details.php?id=199958&amp;cid=3" rel="nofollow">(Bangladesh News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: The Syrian army encircles the city of <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> after one of the largest protests against the regime of <a href="/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad" title="Bashar al-Assad">Bashar al-Assad</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/world/story/2011/07/03/syria-sunday.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_uprising" title="2011 Bahraini uprising">2011 Bahraini uprising</a>: Violent clashes erupt in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shia" title="Shia">Shia</a> village during a "national dialogue" in <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/f5da391a-a59a-11e0-83b2-00144feabdc0.html#axzz1R4zgzb00" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Financial Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Moroccan_protests" title="2011 Moroccan protests">2011 Moroccan protests</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/February_20_Movement" title="February 20 Movement">February 20 Movement</a> rejects <a href="/wiki/Moroccan_constitutional_referendum,_2011" title="Moroccan constitutional referendum, 2011">last Friday's constitutional referendum</a> as nationwide demonstrations against the regime continue. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/20117321108674406.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>: Turkey recognizes the <a href="/wiki/National_Transitional_Council" title="National Transitional Council">National Transitional Council</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Anti-Gaddafi_forces" title="Anti-Gaddafi forces">anti-Gaddafi forces</a>, with <a href="/wiki/List_of_Ministers_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Turkey)" title="List of Ministers of Foreign Affairs (Turkey)">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ahmet_Davuto%C4%9Flu" title="Ahmet Davutoğlu">Ahmet Davutoğlu</a> meeting with rebel leaders in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a> and offering at least $200 million in aid. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201173145538817561.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14009206" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II" title="Freedom Flotilla II">Freedom Flotilla II</a>:
<ul>
<li>Members of the Dutch-Italian vessel issue an open letter to the Greek prime minister <a href="/wiki/Georgios_Papandreou" title="Georgios Papandreou">Georgios Papandreou</a> following the alleged sabotage of two ships and the prevention of the rest from setting sail for <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/201173115538534109.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2011/7/3/nation/9023408&amp;sec=nation" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysia Star</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/07/04/3259958.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
<li>Israeli foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Avigdor_Lieberman" title="Avigdor Lieberman">Avigdor Lieberman</a>, speaking on radio, welcomes a diplomatic victory after its attempts to stop the flotilla from setting sail to Gaza are assisted by the Greek ban on the ships from leaving port. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/middleeast/israel/8614090/Israel-claims-diplomatic-victory-as-Greece-stops-Gaza-flotilla.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>According to reports in the <i><a href="/wiki/Toronto_Star" title="Toronto Star">Toronto Star</a></i>, the flotilla is to make an attempt to set sail on Monday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com/news/world/article/1018707--ships-ready-to-leave-greece-on-monday?bn=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>Toronto Star</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least 5 people are killed and at least 10 others are wounded in a bomb attack on a bar in <a href="/wiki/Maiduguri" title="Maiduguri">Maiduguri</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. It follows a bomb that killed 25 people this day last week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14009284" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/07/03/uk-nigeria-blast-idUKTRE7621W920110703" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/20117320105949969.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/A._E._Hotchner" title="A. E. Hotchner">A. E. Hotchner</a>, a friend and collaborator of the <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize" title="Nobel Prize">Nobel Prize</a>-winning writer <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Hemingway" title="Ernest Hemingway">Ernest Hemingway</a>, writing in <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> on the 50th anniversary of Hemingway's death, expresses his belief that the <a href="/wiki/J._Edgar_Hoover" title="J. Edgar Hoover">J. Edgar Hoover</a>-led <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">Federal Bureau of Investigation</a>'s surveillance "substantially contributed to his anguish and his suicide", with Hotchner saying he "regretfully misjudged" Hemingway's fear of the FBI. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/books/2011/jul/03/fbi-and-ernest-hemingway" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Observer</i>)</a></li>
<li>American <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Televangelist" title="Televangelist">televangelist</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_H._Schuller" title="Robert H. Schuller">Robert H. Schuller</a> is ousted from the board of the <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Cathedral" title="Crystal Cathedral">Crystal Cathedral</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ocregister.com/news/schuller-306881-church-board.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Orange County Register</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mount_Soputan" title="Mount Soputan">Mount Soputan</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Volcano" title="Volcano">volcano</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/North_Sulawesi" title="North Sulawesi">North Sulawesi</a> province, erupts. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110703-indonesian-volcano-erupts" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
<li>At least 10 people have been killed in a series of bombings and shootings in northeastern <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/english/news/africa/Shootings-Bombings-Kill-10-in-Northern-Nigeria-124948689.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
<li>Storms in the region of <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> in the US kill one person in <a href="/wiki/Montgomery_County,_Maryland" title="Montgomery County, Maryland">Montgomery County</a> and cuts power to 40,000 homes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/blogs/post_now/post/wind-rain-lightning-knock-out-power-to-thousands/2011/07/03/AGmYRwwH_blog.html?tid=sm_twitter_washingtonpost" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>A tourist boat <a href="/wiki/List_of_shipwrecks_in_2011#July" title="List of shipwrecks in 2011">sinks</a> in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_of_Cortez" title="Sea of Cortez">Sea of Cortez</a> off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Baja_California" title="Baja California">Baja California</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> with 23 people missing. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFTRE7630TV20110704" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/americas/07/07/mexico.boat.capsize/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> announces plans to submit a claim to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> to a larger <a href="/wiki/Territorial_waters" title="Territorial waters">portion</a> of the <a href="/wiki/East_China_Sea" title="East China Sea">East China Sea</a> in a move which is likely to be disputed by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> and <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/03/0200000000AEN20110703001700315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Switzerland" title="Government of Switzerland">Swiss Government</a> blocks 27 million <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">Swiss francs</a> worth of assets linked to senior <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> officials. <a class="external text" href="http://www.metronews.ca/calgary/world/article/906771--swiss-block-over-30-million-in-syrian-funds" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Metro News)</i></a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> go to the polls for local elections in the states of <a href="/wiki/State_of_Mexico" title="State of Mexico">Mexico</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coahuila" title="Coahuila">Coahuila</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nayarit" title="Nayarit">Nayarit</a>, <a href="/wiki/Puebla" title="Puebla">Puebla</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hidalgo_(state)" title="Hidalgo (state)">Hidalgo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/03/us-mexico-elections-idUSTRE7621M120110703" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a>
<ul>
<li>Opposition <a href="/wiki/Institutional_Revolutionary_Party" title="Institutional Revolutionary Party">PRI</a> sweeps the three gubernatorial elections in the State of Mexico, Coahuila and Nayarit. <a class="external text" href="http://www.americasquarterly.org/node/2633" rel="nofollow">(Americas Quarterly)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eruviel_%C3%81vila_Villegas" title="Eruviel Ávila Villegas">Eruviel Ávila Villegas</a> of the PRI is elected <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_the_State_of_Mexico" title="Governor of the State of Mexico">Governor of the State of Mexico</a>, defeating <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alejandro_Encinas" title="Alejandro Encinas">Alejandro Encinas</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Party_of_the_Democratic_Revolution" title="Party of the Democratic Revolution">PRD</a> by 40 points. <a class="external text" href="http://www.americasquarterly.org/node/2633" rel="nofollow">(Americas Quarterly)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rub%C3%A9n_Moreira_Valdez" title="Rubén Moreira Valdez">Rubén Moreira Valdez</a> of the PRI is elected <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Coahuila" title="Governor of Coahuila">Governor of</a> <a href="/wiki/Coahuila" title="Coahuila">Coahuila</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roberto_Sandoval_Casta%C3%B1eda" title="Roberto Sandoval Castañeda">Roberto Sandoval Castañeda</a> of the PRI is elected <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Nayarit" title="Governor of Nayarit">Governor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Nayarit" title="Nayarit">Nayarit</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> votes in its <a href="/wiki/Thai_general_election,_2011" title="Thai general election, 2011">26th general election</a> with results showing the <a href="/wiki/Pheu_Thai_Party" title="Pheu Thai Party">Pheu Thai Party</a> loyal to former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Thaksin_Shinawatra" title="Thaksin Shinawatra">Thaksin Shinawatra</a> winning a majority. <a href="/wiki/Yingluck_Shinawatra" title="Yingluck Shinawatra">Yingluck Shinawatra</a>, the opposition party leader, is expected to be the first female <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister of Thailand</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.mcot.net/cfcustom/cache_page/232248.html" rel="nofollow">(Thai News Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14004755" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/politics/245126/poll-result-to-be-known-around-10pm" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-07-03/pro-thaksin-party-to-win-parliamentary-majority-thailand-exit-poll-shows.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/07/03/3259845.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2011/07/2011739048966149.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a>'s leader <a href="/wiki/Hassan_Nasrallah" title="Hassan Nasrallah">Hassan Nasrallah</a> rejects the indictment and arrest warrants served by the <a href="/wiki/Special_Tribunal_for_Lebanon" title="Special Tribunal for Lebanon">Special Tribunal for Lebanon</a> three days earlier against the party's four senior members. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14004096" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201172183540290278.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailystar.com.lb/News/Politics/2011/Jul-03/Lebanons-Arabic-press-digest---July-3-2011.ashx" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Star</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_Communities_and_Local_Government" title="Secretary of State for Communities and Local Government">British Communities Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Eric_Pickles" title="Eric Pickles">Eric Pickles</a> has warned Downing Street that plans to cap <a href="/wiki/Housing_Benefit" title="Housing Benefit">Housing Benefit</a> could result in 20,000 people in the UK being made homeless. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14004551" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An executive and her director boyfriend working with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/London_2012_Olympic_Legacy" title="London 2012 Olympic Legacy">Olympic Park Legacy Company</a> are reportedly suspended following claims that they were paid by <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United F.C.</a> to secure the use of the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> stadium after the games. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201009116023214" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Novak_Djokovic" title="Novak Djokovic">Novak Djokovic</a> of <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/2011_Wimbledon_Championships_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_Singles" title="2011 Wimbledon Championships – Men's Singles">Men's singles</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2011_Wimbledon_Championships" title="2011 Wimbledon Championships">2011 Wimbledon Championships</a> defeating <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Nadal" title="Rafael Nadal">Rafael Nadal</a> of <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> 6-4, 6-1, 1-6, 6-3, and becoming number 1 on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ATP_World_Tour" title="ATP World Tour">ATP World Tour</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.todayonline.com/Sports/EDC110704-0000229/Djokovic-beats-Nadal-to-take-first-Wimbledon-title" rel="nofollow">(Today Online)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/tennis/14006575.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/sport/tennis/2011/07/201173155826984485.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Moroccan_protests" title="2011 Moroccan protests">2011 Moroccan protests</a>: Democracy campaigners dismiss as "unbelievable" government figures showing that 98 per cent of voters backed <a href="/wiki/Moroccan_constitutional_referendum,_2011" title="Moroccan constitutional referendum, 2011">Morocco's constitutional referendum</a> amid allegations of multiple voting, with people marching through <a href="/wiki/Rabat" title="Rabat">Rabat</a>, <a href="/wiki/Casablanca" title="Casablanca">Casablanca</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tangier" title="Tangier">Tangier</a> chanting "The interior minister is a liar". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14011212" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Government troops arrive in <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> in buses to raid houses and arrest civilians following the mass popular anti-government protests there on Friday. Tanks laying siege to the city move north to other villages. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14011188" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_uprising" title="2011 Yemeni uprising">2011 Yemeni uprising</a>: Thousands of people rally against authority in <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a>, marching towards the residence of Vice-President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Abd_al-Rab_Mansur_al-Hadi" title="Abd al-Rab Mansur al-Hadi">Abd al-Rab Mansur al-Hadi</a> since <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a>, who has ruled the country for 33 years, remains in <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> receiving treatment for his wounds. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14017949" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>: <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> chief <a href="/wiki/Anders_Fogh_Rasmussen" title="Anders Fogh Rasmussen">Anders Fogh Rasmussen</a> defends the group's presence in Libya during a meeting of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NATO-Russia_Council" title="NATO-Russia Council">NATO-Russia Council</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sochi" title="Sochi">Sochi</a>, claiming that its mission is in "strict conformity" with <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_1973" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 1973">United Nations Security Council Resolution 1973</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14010305" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>: Clashes break out at a courthouse as 7 police officers, suspected of killing protesters in <a href="/wiki/Suez" title="Suez">Suez</a> during the popular revolution that ousted <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> from power, are released on <a href="/wiki/Bail" title="Bail">bail</a> by a judge in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14023293" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/middle-east/Riots-erupt-in-Egypt-after-court-releases-police/articleshow/9106161.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/middle-east/riots-erupt-after-court-releases-egyptian-police-charged-with-killing-protesters-in-uprising/2011/07/04/gHQAp5ipxH_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tunisian_revolution" title="Tunisian revolution">Tunisian revolution</a>: <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a>, who fled to <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> as his regime was ousted from power in a popular revolution, is convicted <i><a href="/wiki/Trial_in_absentia" title="Trial in absentia">in absentia</a></i> on charges of possessing illegal drugs and weapons and sentenced to 15 years in jail at a court in <a href="/wiki/Tunis" title="Tunis">Tunis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14014757" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/05/world/africa/05briefs-Tunisia.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Saboteurs bomb an <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> <a href="/wiki/Arab_Gas_Pipeline" title="Arab Gas Pipeline">pipeline</a> at <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Nagah&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Nagah (page does not exist)">Nagah</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Sinai_Peninsula" title="Sinai Peninsula">Sinai Peninsula</a> delivering gas to <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartaglobe.com/afp/saboteurs-bomb-egypt-gas-pipeline-to-israel-jordan/450645" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Jakarta Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011740176861868.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Corporal" title="Corporal">corporal</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Korea_Marine_Corps" title="Republic of Korea Marine Corps">Republic of Korea Marine Corps</a> goes on a killing spree while on duty at a guard post on <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ganghwa_Island" title="Ganghwa Island">Ganghwa Island</a>, killing 3 people and injuring 2 others. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/national/2011/07/04/33/0302000000AEN20110704004151315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14009913" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II" title="Freedom Flotilla II">Freedom Flotilla II</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Hellenic_Coast_Guard" title="Hellenic Coast Guard">Greek Coast Guard</a> pursues with <a href="/wiki/Water_cannon" title="Water cannon">water cannons</a> then boards the ship carrying activists from <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> after an unsuccessful attempt to leave <a href="/wiki/Crete" title="Crete">Crete</a> harbour. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/2011741529521330.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australian_Army" title="Australian Army">Australian Army</a> soldier, Sergeant Todd Langley, is killed in fighting in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, bringing Australian casualties <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">in the war</a> to 28. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/news/diggers-in-new-incident-in-afghanistan/story-e6freuy9-1226087755045" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Religious conservatives in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> condemn as "cultural terrorism" the recent support shown for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LGBT_rights" title="LGBT rights">LGBT rights</a> in <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14010106" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> leaves her agent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Christopher_Little" title="Christopher Little">Christopher Little</a> after 15 years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/books/2011/jul/04/harry-potter-jk-rowling-agent" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Corp." title="Sony Corp.">Sony Corp.</a> says that it will fully restore all the <a href="/wiki/PlayStation_Network" title="PlayStation Network">PlayStation Network</a> videogame services in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>, which will complete worldwide restoration of those services, disrupted in April. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/04/us-sony-playstation-idUSTRE7630O020110704" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 2 people are killed and 4 others are declared missing after a <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">landslide</a> in a village in western <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia-pacific/landslide-hits-village-in-nepals-western-mountains-killing-2-people-4-missing/2011/07/04/AGr0hFxH_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Several African countries experience their worst <a href="/wiki/Drought" title="Drought">drought</a> in 60 years, with millions of people affected. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14020452" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> announces that it will transfer the bodies of 84 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> militants to the <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian Authority</a>, apparently as a diplomatic gesture to the Palestinians ahead of <a href="/wiki/Ramadan" title="Ramadan">Ramadan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4091029,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a></li>
<li>A statue of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Reagan" title="Ronald Reagan">Ronald Reagan</a> is unveiled at a ceremony outside the American embassy in <a href="/wiki/Grosvenor_Square" title="Grosvenor Square">Grosvenor Square</a>, <a href="/wiki/Central_London" title="Central London">Central London</a>, opposite a statue of <a href="/wiki/Dwight_D._Eisenhower" title="Dwight D. Eisenhower">Dwight D. Eisenhower</a>. Those invited include <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Thatcher" title="Margaret Thatcher">Margaret Thatcher</a> and <a href="/wiki/Condoleezza_Rice" title="Condoleezza Rice">Condoleezza Rice</a>, while a piece of the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Wall" title="Berlin Wall">Berlin Wall</a> also features. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14009137" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Trial of <a href="/wiki/Ratko_Mladi%C4%87" title="Ratko Mladić">Ratko Mladić</a> in <a href="/wiki/The_Hague" title="The Hague">The Hague</a>:
<ul>
<li>Former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bosnian_Serb" title="Bosnian Serb">Bosnian Serb</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Colonel_General" title="Colonel General">Colonel General</a> <a href="/wiki/Ratko_Mladi%C4%87" title="Ratko Mladić">Ratko Mladić</a> is scheduled to enter a plea on charges of <a href="/wiki/Genocide" title="Genocide">genocide</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Srebrenica_massacre" title="Srebrenica massacre">Srebrenica massacre</a> during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bosnian_war" title="Bosnian war">Bosnian war</a> at a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_crimes" title="War crimes">war crimes</a> court. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110704-mladic-expected-boycott-war-crimes-court?ns_campaign=nl_obs_en&amp;ns_mchannel=email_marketing&amp;ns_source=BOWE_27_20110704&amp;ns_linkname=20110704_mladic_expected_boycott_war_crimes_court&amp;ns_fee=0&amp;f24_member_id=1043505976770" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via France 24)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ratko_Mladi%C4%87" title="Ratko Mladić">Ratko Mladić</a> is removed from his hearing after he is ruled to have spoken out of turn while asking that he have his own lawyer instead of one appointed by the court, then quarrelling with the judge to be allowed speak. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14012057" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hugh_Orde" title="Hugh Orde">Sir Hugh Orde</a>, President of the UK's Association of Chief Police Officers, announces that key policing services are being left "unfunded" as a result of cuts. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14009444" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>At his trial Japanese man Tatsuya Ichihashi admits to killing British teacher <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Lindsay_Hawker" title="Murder of Lindsay Hawker">Lindsay Ann Hawker</a> whose body was found in a bathtub in 2007. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-coventry-warwickshire-14010308" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Lawyers for <a href="/wiki/French_people" title="French people">French</a> novelist <a href="/wiki/Tristane_Banon" title="Tristane Banon">Tristane Banon</a> say that she will file a criminal complaint accusing former <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> head <a href="/wiki/Dominique_Strauss-Kahn" title="Dominique Strauss-Kahn">Dominique Strauss-Kahn</a> of attempted rape. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43631294" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> general election:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abhisit_Vejjajiva" title="Abhisit Vejjajiva">Abhisit Vejjajiva</a>, the outgoing <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister of Thailand</a>, resigns as the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Democrat_Party_(Thailand)" title="Democrat Party (Thailand)">Democrat Party</a> following a heavy defeat in yesterday's <a href="/wiki/Thai_general_election,_2011" title="Thai general election, 2011">general election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/breakingnews/245369/abhisit-quits-as-democrat-leader" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The presumptive Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Yingluck_Shinawatra" title="Yingluck Shinawatra">Yingluck Shinawatra</a> announces a five party coalition led by her <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puea_Thai_Party" title="Puea Thai Party">Puea Thai Party</a> which will have a membership of 60 per cent of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Thailand" title="Parliament of Thailand">Thai parliament</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/04/thailand-election-coalition-idUSL3E7I40NU20110704" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least 88 lawmakers in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/States_and_territories_of_India" title="States and territories of India">Indian state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh" title="Andhra Pradesh">Andhra Pradesh</a> resign <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/En_masse" title="En masse">en masse</a></i> in support of the creation of a new state called <a href="/wiki/Telangana" title="Telangana">Telangana</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14009929" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/india/Telangana-on-the-boil-again-78-MLAs-10MPs-resign/articleshow/9105090.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehindu.com/news/national/article2158170.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hindu</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karim_Wade" title="Karim Wade">Karim Wade</a>, son of Senegalese president <a href="/wiki/Abdoulaye_Wade" title="Abdoulaye Wade">Abdoulaye Wade</a>, issues a strong denial of speculation that his father plans to pass on power to him as if he were a <a href="/wiki/Monarch" title="Monarch">monarch</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14020986" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> is falsely declared dead by the <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> account of the U.S. broadcaster <a href="/wiki/Fox_News" title="Fox News">Fox News</a> in a series of messages stating, "@BarackObama has just passed. The President is dead" and "BREAKING NEWS: @BarackObama assassinated, 2 gunshot wounds have proved too much". Hackers are blamed though the messages remain online several hours later. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/technology-14012294" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-technology/hacking-on-fox-news-twitter-reports-obamas-death-20110704-1gz44.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/TECH/social.media/07/04/fox.hack/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Return of <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> returns to <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> after undergoing surgery for <a href="/wiki/Cancer" title="Cancer">cancer</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14017135" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of people turn out to cheer on Hugo Chávez upon his return to <a href="/wiki/Caracas" title="Caracas">Caracas</a>; he vows to win back his health and describes the support of his people as "the best medicine for whatever illness". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14023775" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_coalition_government_(2010-present)" title="United Kingdom coalition government (2010-present)">UK government</a> will introduce emergency legislation designed to reverse a controversial judgement on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Police_bail" title="Police bail">police bail</a> for debate in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_(United_Kingdom)" title="House of Commons (United Kingdom)">House of Commons</a> on Thursday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14019396" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Experts declare that drugs used during <i><a href="/wiki/In_vitro_fertilisation" title="In vitro fertilisation">in vitro fertilisation</a></i> for older women may increase the risk of <a href="/wiki/Down_syndrome" title="Down syndrome">Down syndrome</a> for their baby. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/health-13992232" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Novak_Djokovic" title="Novak Djokovic">Novak Djokovic</a> returns home to <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> and is welcomed by tens of thousands of people in <a href="/wiki/Belgrade" title="Belgrade">Belgrade</a>, one day after winning <a href="/wiki/2011_Wimbledon_Championships" title="2011 Wimbledon Championships">Wimbledon</a> by defeating <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Nadal" title="Rafael Nadal">Rafael Nadal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14022467" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a>, retired <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> players take legal action against current players and team owners in efforts to preserve current pension entitlements. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/05/sports/football/retired-nfl-players-filing-complaint-complicating-talks.html?_r=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>:
<ul>
<li>Demonstrators against the regime in <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> are met with tanks and troops that surround the city. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/20117575942416758.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> calls for a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> investigation into allegations of <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> abuses in <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14032765" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>At least six people are killed and at least 20 others are arrested as regime forces attack <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14035274" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Government spokesperson <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Ibrahim" title="Moussa Ibrahim">Moussa Ibrahim</a> states that two boatloads of arms intended for use by <a href="/wiki/Anti-Gaddafi_forces" title="Anti-Gaddafi forces">anti-Gaddafi forces</a> have been seized near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Janzour" title="Janzour">Janzour</a> outside <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/2011755223504921.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>At least 11 people killed near <a href="/wiki/Misrata" title="Misrata">Misrata</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14037358" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>: 3 ministers from the regime of <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a>, ousted from power by a popular revolution, are acquitted in court of the misuse of public money. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14029397" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201175111239347361.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair"><i>News of the World</i> phone hacking affair</a>:
<ul>
<li>British tabloid the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> faces fresh allegations linking it to hacking activities, this time after it emerges that the mobile phone of murdered 13-year-old schoolgirl <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Milly_Dowler" title="Milly Dowler">Milly Dowler</a> was interfered with and messages left by relatives were deleted. This gave relatives the false impression that Milly Dowler was still alive when she was not. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14024668" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/video/europe/2011/07/201175155513420452.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Colin_Stagg" title="Colin Stagg">Colin Stagg</a>, the man who was falsely accused of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rachel_Nickell" title="Rachel Nickell">Rachel Nickell</a>'s 1992 murder on <a href="/wiki/Wimbledon_Common" title="Wimbledon Common">Wimbledon Common</a>, is informed that he too had his phone hacked by the <i>News of the World</i>, as many as six years after he was acquitted. <a href="/wiki/Robert_Napper" title="Robert Napper">Robert Napper</a> later admitted responsibility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/05/phone-hacking-colin-stagg-news-of-the-world?intcmp=239" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Peta_Buscombe,_Baroness_Buscombe" title="Peta Buscombe, Baroness Buscombe">Peta Buscombe, Baroness Buscombe</a> states in an interview on the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> that the <i>News of the World</i> tabloid told lies to the <a href="/wiki/Press_Complaints_Commission" title="Press Complaints Commission">Press Complaints Commission</a> (PCC), an alteration in opinion. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/05/phone-hacking-lie-pcc-buscombe" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
