<li><a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a> police are given more powers to remove <a href="/wiki/Burqa" title="Burqa">burqas</a> as anyone refusing to do so faces fines of thousands of dollars or months behind bars. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14025386" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110705-australia-police-get-power-demand-burqa-removal-0" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/05/australia-new-south-wales-police-burqa-removal" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Up to 7,000 police march on <a href="/wiki/Yonge_Street" title="Yonge Street">Yonge Street</a> in <a href="/wiki/Newmarket,_Ontario" title="Newmarket, Ontario">Newmarket, Ontario</a>, including some <a href="/wiki/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police" title="Royal Canadian Mounted Police">Royal Canadian Mounted Police</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Police_of_the_United_States" title="Police of the United States">American</a> officers, accompanied by thousands of spectators for the <a href="/wiki/Funeral_procession" title="Funeral procession">funeral procession</a> for <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canadian</a> <a href="/wiki/York_Regional_Police" title="York Regional Police">YRP</a> police <a href="/wiki/Constable" title="Constable">Constable</a> Garrett Styles, killed when a 15-year-old <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Underage_driver" title="Underage driver">underage driver</a> accelerated during a <a href="/wiki/Traffic_stop" title="Traffic stop">traffic stop</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/toronto/story/2011/06/29/styles-officer-tributes548.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://livenews.thestar.com/Event/Funeral_for_Const_Garrett_Styles" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Toronto Star</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thespec.com/news/article/558183--thousands-gather-for-police-funeral" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hamilton Spectator</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_England_and_Wales" title="Supreme Court of England and Wales">Supreme Court of England and Wales</a> dismisses an attempt by police to suspend a legal ruling limiting the powers of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Police_bail" title="Police bail">police bail</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14032706" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somali</a> man, Ahmed Abdulkadir Warsame, is charged in the US city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_City,_New_York" title="New York City, New York">New York</a> with assisting the terrorist groups <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al Shaabab</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda_in_the_Arabian_Peninsula" title="Al Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula">Al Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/06/world/africa/06detain.html?_r=1&amp;hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Casey Anthony is acquitted of murder in relation to the <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Caylee_Anthony" title="Death of Caylee Anthony">death of her daughter Caylee</a>, but guilty on four counts of misdemeanor providing false information to a law enforcement officer. <a class="external text" href="http://www.freep.com/article/20110705/NEWS07/110705037/Casey-Anthony-acquitted-daughter-s-slaying" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Detroit Free Press</i>)</a><a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/ondeadline/post/2011/07/casey-anthony-jury-reaches-verdict/1" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_House_of_Commons" title="United Kingdom House of Commons">United Kingdom House of Commons</a> inquiry into allegations of corruption associated with bids for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018</a> and <a href="/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2022 FIFA World Cup">2022</a> <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> tournaments accuses <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> of trying to dismiss the allegations and questions FIFA President <a href="/wiki/Sepp_Blatter" title="Sepp Blatter">Sepp Blatter</a>'s commitment to reform. <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/football-news/mps-accuse-fifa-cover-up-4286068?ref=rss&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed" rel="nofollow">(Reuters vis TV New Zealand)</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Yuri_Ogorodonik&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Yuri Ogorodonik (page does not exist)">Yuri Ogorodonik</a> is sacked as the coach of <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Track_and_field" title="Track and field">track and field</a> squad after eight athletes were suspended within a week for failing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doping_test" title="Doping test">doping tests</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/sports/olympics/2011-07-05-651740479_x.htm" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Rebels <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Nafusa_Mountains_Campaign" title="2011 Nafusa Mountains Campaign">launch an offensive</a> in the western <a href="/wiki/Nafusa_Mountains" title="Nafusa Mountains">Nafusa Mountains</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/07/06/libya-mountains-advance-idUKLDE7650HM20110706" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Al-Qwalish&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Al-Qwalish (page does not exist)">al-Qwalish</a> is taken by <a href="/wiki/Anti-Gaddafi_forces" title="Anti-Gaddafi forces">anti-Gaddafi forces</a>, who make gains of 12 kilometres, after a battle lasting 6 hours. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201176153213449975.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: A <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> human rights organisation claims that <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> troops have killed 22 people in the town of <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> since yesterday. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/liveblog/syria-jul-6-2011-1123" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>: A court in <a href="/wiki/Suez" title="Suez">Suez</a> upholds the release of police accused of killing 17 people during the popular revolution that ousted the regime of <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> from power; family members attack police cars and the court building as a result. There is a call for 1 million people to demonstrate in <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a> on Friday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14051679" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201176144549657602.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nigerian_Sharia_conflict" title="Nigerian Sharia conflict">Nigerian Sharia conflict</a>:
<ul>
<li>An explosion and gunfire are heard in the northern <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigerian</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Maiduguri" title="Maiduguri">Maiduguri</a>, amid activity by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist" title="Islamist">Islamist</a> group <a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2011/7/6/worldupdates/2011-07-06T133601Z_01_NOOTR_RTRMDNC_0_-581027-1&amp;sec=Worldupdates" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysia Star</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Iconic Indian filmmaker <a href="/wiki/Mani_Kaul" title="Mani Kaul">Mani Kaul</a> dies in <a href="/wiki/Delhi" title="Delhi">Delhi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14042013" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/entertainment/bollywood/news-interviews/Mani-Kaul-was-by-far-our-most-original-filmmaker/articleshow/9127838.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/news-by-industry/media/entertainment-/media/mani-kaul-pioneer-of-new-age-cinema-dead/articleshow/9129846.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Economic Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraphindia.com/1110706/jsp/frontpage/story_142022490.jsp" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> denounces international credit ratings agencies as "questionable" after <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> is downgraded by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moody%27s" title="Moody's">Moody's</a>, while <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>'s foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Stavros_Lambrinidis" title="Stavros Lambrinidis">Stavros Lambrinidis</a> calls their behaviour "madness". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14043293" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Jiji_Press" title="Jiji Press">Jiji Press</a> reports that the country will conduct stress tests for all <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_reactor" title="Nuclear reactor">nuclear reactors</a> in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/06/us-japan-nuclear-minister-idUSTRE76501Z20110706" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Authorities report that a cargo plane has crashed in eastern <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> with casualties feared. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia-pacific/afghan-officials-cargo-plane-has-crashed-in-eastern-afghanistan-casualties-feared/2011/07/06/gIQA9su9zH_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>7 people are killed during <a href="/wiki/2011_China_floods" title="2011 China floods">heavy floods</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sichuan_Province" title="Sichuan Province">Sichuan Province</a> in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-07/06/c_13968755.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Bell_UH-1Y_Venom" title="Bell UH-1Y Venom">Bell UH-1Y Venom</a> <a href="/wiki/Helicopter" title="Helicopter">helicopter</a> crashes on a training flight at <a href="/wiki/Marine_Corps_Base_Camp_Pendleton" title="Marine Corps Base Camp Pendleton">Marine Corps Base Camp Pendleton</a> near the US city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego,_California" title="San Diego, California">San Diego</a> with one person dead and five people injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.signonsandiego.com/news/2011/jul/06/crews-respond-downed-helicopter-camp-pendleton/" rel="nofollow">(Sign On San Diego)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Ninth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Ninth Circuit">Ninth U.S. Circuit Court of Appeals</a> orders the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_administration" title="Obama administration">Obama administration</a> to cease its enforcement of the ban on <a href="/wiki/Homosexuality" title="Homosexuality">gay</a> men and women in the military ("<a href="/wiki/Don%27t_ask,_don%27t_tell" title="Don't ask, don't tell">Don't ask, don't tell</a>"). <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14056365" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2011984/Dont-ask-dont-tell-stopped-immediately-rule-appeal-judges.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
<li>5 <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarusian</a> journalists are sentenced to administrative arrests ranging from 3 to 12 days for attending unsanctioned rallies in <a href="/wiki/Minsk" title="Minsk">Minsk</a> and other cities. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20110706/165045628.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>7 people are jailed before a trial into suspicions of match-fixing in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkish_League" title="Turkish League">Turkish League</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/sport/football/2011/07/20117611195312789.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> government daily <i><a href="/wiki/Rossiyskaya_Gazeta" title="Rossiyskaya Gazeta">Rossiyskaya Gazeta</a></i> publishes a list of individuals and companies allegedly involved in <a href="/wiki/Money_laundering" title="Money laundering">money laundering</a> and financing of <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/russia/20110706/165046783.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Perjury" title="Perjury">perjury</a> trial of retired star <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">baseball</a> <a href="/wiki/Pitcher" title="Pitcher">pitcher</a> <a href="/wiki/Roger_Clemens" title="Roger Clemens">Roger Clemens</a> commences in the U.S. over allegedly false statements made to a <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> Committee over use of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Performance-enhancing_drugs" title="Performance-enhancing drugs">performance-enhancing drugs</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://old.news.yahoo.com/s/nm/20110706/ts_nm/us_baseball_clemens" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Yahoo)</a></li>
<li>Nine <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_people" title="German people">Germans</a> are convicted <a href="/wiki/Trial_in_absentia" title="Trial in absentia"><i>in absentia</i></a> in <a href="/wiki/Verona" title="Verona">Verona</a> <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> for killing hundreds of civilians during <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14057055" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair"><i>News of the World</i> phone hacking affair</a>:
<ul>
<li>Members of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_House_of_Commons" title="United Kingdom House of Commons">United Kingdom House of Commons</a> discuss a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(United_Kingdom)" title="Labour Party (United Kingdom)">Labour Party</a> proposal to set up a public inquiry into the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">News of the World phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14036673" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/20117682634336422.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> uncovers emails indicating that thousands of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/English_pound" title="English pound">pounds</a> were paid to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police" title="Metropolitan Police">Metropolitan Police</a> officers by News International staff for information. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14043770" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14046070" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vauxhall" title="Vauxhall">Vauxhall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mitsubishi" title="Mitsubishi">Mitsubishi</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Co-op" title="Co-op">Co-op</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lloyds_TSB" title="Lloyds TSB">Lloyds TSB</a> and <a href="/wiki/Virgin_Holidays" title="Virgin Holidays">Virgin Holidays</a> all join <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ford_UK" title="Ford UK">Ford</a> in suspending advertising with the <i>News of the World</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14044052" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" title="The Daily Telegraph">The Daily Telegraph</a></i> reports that phones belonging to the relatives of British soldiers killed in combat were hacked. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14052909" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a>, chairman and chief executive of News Corporation, calls the allegations "deplorable and unacceptable". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14036673" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepalese</a> authorities ban <a href="/wiki/Exile" title="Exile">exiled</a> <a href="/wiki/Tibetan_people" title="Tibetan people">Tibetans</a> from celebrating the <a href="/wiki/Dalai_Lama" title="Dalai Lama">Dalai Lama</a>'s birthday for fears that the gatherings will turn anti-<a href="/wiki/Chinese_people" title="Chinese people">Chinese</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43649818" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>Irish government lawmaker <a href="/wiki/Denis_Naughten" title="Denis Naughten">Denis Naughten</a> votes against his own government over cuts to a hospital, amid protests by hundreds of people outside <a href="/wiki/D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann" title="Dáil Éireann">Dáil Éireann</a>; he now faces expulsion from <a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> with the hospital's emergency department to close on Monday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishexaminer.com/breakingnews/ireland/naughten-votes-against-govt-in-roscommon-hospital-dail-motion-511794.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Examiner</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0706/breaking33.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0706/roscommon.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II" title="Freedom Flotilla II">Freedom Flotilla II</a>:
<ul>
<li>The French ship <i>Dignity Al Karama</i> is reported to have successfully reached <a href="/wiki/International_waters" title="International waters">international waters</a> and is heading for the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza Strip</a>, with hopes expressed that the remaining unsabotaged ships currently being held by Greek authorities will soon join it. <a class="external text" href="http://english.ruvr.ru/2011/07/06/52876705.html" rel="nofollow">(The Voice of Russia)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> announces the deportation of 5 people involved in activism to <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> and <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> amid reports that hundreds more are to fly in from <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> and <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://channel6newsonline.com/2011/07/israel-deports-five-pro-palestinian-activists-ahead-of-arrival-of-gaza-bound-aid-flotilla/" rel="nofollow">(Channel 6 News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Israeli officials are reported to be boycotting a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> official over an unpublished report concerning the part played by Israeli forces in the recent deaths of 7 Palestinian protesters during the annual <a href="/wiki/2011_Nakba_Day" title="2011 Nakba Day">Nakba</a> commemorations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14051618" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>China <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Internet_censorship_in_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Internet censorship in the People's Republic of China">blocks mentions</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a> to <a href="/wiki/Jiang_Zemin" title="Jiang Zemin">Jiang Zemin</a> due to speculation of his death. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14054456" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Turkish Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a> announces the <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_Erdo%C4%9Fan_III" title="Cabinet Erdoğan III">new cabinet</a> of <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>.</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pyeongchang" title="Pyeongchang">Pyeongchang</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> is named as host of the <a href="/wiki/2018_Winter_Olympics" title="2018 Winter Olympics">2018 Winter Olympics</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://sports.espn.go.com/oly/news/story?id=6742361" rel="nofollow">(AP via ESPN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/other_sports/winter_sports/8753631.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/sport/olympics/2011/07/201176154557397364.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Rugby_league" title="Rugby league">rugby league</a>, <a href="/wiki/Queensland_rugby_league_team" title="Queensland rugby league team">Queensland</a> defeat <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales_rugby_league_team" title="New South Wales rugby league team">New South Wales</a> 34–24 in the decider of the <a href="/wiki/2011_State_of_Origin_series" title="2011 State of Origin series">State of Origin series</a>. It is the sixth consecutive series win for Queensland. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxsports.com.au/league/state-of-origin/johnathan-thurston-injured-as-queensland-mark-darren-lockyers-farewell-with-crushing-win-over-nsw/story-fn31yxah-1226089295128" rel="nofollow">(Australian AP via Fox Sports Australia)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 7, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-07</span>)</span> (Thursday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_7&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_7&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_7&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Over a thousand people flee <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> in fear of a government attack by the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/20117711451884870.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> announces plans to send another planeload of humanitarian aid to the Libyan cities of <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20110707/165066099.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> bombs Libyan <a href="/wiki/Petroleum_industry" title="Petroleum industry">oil facilities</a> for the first time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/africa/nato-strikes-at-libyas-oil-in-bid-to-oust-gaddafi-2308962.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_uprising" title="2011 Yemeni uprising">2011 Yemeni uprising</a>: Security forces clash with rebels near the town of <a href="/wiki/Zinjibar" title="Zinjibar">Zinjibar</a> with eight dead including one soldier. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/liveblog/yemen-jul-7-2011-0328" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> ends mission in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> and withdraws 2850 troops. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/story/2011/07/07/kandahar-final-handover.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia-pacific/canada-ends-combat-operations-in-afghanistan-shifts-focus-to-training/2011/07/07/gIQAUIbx1H_story.html?tid=sm_twitter_washingtonpost" rel="nofollow">(Washington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Thirty-four people are killed in attacks on buses and houses in <a href="/wiki/Karachi" title="Karachi">Karachi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, with a total three-day death toll of 63. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dawn.com/2011/07/08/death-toll-rises-to-37-in-karachi-violence.html" rel="nofollow">(Dawn)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> automaker <a href="/wiki/Toyota" title="Toyota">Toyota</a> announces plans to fully restore production from the <a href="/wiki/2011_T%C5%8Dhoku_earthquake_and_tsunami" title="2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami">2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami</a> in October, one month earlier than previously announced. <a class="external text" href="http://search.japantimes.co.jp/cgi-bin/nb20110707a1.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Japan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Civil_Aviation_Safety_Authority" title="Civil Aviation Safety Authority">Civil Aviation Safety Authority</a> applies to extend grounding of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tiger_Airways" title="Tiger Airways">Tiger Airways</a> services in Australia to August 1. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14058084" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NYSE_Euronext" title="NYSE Euronext">NYSE Euronext</a> shareholders approve of the acquisition of that company, parent corporation of the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">New York Stock Exchange</a>, by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deutsche_Boerse_AG" title="Deutsche Boerse AG">Deutsche Boerse AG</a>. The deal still needs to receive the approval of the acquiring firm's shareholders. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/07/us-nyse-deutscheboerse-idUSTRE7660SZ20110707" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair"><i>News of the World</i> phone hacking affair</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> shuts down the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> newspaper the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i>, as a result of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>, with the final edition coming out Sunday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/blog/2011/jul/07/news-of-the-world-phone-hacking-live-coverage#block-98" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14070733" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/International/Article.aspx?id=228369" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police_Service" title="Metropolitan Police Service">Metropolitan Police</a> are contacting up to 4,000 people whose names appear on documents which were seized from the <i>News of the World</i> in 2005. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14067935" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A 7.6 magnitude <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> occurs off the coast of <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Kermadec_Islands" title="Kermadec Islands">Kermadec Islands</a> resulting in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tidal_surge" title="Tidal surge">tidal surge</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/world-news/first-tidal-surge-hits-nz-after-7-6-quake-4289781?ref=rss&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed" rel="nofollow">(TV New Zealand)</a></li>
<li>At least 36 people are trapped underground in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coal_mine" title="Coal mine">coal mine</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shandong_Province" title="Shandong Province">Shandong Province</a> after a fire breaks out. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_688048.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least thirty people are feared dead after a collision between a passenger train and a bus in <a href="/wiki/Uttar_Pradesh" title="Uttar Pradesh">Uttar Pradesh</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/india/30-feared-killed-in-train-bus-collision-in-UP/articleshow/9132484.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Enschede" title="Enschede">Enschede</a> the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> part of the roof of the stadium of football club <a href="/wiki/FC_Twente" title="FC Twente">FC Twente</a> <i><a href="/wiki/De_Grolsch_Veste" title="De Grolsch Veste">De Grolsch Veste</a></i> collapses leaving persons dead and a dozen injured. <a class="external text" href="http://nos.nl/artikel/254219-dak-grolsch-veste-ingestort-een-dode.html" rel="nofollow">(NOS)</a></li>
<li>A heavy storm in the US city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Denver,_Colorado" title="Denver, Colorado">Denver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>, causes localized <a href="/wiki/Flood" title="Flood">flooding</a> and causing 10,000 houses to lose power. <a class="external text" href="http://www.denverpost.com/breakingnews/ci_18434449" rel="nofollow">(<i>Denver Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> starts work on a new facility to rehouse <a href="/wiki/Refugee" title="Refugee">refugees</a> from <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> to avoid both food shortages and political oppression. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/07/0200000000AEN20110707003000315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Janet_Napolitano" title="Janet Napolitano">Janet Napolitano</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Homeland_Security" title="United States Secretary of Homeland Security">United States Secretary of Homeland Security</a>, rolls out the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_administration" title="Obama administration">Obama administration</a>'s strategy to curb <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drug_smuggling" title="Drug smuggling">drug smuggling</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexican</a> border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43678647/ns/us_news-security/?ocid=twitter" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via MSNBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> bans eight types of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Synthetic_cannabis" title="Synthetic cannabis">synthetic cannabis</a> from tomorrow. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/national/eight-types-of-synthetic-cannabis-set-for-national-ban-from-tomorrow/story-e6frfku9-1226089600077" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li>A man holds thirty children and teachers hostage in a kindergarten in the city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muar_town" title="Muar town">Muar</a> in <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Johor" title="Johor">Johor</a> state; the hostages are all later rescued when police storm the classroom. <a class="external text" href="http://www.edmontonsun.com/2011/07/07/malaysia-police-storm-preschool-free-30-children" rel="nofollow">(Edmonton Sun)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Grand_Rapids,_Michigan_shooting_spree" title="2011 Grand Rapids, Michigan shooting spree">Seven people are shot dead</a> in the US city of <a href="/wiki/Grand_Rapids,_Michigan" title="Grand Rapids, Michigan">Grand Rapids</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">Michigan</a>, with Rodrick Dantzler the suspect committing suicide and hostages being released. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gVaXh1rRJ-RuRAbfOXqUVsA8izmw?docId=684462df6d9f45429e9a9d7571db00ae" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.mlive.com/news/grand-rapids/index.ssf/2011/07/live_coverage_police_report_mu.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Grand Rapids Press</i>)</a></li>
<li>Humberto Leal García, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_people" title="Mexican people">Mexican</a> national, is executed in the US state of <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> despite concerns over whether the circumstances of his execution would breach <a href="/wiki/International_law" title="International law">international law</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14041953" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Casey_Anthony_trial" title="Casey Anthony trial">Casey Anthony</a> is sentenced to four years for lying to law enforcement regarding the death of her child Caylee in the U.S. state of <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a> but after credit for time served will be released on July 17. <a class="external text" href="http://www.orlandosentinel.com/news/local/caylee-anthony/os-casey-anthony-sentencing-hearing-20110707,0,1907202.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Orlando Sentinel</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/General_strike" title="General strike">general strike</a> continues in <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> over a proposed change to the electoral system. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/07/06/bangladesh.protests/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> dismisses reports of the death of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="President of the People's Republic of China">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Jiang_Zemin" title="Jiang Zemin">Jiang Zemin</a> as "pure rumour". <a class="external text" href="http://old.news.yahoo.com/s/afp/20110707/wl_asia_afp/chinapoliticspartyjiang" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_Flotilla_II" title="Freedom Flotilla II">Freedom Flotilla II</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Hellenic_Coast_Guard" title="Hellenic Coast Guard">Greek Coast Guard</a> prevents the ship <i>Dignity Al Karama</i> from sailing to the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza Strip</a> after it stops to refuel in <a href="/wiki/Crete" title="Crete">Crete</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/liveblog/Crete" rel="nofollow">(aljazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/DiplomacyAndPolitics/Article.aspx?id=228276" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The southern branch of Sudan's ruling <a href="/wiki/National_Congress_(Sudan)" title="National Congress (Sudan)">National Congress Party</a> announces its split from the northern party ahead of <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a>'s independence <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/indepth/spotlight/southernsudanindependence/2011/07/2011771214156975.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a>.</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The molecular basis for the breakage of <a href="/wiki/DNA" title="DNA">DNA</a>, an important process in the development of <a href="/wiki/Cancer" title="Cancer">cancer</a>, has been identified by <a href="/wiki/Hebrew_University_of_Jerusalem" title="Hebrew University of Jerusalem">Hebrew University of Jerusalem</a> scientists. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/HealthAndSci-Tech/Health/Article.aspx?id=228363" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 8, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-08</span>)</span> (Friday)</span></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/First_Lady_of_the_United_States" title="First Lady of the United States">First Lady</a> <a href="/wiki/Betty_Ford" title="Betty Ford">Betty Ford</a>, wife of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">U.S. President</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gerald_R._Ford" title="Gerald R. Ford">Gerald R. Ford</a>, dies at 93. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/theoval/post/2011/07/betty-ford-died-/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A court in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> announces a delay of an investigation into whether <a href="/wiki/Christine_Lagarde" title="Christine Lagarde">Christine Lagarde</a> abused her authority as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minister_of_the_Economy,_Industry_and_Employment_(France)" title="Minister of the Economy, Industry and Employment (France)">Finance Minister</a> of that country. Lagarde is the new <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund#Managing_Director" title="International Monetary Fund">Director</a> of the <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/09/business/global/french-court-delays-inquiry-into-lagardes-handling-of-2007-case.html?_r=1&amp;ref=business" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2011 Pacific hurricane season">Tropical Storm Calvin</a> forms off the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific</a> coast of <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/" rel="nofollow">(National Hurricane Centre)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hewa_Bora" title="Hewa Bora">Hewa Bora</a> <a href="/wiki/Boeing_727" title="Boeing 727">Boeing 727</a> airliner <a href="/wiki/Hewa_Bora_Airways_Flight_952" title="Hewa Bora Airways Flight 952">crashes</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> killing 74 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/08/us-congo-democratic-crash-idUSTRE7673OU20110708" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> discusses sending a <a href="/wiki/Peacekeeping" title="Peacekeeping">peacekeeping</a> force to the Republic of <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> when it becomes an <a href="/wiki/Independence" title="Independence">independent</a> nation tomorrow. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/middle-east/new-un-force-in-south-sudan-will-have-7000-military-and-900-police/2011/07/08/gIQArEKA3H_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i>News of the World</i>:
<ul>
<li>Former editor of the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Andy_Coulson" title="Andy Coulson">Andy Coulson</a>, is arrested for questioning due to alleged involvement in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/07/andy-coulson-arrest-phone-hacking" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.skynews.com.au/topstories/article.aspx?id=635470&amp;vId=" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>Police also arrest former <i>News of the World</i> reporter <a href="/wiki/Clive_Goodman" title="Clive Goodman">Clive Goodman</a> and raid the <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> offices of the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daily_Star_(United_Kingdom)" title="Daily Star (United Kingdom)">Daily Star</a></i>, Goodman's current employer. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/UK-News/News-Of-The-World-Andy-Coulson-Former-Editor-Arrested-By-Police-Investigating-Phone-Hacking/Article/201107216026496?lpos=UK_News_Right_Promo_Region_2&amp;lid=ARTICLE_16026496_News_Of_The_World%3A_Andy_Coulson%2C_Former_Editor%2C_Arrested_By_Police_Investigating_Phone_Hacking" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> announces that a judge will lead an inquiry into the scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14077405" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Prosecutors ask <a href="/wiki/Strathclyde_Police" title="Strathclyde Police">Strathclyde Police</a> to investigate claims of phone hacking in Scotland by the <i>News of the World</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-scotland-glasgow-west-14081387" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Timeline_of_the_2011_Egyptian_revolution_under_Supreme_Council_of_the_Armed_Forces#July" title="Timeline of the 2011 Egyptian revolution under Supreme Council of the Armed Forces">A large protest</a> with as many as a million people participating is planned for the <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> over perceived lack of progress since the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFTRE7670AJ20110708?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">Space Shuttle Atlantis</a> lifts off for <a href="/wiki/STS-135" title="STS-135">the final mission</a> of the US <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">Space Shuttle</a> program. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/08/us-space-shuttle-idUSTRE7634ZA20110708?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nasa.gov/mission_pages/shuttle/main/index.html" rel="nofollow">(NASA)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Olympics" title="Olympics">Olympics</a>
<ul>
<li>More tickets go on sale for the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> in the "second chance" phase. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14066068" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a> adopts a "no needle" policy preventing athletes from possessing <a href="/wiki/Syringe" title="Syringe">syringes</a> and other equipment that can be used for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Use_of_performance-enhancing_drugs_in_sport" title="Use of performance-enhancing drugs in sport">doping</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/sports/olympics/2011-07-08-3604674859_x.htm" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> issues a report claiming that <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> soldiers have been issued orders to shoot protesters participating in demonstrations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43695260/ns/world_news-mideast_n_africa/" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>Argentine singer-songwriter <a href="/wiki/Facundo_Cabral" title="Facundo Cabral">Facundo Cabral</a> is assassinated in an apparent ambush in <a href="/wiki/Guatemala_City" title="Guatemala City">Guatemala City</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14093876" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Inflation" title="Inflation">Inflation</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> rises to its highest level in three years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/09/china-economy-inflation-idUSL3E7I901B20110709" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-07/09/c_13974827.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a> court orders <a href="/wiki/Fininvest" title="Fininvest">Fininvest</a>, <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a>'s family company, to pay 560 million <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">euros</a> in damages to <a href="/wiki/CIR_Group" title="CIR Group">Compagnie Industriali Riunite</a> in a long running legal dispute. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702303365804576435290994415536.html?mod=googlenews_wsj" rel="nofollow">(Dow Jones via <i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> secedes from <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>, becoming a <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign state</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/news/nationworld/world/la-fg-sudan-independence-20110709,0,732440.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Malaysia" title="Law enforcement in Malaysia">Malaysian police</a> fire <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> and arrest hundreds of people as more than 20,000 people march in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bersih_2.0_rally" title="2011 Bersih 2.0 rally">2011 Bersih 2.0 rally</a> demanding electoral reform in <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessweek.com/news/2011-07-09/malaysian-police-fire-tear-gas-at-kuala-lumpur-protesters.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg via Business Week)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.seattlepi.com/news/article/Malaysia-arrests-236-ahead-of-banned-rally-1458822.php" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Seattle Post-Intelligencer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14076424" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Queensland_Reds" title="Queensland Reds">Queensland Reds</a> of <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> defeats the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canterbury_Region" title="Canterbury Region">Canterbury</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crusaders_(rugby)" title="Crusaders (rugby)">Crusaders</a> of <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> 18-13 to win the <a href="/wiki/2011_Super_Rugby_season" title="2011 Super Rugby season">Super Rugby</a> championship. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theroar.com.au/2011/07/09/reds-win-super-rugby-final/?utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+theroar+%28The+Roar%29" rel="nofollow">(The Roar)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Derek_Jeter" title="Derek Jeter">Derek Jeter</a>, shortstop for the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Yankees" title="New York Yankees">New York Yankees</a>, becomes the 28th member of the <a href="/wiki/3,000_hit_club" title="3,000 hit club">3,000 hit club</a> in <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> history by means of a <a href="/wiki/Home_run" title="Home run">home run</a> off <a href="/wiki/David_Price_(baseball)" title="David Price (baseball)">David Price</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Tampa_Bay_Rays" title="Tampa Bay Rays">Tampa Bay Rays</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/10/sports/baseball/jeter-reaches-3000-hits-with-home-run.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>

<ul>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a>
<ul>
<li>The final edition of the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> is published in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/blog/2011/jul/09/phone-hacking-newsoftheworld#block-25" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Government of the United Kingdom">Government of the United Kingdom</a> looks for ways to stop News International taking over <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BSkyB" title="BSkyB">BSkyB</a> as evidence emerges that senior executives mounted a cover-up of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">News of the World phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/media/press/news-international-knew-hacking-was-widespread-in-2007-2311629.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A strong <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> of 7.1 magnitude occurs off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Honshu" title="Honshu">Honshu</a> in Japan <a href="/wiki/Tsunami_warning_system" title="Tsunami warning system">sparking</a> a <a href="/wiki/Tsunami" title="Tsunami">tsunami</a> warning. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia-pacific/magnitude-71-earthquake-hits-off-northeastern-japan-coast-still-recovering-from-tsunami/2011/07/09/gIQAkAHB6H_story.html?wpisrc=al_national" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>A fire in a retirement home in the village of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Beloye,_Ukraine&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Beloye, Ukraine (page does not exist)">Beloye</a> in the western <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> kills 16 people. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/exsoviet/20110710/165114848.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>A hundred people are injured as the <a href="/wiki/Kalka_Mail" title="Kalka Mail">Kalka Mail</a> is <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kalka_Mail_Accident" title="Kalka Mail Accident">derailed</a> near the town of Fathepur Malwa in the <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Uttar_Pradesh" title="Uttar Pradesh">Uttar Pradesh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ibnlive.in.com/news/kalka-express-derails-in-up-25-injured/166410-3.html" rel="nofollow">(IBN Live)</a></li>
<li>The cruise ship <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria_(ship)" title="Bulgaria (ship)"><i>Bulgaria</i></a> sinks in the <a href="/wiki/Volga_River" title="Volga River">Volga River</a> near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bolgar_(town)" title="Bolgar (town)">Bolgar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. At least 110 of the 196 on board go down with the ship and drown, while 80 were rescued alive. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14099637" rel="nofollow">(BBC Europe)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Twenty prisoners escape from a jail in the town of <a href="/wiki/Tumaco" title="Tumaco">Tumaco</a> in <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Nari%C3%B1o_Department" title="Nariño Department">Nariño Department</a> with three people recaptured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14101416?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<dt>Politics</dt>

<li>Pro-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> activists begin a week of protests on the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/NationalNews/Article.aspx?ID=228627&amp;R=R1&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Sports</dt>

<li>In <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_under-17_football_team" title="Mexico national under-17 football team">Mexico</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/2011_FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="2011 FIFA U-17 World Cup">2011 FIFA U-17 World Cup</a>, defeating <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_under-17_football_team" title="Uruguay national under-17 football team">Uruguay</a> 2–0 at <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Azteca" title="Estadio Azteca">Estadio Azteca</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.fifa.com/u17worldcup/matches/round=255963/match=300151853/index.html" rel="nofollow">(Official FIFA U-17 World Cup Website)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Protesters loyal to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Syria" title="List of heads of state of Syria">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad" title="Bashar al-Assad">Bashar al-Assad</a> in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a> break into the <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_the_United_States" title="List of diplomatic missions of the United States">United States embassy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Damascus" title="Damascus">Damascus</a> and try to break into the <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_France" title="List of diplomatic missions of France">French embassy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/breaking-news/syrian-loyalists-break-into-us-embassy-in-damascus/story-fn3dxity-1226092714961" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> jails a doctor who helped the US <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">Central Intelligence Agency</a> confirm that <a href="/wiki/Osama_bin_Laden" title="Osama bin Laden">Osama bin Laden</a> was living in <a href="/wiki/Abbottabad" title="Abbottabad">Abbottabad</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.mcclatchydc.com/2011/07/11/117445/pakistan-holds-doctor-who-tried.html" rel="nofollow">(McClatchy)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sanofi" title="Sanofi">Sanofi</a> announces positive results of the late-stage trial of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lemtrada" title="Lemtrada">Lemtrada</a>, its new <a href="/wiki/Multiple_sclerosis" title="Multiple sclerosis">multiple sclerosis</a> treatment. <a class="external text" href="http://en.sanofi.com/binaries/20110711_CARE-MSI-RESULTS_en_tcm28-33024.pdf" rel="nofollow">(Press Release)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The death toll from a train crash in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Uttar_Pradesh" title="Uttar Pradesh">Uttar Pradesh</a> state rises to 69. <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/politics/nation/toll-in-up-accident-69-23-yet-to-be-identified/articleshow/9187994.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Economic Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Captured explosives from <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> stored in a <a href="/wiki/Cyprus_Navy" title="Cyprus Navy">Cyprus Navy</a> base <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Munitions_dump" title="Munitions dump">munitions dump</a> catches fire, when a <a href="/wiki/Wildfire" title="Wildfire">wildfire</a> reached the military base, causing massive explosions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/11/cyprus-base-explosions-idUSLDE76A01S20110711" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/cyprus/8630190/Iran-explosives-at-centre-of-Cypriot-intrigue.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/news/nationworld/world/la-fg-cyprus-explosion-20110712,0,4119758.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a>
<ul>
<li>The head of the <a href="/wiki/Cyprus_Navy" title="Cyprus Navy">Cyprus Navy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andreas_Ioannides_(naval_officer)" title="Andreas Ioannides (naval officer)">Andreas Ioannides</a> and the Commander of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evangelos_Florakis_Navy_Base" title="Evangelos Florakis Navy Base">Evangelos Florakis Navy Base</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lambros_Lambrou_(naval_officer)" title="Lambros Lambrou (naval officer)">Lambros Lambrou</a>, are reportedly killed in the blast. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14115103" rel="nofollow">(<i>BBC News</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cypriot_National_Guard" title="Cypriot National Guard">Cypriot National Guard</a> chief of staff <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Petros_Tsalikidis&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Petros Tsalikidis (page does not exist)">Petros Tsalikidis</a> and Cypriot Defense Minister <a href="/wiki/Costas_Papacostas" title="Costas Papacostas">Costas Papacostas</a> both resign from office. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14115103" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Heavy damage is reported to the nearby Vassilikos <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Power_plant" title="Power plant">power plant</a>, which provides 60% of Cyprus' electricity. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14115103" rel="nofollow">(<i>BBC News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Heavy thunderstorms with 75 mph winds, in the US city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chicago,_Illinois" title="Chicago, Illinois">Chicago</a>, <a href="/wiki/Illinois" title="Illinois">Illinois</a>, cut power and disrupt transport. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chicagotribune.com/news/local/breaking/chi-severe-thunderstorm-watch-for-northern-illinois-20110711,0,1006535.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chicago Tribune</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>The <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Korea_Air_Force" title="Republic of Korea Air Force">Republic of Korea Air Force</a> announces that it will conduct regular midair refuelling drills with the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> commencing later this year. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/11/0200000000AEN20110711000500315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> will boycott the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/Conference_on_Disarmament" title="Conference on Disarmament">Conference on Disarmament</a> to protest against <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> being named its chair. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/politics/story/2011/07/11/pol-baird-un-north-korea.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>Ten members of the <a href="/wiki/British_royal_family" title="British royal family">British royal family</a> including the <a href="/wiki/Prince_of_Wales" title="Prince of Wales">Prince of Wales</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Duchess_of_Cornwall" title="Duchess of Cornwall">Duchess of Cornwall</a> are believed to be among the victims of the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/11/phone-hacking-charles-camilla" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>News International publications including the <i>News of the World</i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Times" title="The Sunday Times">The Sunday Times</a></i> are revealed to have improperly accessed private information of former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/11/phone-hacking-news-international-gordon-brown" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>7 people are killed and 3 others are injured by a <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drone_attacks_in_Pakistan" title="Drone attacks in Pakistan">drone attack</a> in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/South_Waziristan" title="South Waziristan">South Waziristan</a> region. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dawn.com/2011/07/12/us-drone-strike-kills-seven-in-s-waziristan.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Dawn</i>)</a></li>
<li>Miners clash with police in <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.net/2011/07/12/miners-clash-with-police-in-chile/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of people flee <a href="/wiki/Maiduguri" title="Maiduguri">Maiduguri</a> in <a href="/wiki/Borno_State" title="Borno State">Borno State</a> after recent deadly attacks there. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14122175" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> special rapporteur on torture and other cruel, inhuman or degrading treatment or punishment <a href="/wiki/Juan_E._M%C3%A9ndez" title="Juan E. Méndez">Juan E. Méndez</a> suggests the United States is violating UN rules by refusing unmonitored access to imprisoned <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">United States Army</a> private <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bradley_Manning" title="Bradley Manning">Bradley Manning</a>, the young serviceman the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_administration" title="Obama administration">Obama administration</a> accuses of passing classified information on secret U.S. activities to the <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> <a href="/wiki/Whistleblower" title="Whistleblower">whistleblower</a> website. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14126223" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www2.ohchr.org/english/issues/torture/rapporteur/" rel="nofollow">(United Nations Human Rights Council)</a></li>
<li>It is reported that the U.S. government's <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">Central Intelligence Agency</a> (CIA) deployed a fake <a href="/wiki/Vaccine" title="Vaccine">vaccine</a> programme in <a href="/wiki/Abbottabad" title="Abbottabad">Abbottabad</a> ahead of <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Osama_bin_Laden" title="Death of Osama bin Laden">its assassination</a> of <a href="/wiki/Osama_bin_Laden" title="Osama bin Laden">Osama bin Laden</a> in an effort to obtain a <a href="/wiki/DNA" title="DNA">DNA</a> sample from <a href="/wiki/Bin_Laden_family" title="Bin Laden family">his family</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14117438" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Timeline_of_the_2011_Egyptian_revolution_under_Supreme_Council_of_the_Armed_Forces#July" title="Timeline of the 2011 Egyptian revolution under Supreme Council of the Armed Forces">A large protest</a> with as many as a million people participating is planned for the <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> over perceived lack of progress since the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://gulfnews.com/news/region/egypt/egyptian-protesters-unimpressed-by-promised-changes-1.837349" rel="nofollow">(<i>Gulf News</i>)</a></li>
<li>An evening rally is held in <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14128073" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Egypt's deputy prime minister <a href="/wiki/Yehia_El-Gamal" title="Yehia El-Gamal">Yehia El-Gamal</a> resigns on the fifth day of the sit-in at <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011712141530691382.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>3 former Egyptian ministers - former interior minister <a href="/wiki/Habib_el-Adly" title="Habib el-Adly">Habib el-Adly</a>, former finance minister <a href="/wiki/Youssef_Boutros_Ghali" title="Youssef Boutros Ghali">Youssef Boutros Ghali</a> (<i><a href="/wiki/Trial_in_absentia" title="Trial in absentia">in absentia</a></i>) and former prime minister <a href="/wiki/Ahmed_Nazif" title="Ahmed Nazif">Ahmed Nazif</a> - from the <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Mubarak</a> regime are given jail sentences. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news24.com/Africa/News/Egypt-number-plate-ministers-jailed-20110712" rel="nofollow">(News 24)</a></li>
<li>Armed gunmen <a href="/wiki/Arab_Gas_Pipeline" title="Arab Gas Pipeline">blow up</a> an <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> <a href="/wiki/Natural_gas" title="Natural gas">natural gas</a> pipeline to <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a> in the town of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/El-Arish" title="El-Arish">El-Arish</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Sinai_Peninsula" title="Sinai Peninsula">Sinai Peninsula</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43719969/ns/world_news-mideast_n_africa/" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> sends a delegation to <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>; they hand over digital material to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tsipi_Livni" title="Tsipi Livni">Tsipi Livni</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/DiplomacyAndPolitics/Article.aspx?id=228717" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_France" title="National Assembly of France">National Assembly of France</a> votes to approve continued participation in <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> operations in <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110712-french-national-assembly-approves-military-operation-libya-nato" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Suspected <a href="/wiki/Abu_Sayyaf" title="Abu Sayyaf">Abu Sayyaf</a> gunmen abduct two <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> citizens and a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Filipino_people" title="Filipino people">Filipino</a> relative from an island village in <a href="/wiki/Zamboanga_City" title="Zamboanga City">Zamboanga City</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/nation/article.aspx?publicationSubCategoryId=200&amp;articleId=705341" rel="nofollow">(Philstar)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> visits <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> to meet with the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Afghanistan" title="President of Afghanistan">President of Afghanistan</a> <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a> and commander of the <a href="/wiki/International_Security_Assistance_Force" title="International Security Assistance Force">International Security Assistance Force</a> <a href="/wiki/David_Petraeus" title="David Petraeus">David Petraeus</a> before visiting French troops stationed in <a href="/wiki/Surobi,_Kabul" title="Surobi, Kabul">Surobi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.trust.org/alertnet/news/frances-sarkozy-visits-afghanistan" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Alertnet)</a></li>
<li>Nicolas Sarkozy announces the withdrawal of 1000 troops from Afghanistan by the end of 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFTRE76B0OR20110712" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> claims responsibility for the death of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ahmad_Wali_Karzai" title="Ahmad Wali Karzai">Ahmad Wali Karzai</a>, the brother of <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a>, and one of the most powerful people in Afghanistan. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dawn.com/2011/07/12/brother-of-hamid-karzai-killed.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Dawn</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14118884" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
