</dl>
<ul>
<li>A British ticket scoops the largest ever lottery prize in Europe, the £161,653,000 <a href="/wiki/EuroMillions" title="EuroMillions">EuroMillions</a> jackpot, by securing all five numbers and both Lucky Stars. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14132264" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>American television producer <a href="/wiki/Sherwood_Schwartz" title="Sherwood Schwartz">Sherwood Schwartz</a>, the creator of <i><a href="/wiki/Gilligan%27s_Island" title="Gilligan's Island">Gilligan's Island</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Brady_Bunch" title="The Brady Bunch">The Brady Bunch</a></i>, dies in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Los_Angeles,_California" title="Los Angeles, California">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/entertainment/tv-radio/brady-bunch-and-gilligans-island-creator-sherwood-schwartz-dies-aged-94/story-e6frf9ho-1226093753828" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>'s debt rating is reduced to "junk" status by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moody%27s" title="Moody's">Moody's</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0712/economy1.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14131959" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Apple_Inc." title="Apple Inc.">Apple</a>'s chief <a href="/wiki/Patent" title="Patent">patent</a> lawyer is leaving the company, Reuters reports, amidst a slew of patent-related conflicts with <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samsung" title="Samsung">Samsung</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nokia" title="Nokia">Nokia</a>, others. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/12/us-apple-hp-patent-idUSTRE76B0SF20110712" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> officials announce their intention to send the country's <a href="/wiki/Whaling" title="Whaling">whaling</a> fleet back to <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a> later in the year; the <a href="/wiki/Sea_Shepherd_Conservation_Society" title="Sea Shepherd Conservation Society">Sea Shepherd Conservation Society</a> (SSCS) is also to return. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-14132320" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evangelos_Florakis_Navy_Base_explosion" title="Evangelos Florakis Navy Base explosion">Evangelos Florakis Navy Base explosion</a>: Thousands of people march on the <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Palace,_Nicosia" title="Presidential Palace, Nicosia">Presidential Palace</a> in <a href="/wiki/Nicosia" title="Nicosia">Nicosia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>; police fire <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> at the demonstrators who tie a banner to the palace gates stating "<a href="/wiki/Demetris_Christofias" title="Demetris Christofias">Christofias</a> [their ruler] is a murderer and must go to jail". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14132130" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Four <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquakes</a> ranging from 5 to 6.2 in magnitude hit the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/07/12/3267412.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(AFP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/rest-of-world/New-Article/articleshow/9193808.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>Sinking of <i><a href="/wiki/Bulgaria_(ship)" title="Bulgaria (ship)">Bulgaria</a></i>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> state television reports that at least 59 bodies have been recovered from the sinking of the <a href="/wiki/Cruise_ship" title="Cruise ship">cruise ship</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Bulgaria_(ship)" title="Bulgaria (ship)">Bulgaria</a></i> on the <a href="/wiki/Volga_River" title="Volga River">Volga River</a>, with more than 200 people on board. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com//2011/WORLD/europe/07/12/russia.boat.sinks/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Russia observes a day of mourning after the disaster. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14118040" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">United States Coast Guard</a> ends aerial searches for seven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_people" title="American people">Americans</a> still missing after a charter fishing boat sank in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_of_Cortez" title="Sea of Cortez">Sea of Cortez</a> off <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> on July 3. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcsandiego.com/news/local/Search-Ends-for-7-Missing-Boaters-125459988.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> refuses entry to <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lankan</a> <a href="/wiki/Asylum_seeker" title="Asylum seeker">asylum seekers</a> detained in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> who claimed to be heading there. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/1569611/NZ-shuts-door-on-asylum-seekers" rel="nofollow">(SBS)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a> appears in <a href="/wiki/High_Court_of_Justice" title="High Court of Justice">London's High Court</a> to begin his appeal against extradition to <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a> as his UK <a href="/wiki/House_arrest" title="House arrest">house arrest</a> enters its 216th day. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2011-07-13/wikileaks-assange-extradition-appeal/2792358" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/12/julian-assange-strategy-fight-extradition" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> approves a new <a href="/wiki/Law_for_Prevention_of_Damage_to_State_of_Israel_through_Boycott" title="Law for Prevention of Damage to State of Israel through Boycott">boycott law</a> which would allow Israeli courts to impose heavy sanctions on Israeli individuals or organizations whom would initiate or promote a boycott against Israeli companies and entities.<a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/11/israel-passes-law-boycotts" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Guatemala" title="Guatemala">Guatemalan</a> police arrest two men in relation to the assassination of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Argentinian_people" title="Argentinian people">Argentine</a> singer <a href="/wiki/Facundo_Cabral" title="Facundo Cabral">Facundo Cabral</a> as fans across the continent mourn his shooting and a tribute concert is held in his memory. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14131705" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14102856" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14108924" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A three judge panel of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Ninth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Ninth Circuit">U.S. 9th Circuit Court of Appeals</a> rules that <a href="/wiki/Jared_Lee_Loughner" title="Jared Lee Loughner">Jared Lee Loughner</a>, the suspect in the <a href="/wiki/2011_Tucson_shooting" title="2011 Tucson shooting">2011 Tucson shooting</a>, has the right to refuse <a href="/wiki/Antipsychotic" title="Antipsychotic">antipsychotic</a> medication while he appeals the treatment prescribed by prison mental health authorities. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/lanow/2011/07/tuscon-shooter-loughner-can-refuse-anti-psychotic-drugs-court-rules.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>U.S. actress <a href="/wiki/Halle_Berry" title="Halle Berry">Halle Berry</a> is granted a restraining order against a convicted <a href="/wiki/Felony" title="Felony">felon</a> arrested on her <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Hills" title="Hollywood Hills">Hollywood Hills</a> property on Monday. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/lanow/2011/07/halle-berry-alleged-stalker-terrorized-me-and-my-family.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a> reports that the U.S. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bureau_of_Alcohol,_Tobacco,_Firearms,_and_Explosives" title="Bureau of Alcohol, Tobacco, Firearms, and Explosives">Bureau of Alcohol, Tobacco, Firearms, and Explosives</a> has lost track of 1,400 guns involved in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Operation_Fast_and_Furious" title="Operation Fast and Furious">Operation Fast and Furious</a> aimed at tracing the flow of weapons to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_drug_cartel" title="Mexican drug cartel">Mexican drug cartels</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/POLITICS/07/12/atf.guns/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/California%27s_36th_congressional_district" title="California's 36th congressional district">California's 36th congressional district</a> go to the polls for a <a href="/wiki/California%27s_36th_congressional_district_special_election,_2011" title="California's 36th congressional district special election, 2011">special election</a> to replace former Rep. <a href="/wiki/Jane_Harman" title="Jane Harman">Jane Harman</a> with <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democrat</a> <a href="/wiki/Janice_Hahn" title="Janice Hahn">Janice Hahn</a> defeating <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> <a href="/wiki/Craig_Huey" title="Craig Huey">Craig Huey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.politico.com/blogs/davidcatanese/0711/CA36_Hahn_leads_Huey_by_8.html" rel="nofollow">(Politico)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/ap/top/all/7650982.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_coalition_government_(2010-present)" title="United Kingdom coalition government (2010-present)">UK Government</a> states its intention to support a <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">Labour Party</a> motion in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_(United_Kingdom)" title="House of Commons (United Kingdom)">House of Commons</a> calling for the withdrawal of <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a>'s bid to take over <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BSkyB" title="BSkyB">BSkyB</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14127282" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The funeral of former <a href="/wiki/First_Lady_of_the_United_States" title="First Lady of the United States">U.S. First Lady</a> <a href="/wiki/Betty_Ford" title="Betty Ford">Betty Ford</a>, wife of <a href="/wiki/Gerald_Ford" title="Gerald Ford">Gerald Ford</a>, occurs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14132170" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>, riots mark the culmination of the <a href="/wiki/Parades_in_Northern_Ireland" title="Parades in Northern Ireland">Belfast marching season</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.net/2011/07/12/riots-mark-culmination-of-belfast-marching-season/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a></li>
<li>U.S. <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> presidential candidate <a href="/wiki/Ron_Paul" title="Ron Paul">Ron Paul</a> announces that he will not stand again for his <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> <a href="/wiki/Texas%27s_14th_congressional_district" title="Texas's 14th congressional district">district</a> in 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304584404576442223826681388.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Wall Street Journal</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.csmonitor.com/USA/Politics/The-Vote/2011/0712/Ron-Paul-says-he-s-all-in-for-the-presidency-won-t-run-again-for-Congress" rel="nofollow">(<i>Christian Science Monitor</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_Arizona" title="Governor of Arizona">Governor</a> of the <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a> calls a <a href="/wiki/Recall_election" title="Recall election">recall</a> election for <a href="/wiki/Arizona_Senate" title="Arizona Senate">state Senate President</a> <a href="/wiki/Russell_Pearce" title="Russell Pearce">Russell Pearce</a> known for his immigration legislation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.azcentral.com/news/election/azelections/articles/2011/07/12/20110712pearce-recall-set-november-8-brewer.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Arizona Republic</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> <a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">astronauts</a> on board <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis"><i>Atlantis</i></a> complete the final <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spacewalk" title="Spacewalk">spacewalk</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">Space Shuttle</a> era, recouping an <a href="/wiki/Ammonia" title="Ammonia">ammonia</a> pump on the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> (ISS). <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-14121532" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_rugby_union_team" title="Wales national rugby union team">Wales rugby union international</a> <a href="/wiki/Richard_Parks" title="Richard Parks">Richard Parks</a> becomes the first person ever to complete the <a href="/wiki/Explorers_Grand_Slam" title="Explorers Grand Slam">Explorers Grand Slam</a> — climbing all of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Summits" title="Seven Summits">Seven Summits</a> and reaching both the <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">North</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Pole" title="South Pole">South Poles</a> — in a single calendar year. <a class="external text" href="http://www.espnscrum.com/scrum/rugby/story/143809.html?e=headline" rel="nofollow">(ESPN Scrum)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/13_July_2011_Mumbai_bombings" title="13 July 2011 Mumbai bombings">13 July 2011 Mumbai bombings</a>:
<ul>
<li>Several explosions shake <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Mumbai</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, killing 20 and injuring over 100 persons. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ndtv.com/article/india/three-blasts-in-mumbai-twenty-dead-113-injured-119030" rel="nofollow">(NDTV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/07/2011713164138658155.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14141454" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/13/mumbai-bomb-blasts-india" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The blasts hit the <a href="/wiki/Zaveri_Bazaar" title="Zaveri Bazaar">Zaveri Bazaar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dadar" title="Dadar">Dadar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Royal_Opera_House_(Mumbai)" title="Royal Opera House (Mumbai)">Opera House</a> areas of the central business district. <a class="external text" href="http://ibnlive.in.com/news/twin-blasts-in-mumbai-15-injured/167291-3.html" rel="nofollow">(IBN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Fire damages a pipeline in the <a href="/wiki/Deir_ez-Zor_Governorate" title="Deir ez-Zor Governorate">Deir ez-Zor Governorate</a>, according to regime officials and state media. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14137680" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.sana.sy/eng/21/2011/07/13/358092.htm" rel="nofollow">(SANA)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>: Several hundred police officers are dismissed in concessions to protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011713151838644663.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>: The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> expresses support for <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> acting as a mediator in the uprising. <a class="external text" href="http://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2011/07/13/statement-press-secretary-presidents-meeting-russian-foreign-minister-la" rel="nofollow">(White House)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anti-Gaddafi_forces" title="Anti-Gaddafi forces">Anti-Gaddafi forces</a> reclaim <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qawalish" title="Qawalish">Qawalish</a> from Gaddafi forces hours after they took it. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201171319645404106.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>In response to rocket fire into Israel, a Palestinian woman is injured in an airstrike on <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14134711" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The house in <a href="/wiki/Tutshill" title="Tutshill">Tutshill</a> near <a href="/wiki/Chepstow" title="Chepstow">Chepstow</a> where <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> grew up is for sale. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/books/2011/jul/13/harry-potter-jk-rowling-home" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moody%27s" title="Moody's">Moody's</a> threatens to cut the debt rating of the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14142621" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Sixteen people are killed when <a href="/wiki/Noar_Linhas_A%C3%A9reas_Flight_4896" title="Noar Linhas Aéreas Flight 4896">Noar Linhas Aéreas Flight 4896</a> crashes in <a href="/wiki/Recife" title="Recife">Recife</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/States_of_Brazil" title="States of Brazil">Brazilian state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pernambuco" title="Pernambuco">Pernambuco</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14137774" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Five people are killed in an explosion at an industrial estate in Boston, <a href="/wiki/Lincolnshire" title="Lincolnshire">Lincolnshire</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channel4.com/news/several-dead-at-serious-incident-in-boston" rel="nofollow">(Channel 4)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-lincolnshire-14146993" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/uk/2011/jul/13/explosion-boston-deaths" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> is admitted to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>, the first new member since 2006. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14151390" rel="nofollow">(<i>BBC News</i>)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christopher_Rose_(judge)" title="Christopher Rose (judge)">Sir Christopher Rose</a> is to investigate reports that surveillance tapes recorded by UK police spy <a href="/wiki/Mark_Kennedy_(police_officer)" title="Mark Kennedy (police officer)">Mark Kennedy</a> were suppressed by prosecutors. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/environment/2011/jul/13/mark-kennedy-secret-tapes-inquiry" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_Courts_of_Malaysia" title="High Courts of Malaysia">High Court</a> of <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> sets dates for the <a href="/wiki/Anwar_Ibrahim_sodomy_trials" title="Anwar Ibrahim sodomy trials">trial</a> of Opposition Leader <a href="/wiki/Anwar_Ibrahim" title="Anwar Ibrahim">Anwar Ibrahim</a> on sodomy charges from August 8 to 26. <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2011/7/13/nation/20110713114808" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Star</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sexual_abuse_scandal_in_Cloyne_diocese" title="Sexual abuse scandal in Cloyne diocese">Sexual abuse scandal in Cloyne diocese</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> prepares for the release of a 400-page report into the sexual abuse of children by priests. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/ireland/2011/0713/1224300654778.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/national-news/report-on-sex-abuse-to-be-worse-than-ferns-2818576.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishexaminer.com/breakingnews/ireland/ojkfcweycwid/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Examiner</i>)</a></li>
<li>Bishop <a href="/wiki/John_Magee_(bishop)" title="John Magee (bishop)">John Magee</a>, a former private secretary of <a href="/wiki/Pope_Paul_VI" title="Pope Paul VI">Pope Paul VI</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pope_John_Paul_I" title="Pope John Paul I">Pope John Paul I</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pope_John_Paul_II" title="Pope John Paul II">Pope John Paul II</a>, is found to have deliberately misled an inquiry into child sexual abuse in the Catholic Church. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0713/cloyne.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.belfasttelegraph.co.uk/news/local-national/republic-of-ireland/exbishop-slammed-over-child-abuse-16022689.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Belfast Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">The Vatican</a> is strongly criticised in the report. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/13/irish-report-child-sex-abuse-vatican" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A Palestinian university student is killed as he attempts to defy arrest after residents throw stones at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli_Defense_Forces" title="Israeli Defense Forces">Israeli soldiers</a> in a community north of <a href="/wiki/Nablus" title="Nablus">Nablus</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14134711" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mexican_Drug_War" title="Mexican Drug War">Mexican Drug War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Federal_Police_(Mexico)" title="Federal Police (Mexico)">Mexico's federal police</a> capture a man who was allegedly the top hitman for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Knights_Templar_(gang)" title="Knights Templar (gang)">Knights Templar</a> <a href="/wiki/Drug_cartel" title="Drug cartel">drug cartel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/americas/mexico-captures-man-who-allegedly-served-as-chief-hitman-of-knights-templar-drug-gang/2011/07/13/gIQARXi6CI_story.html?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Twenty-one people are killed in the town of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ciudad_Juarez" title="Ciudad Juarez">Ciudad Juarez</a> in an ongoing war between the <a href="/wiki/Ju%C3%A1rez_Cartel" title="Juárez Cartel">Juárez Cartel</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Sinaloa_Cartel" title="Sinaloa Cartel">Sinaloa Cartel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/deadly-record-21-slain-northern-mexican-city-215846033.html" rel="nofollow">(Yahoo News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>U.S. senators call for a legal investigation into allegations that <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a>'s <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a> hacked victims of the <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">September 11 attacks</a> as the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News of the World phone hacking scandal">phone hacking scandal</a> continues. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/13/us-senators-phone-hacking-inquiry" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a>, makes a statement to the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="House of Commons of the United Kingdom">House of Commons</a> in relation to the judicial inquiry into the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>, hours before the announcement that <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a>'s <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a> had withdrawn its bid to take full ownership of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BSkyB" title="BSkyB">BSkyB</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14142307" rel="nofollow">(<i>BBC News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/murdochs-news-corp-withdraws-bskyb-bid/2011/07/13/gIQAG7YKCI_story.html?wpisrc=al_national" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Norman_Moore_(politician)" title="Norman Moore (politician)">Norman Moore</a>, a senior politician in the <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a>, calls on the state to consider <a href="/wiki/Secession" title="Secession">secession</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.watoday.com.au/wa-news/senior-wa-minister-endorses-secession-to-address-broken-federal-system-20110713-1hd2n.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Western Australia Today</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>'s Election Commission fails to endorse 142 prospective members of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/House_of_Representatives_of_Thailand" title="House of Representatives of Thailand">House of Representatives</a> including incoming <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Yingluck_Shinawatra" title="Yingluck Shinawatra">Yingluck Shinawatra</a> and outgoing Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Abhisit_Vejjajiva" title="Abhisit Vejjajiva">Abhisit Vejjajiva</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/election/246778/leading-names-in-limbo" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister of Japan</a> <a href="/wiki/Naoto_Kan" title="Naoto Kan">Naoto Kan</a> tells a news conference of his plans to wean the country off nuclear energy after the <a href="/wiki/Fukushima_Daiichi_nuclear_disaster" title="Fukushima Daiichi nuclear disaster">Fukushima Daiichi nuclear disaster</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2011/07/201171395417817629.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> reportedly walks out of negotiations with <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> leaders on tackling debt and deficits as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moody%27s" title="Moody's">Moody's</a> Investor Services warns of a potential loss of a AAA credit rating. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/13/us-usa-debt-idUSTRE7646S620110713" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Two studies show that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Antiretroviral_drugs" title="Antiretroviral drugs">antiretroviral drugs</a> taken to treat <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AIDS" title="AIDS">AIDS</a> can also be used to prevent infection with <a href="/wiki/HIV" title="HIV">HIV</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/national/two-studies-show-that-drugs-used-to-treat-aids-can-be-used-to-prevent-hiv-infection-too/2011/07/12/gIQAN51zBI_story.html?hpid=z4&amp;wpisrc=al_national" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> announces that it would like to co-host the <a href="/wiki/2018_Winter_Olympics" title="2018 Winter Olympics">2018 Winter Olympics</a> which is scheduled to be held in the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> alpine town of <a href="/wiki/Pyeongchang_County" title="Pyeongchang County">PyeongChang</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/13/0200000000AEN20110713001500315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>
</ul>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Several deaths are reported as a security crackdown continues against anti-government protests in <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011714115151803721.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan (2001–present)</a>:
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bombing" title="Suicide bombing">suicide bombing</a> at a mosque in <a href="/wiki/Kandahar" title="Kandahar">Kandahar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, kills four people and injures 11 including the head of the provincial religious council while they were praying for <a href="/wiki/Ahmed_Wali_Karzai" title="Ahmed Wali Karzai">Ahmed Wali Karzai</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/14/kandahar-mosque-bomb-ahmad-karzai" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least six <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> militants are killed following an air strike on a police station in the <a href="/wiki/Abyan_Governorate" title="Abyan Governorate">Abyan Governorate</a> that the militants had overrun. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/liveblog/yemen-jul-14-2011-2115" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kurdish%E2%80%93Turkish_conflict" title="Kurdish–Turkish conflict">Kurdish–Turkish conflict</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers Party">Kurdistan Workers Party</a> fighters ambush the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkish_Army" title="Turkish Army">Turkish Army</a> in <a href="/wiki/Diyarbak%C4%B1r_Province" title="Diyarbakır Province">Diyarbakır Province</a>, resulting in the death of 13 soldiers and five militants. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/07/14/uk-turkey-kurds-idUKTRE76D3WF20110714" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_Civil_War" title="2011 Libyan Civil War">Libyan Civil War</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Margelov" title="Mikhail Margelov">Mikhail Margelov</a>, the President of Russia's special envoy on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">Libyan uprising</a>, claims that <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> has a "suicidal plan" to destroy <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a> if the rebels seem likely to capture it. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/africa/2011/07/14/gaddafis-suicidal-plan-tripoli" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force" title="Israeli Air Force">Israeli Air Force</a> bombs the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza Strip</a> after <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> militants launch a missile attack on <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011714222348698192.html?utm_content=automateplus&amp;utm_campaign=Trial5&amp;utm_source=SocialFlow&amp;utm_term=tweets&amp;utm_medium=MasterAccount" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The poet <a href="/wiki/Liao_Yiwu" title="Liao Yiwu">Liao Yiwu</a> tells the BBC of how he fled China via <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> and other countries and arrived in Germany after his struggles with Chinese authorities who have spent decades suppressing his work and imprisoning him. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14149822" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A rare manuscript of an unfinished <a href="/wiki/Jane_Austen" title="Jane Austen">Jane Austen</a> novel has sold for £993,250 (US$1.6m) in London. The work, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Watsons" title="The Watsons">The Watsons</a></i>, was sold at <a href="/wiki/Sotheby%27s" title="Sotheby's">Sotheby's</a> for three times its estimated price. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/entertainment-arts-14152092" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Singapore" title="Economy of Singapore">Singapore's economy</a> falls by 7.8% due to declines in manufacturing output and the services sector. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/singapore-economy-shrinks-78-more-than-expected-2011-07-13?siteid=rss&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A%20marketwatch%2Fmarketpulse%20(MarketWatch.com%20-%20MarketPulse)" rel="nofollow">(Market Watch)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Borders_Group" title="Borders Group">Borders Group</a>, the once-major bookstore chain now in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chapter_11" title="Chapter 11">chapter 11</a> <a href="/wiki/Bankruptcy_in_the_United_States" title="Bankruptcy in the United States">bankruptcy in the United States</a>, says that its arrangement with <a href="/wiki/Stalking_horse" title="Stalking horse">stalking horse</a> bidder <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Najafi_Companies&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Najafi Companies (page does not exist)">Najafi Companies</a> has collapsed, and it will seek a modification of bid procedures. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/14/us-bordersgroup-idUSTRE76D1SG20110714" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Chairman of Ireland's governing <a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> parliamentary party <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charlie_Flanagan" title="Charlie Flanagan">Charlie Flanagan</a> calls for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Papal_Nuncio" title="Papal Nuncio">Papal Nuncio</a> <a href="/wiki/Giuseppe_Leanza" title="Giuseppe Leanza">Giuseppe Leanza</a> to be expelled from the country after the publication of a report into <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sexual_abuse_scandal_in_Cloyne_diocese" title="Sexual abuse scandal in Cloyne diocese">the sexual abuse of children by priests</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Cloyne" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Cloyne">Roman Catholic Diocese of Cloyne</a>, while <a href="/wiki/T%C3%A1naiste" title="Tánaiste">Tánaiste</a> <a href="/wiki/Eamon_Gilmore" title="Eamon Gilmore">Eamon Gilmore</a> attacks the Vatican's interference in the scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0714/cloyne.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Japan's foreign ministry plans to boycott <a href="/wiki/Korean_Air" title="Korean Air">Korean Air</a> services for one month in response to a demonstration flight of a Korean Air <a href="/wiki/Airbus_A380" title="Airbus A380">Airbus A380</a> over the disputed <a href="/wiki/Liancourt_Rocks" title="Liancourt Rocks">Liancourt Rocks</a>, beginning on Monday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/japan-diplomats-to-boycott-korean-air-2011-07-14" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li>India and Bangladesh commence a joint census to resolve claims over disputed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/India-Bangladesh_border" title="India-Bangladesh border">border</a> areas. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14149042" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_Assembly_of_the_United_Nations" title="General Assembly of the United Nations">General Assembly of the United Nations</a> votes to admit <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> as a member of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/africa/07/14/south.sudan.un/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>U.S. security manufacturer <a href="/wiki/Armor_Holdings" title="Armor Holdings">Armor Holdings</a> pays a $16 million fine to settle bribery charges relating to the payment of a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> official. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14148635" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> reporter <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Urunboy_Usmonov&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Urunboy Usmonov (page does not exist)">Urunboy Usmonov</a> is released on <a href="/wiki/Bail" title="Bail">bail</a> in <a href="/wiki/Tajikistan" title="Tajikistan">Tajikistan</a> but still faces trial. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14154303" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/greenslade/2011/jul/14/press-freedom-tajikistan" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/asia/tajikistan/8638080/Tajikistan-frees-jailed-BBC-reporter.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/07/14/uk-tajikistan-reporter-idUKTRE76D3C420110714?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News of the World phone hacking scandal">News of the World phone hacking scandal</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a> chairman <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a>, his son <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Murdoch_(media_executive)" title="James Murdoch (media executive)">James</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> chief executive <a href="/wiki/Rebekah_Brooks" title="Rebekah Brooks">Rebekah Brooks</a> all agree to appear before British MPs next week to answer questions on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">News of the World phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14148658" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Neil_Wallis" title="Neil Wallis">Neil Wallis</a>, former deputy editor of the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> under <a href="/wiki/Andy_Coulson" title="Andy Coulson">Andy Coulson</a>, is arrested and questioned by police investigating the scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/14/news-of-the-world-neil-wallis" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FBI" title="FBI">FBI</a> is investigating reports that <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a> sought to hack the phones of victims of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/September_11_terrorist_attacks" title="September 11 terrorist attacks">September 11 terrorist attacks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14162545" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>In his first major interview on the phone-hacking crisis, Rupert Murdoch says his company has handled it "extremely well" and that News Corp will recover. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14162268" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_District_of_Columbia" title="United States District Court for the District of Columbia">U.S. district court</a> judge <a href="/wiki/Reggie_Walton" title="Reggie Walton">Reggie Walton</a> declares a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mistrial_(law)" title="Mistrial (law)">mistrial</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Perjury" title="Perjury">perjury</a> trial of former baseball star <a href="/wiki/Roger_Clemens" title="Roger Clemens">Roger Clemens</a> after prosecutors present evidence that Walton had previously ruled inadmissible. Walton will hold a hearing on September 2 to determine whether to hold a new trial. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/mlb/story/_/id/6768625/roger-clemens-trial-judge-declares-mistrial" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
<li>At least thirty-two <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chilean</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Chile" title="Law enforcement in Chile">police</a> and 54 demonstrators are arrested in a demonstration demanding more funds for higher education. <a class="external text" href="http://www.antaranews.com/en/news/1310688968/32-police-wounded-54-arrested-in-chile-student-demo" rel="nofollow">(Antara News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_Senate" title="Italian Senate">Italian Senate</a> approves an austerity budget aimed at preventing the need for a financial bailout for Italy. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14149164" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Welsh_Conservative_Party" title="Welsh Conservative Party">Welsh Conservative Party</a> chooses <a href="/wiki/Andrew_R._T._Davies" title="Andrew R. T. Davies">Andrew R. T. Davies</a> as their leader in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Welsh_Assembly" title="Welsh Assembly">Welsh Assembly</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-wales-politics-14143317" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The President of the United States, <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, gives <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">Congressional</a> leader 24 to 36 hours to reach an agreement on debt reduction as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Credit_agency" title="Credit agency">credit agency</a> <a href="/wiki/Standard_%26_Poor%27s" title="Standard &amp; Poor's">Standard &amp; Poor's</a> places the US on a downgrade watch. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/15/us-sp-us-idUSTRE76E01S20110715?feedType=RSS&amp;virtualBrandChannel=10102" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/blogs/2chambers/post/obama-gives-leaders-24-to-36-hours-to-come-to-debt-agreement/2011/07/14/gIQALtXtEI_blog.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/blogs/thetwo-way/2011/07/14/137852207/reports-s-p-says-u-s-rating-could-be-downgraded-if-it-misses-any-payments" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/sp-warns-on-us-debt-50-chance-of-downgrade-2011-07-14" rel="nofollow">(Marketwatch)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic</a> <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Minnesota" title="Governor of Minnesota">Governor of Minnesota</a> <a href="/wiki/Mark_Dayton" title="Mark Dayton">Mark Dayton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> <a href="/wiki/Minnesota_Legislature" title="Minnesota Legislature">legislative</a> leaders reach a budget deal which will end a shutdown of the <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">US state government</a> within days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/15/us-minnesota-shutdown-idUSTRE76D53620110715?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a> completes its first orbit of the Sun since its discovery in 1846. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2011-07-14/neptune-completes-one-year/2794778?WT.mc_id=newsmail" rel="nofollow">(ABC Online)</a></li>
<li>A lost <a href="/wiki/Ansonia_latidisca" title="Ansonia latidisca">rainbow toad</a> thought to have become extinct after its last sighting in 1924 is rediscovered in <a href="/wiki/Borneo" title="Borneo">Borneo</a> by scientists from <a href="/wiki/Universiti_Malaysia_Sarawak" title="Universiti Malaysia Sarawak">Universiti Malaysia Sarawak</a> (UNIMAS) and photographed for the first time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/nature/14151541" rel="nofollow">(BBC Nature)</a></li>
</ul>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> troops report three deaths in <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Maidanpora&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Maidanpora (page does not exist)">Maidanpora</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kupwara" title="Kupwara">Kupwara</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14164787" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>International campaigners against the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drone_attacks_in_Pakistan" title="Drone attacks in Pakistan">drone attacks</a>, carried out by the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, launch their attempt to have former CIA legal chief <a href="/wiki/John_A._Rizzo" title="John A. Rizzo">John A. Rizzo</a> arrested and charged with the murders of hundreds of people after his admission in <i><a href="/wiki/Newsweek" title="Newsweek">Newsweek</a></i> that he approved attacks each month since 2004. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/15/cia-usa" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Soldiers, air force bombers and helicopter gunships begin a major offensive in south-eastern Turkey as the country's prime minister <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a> vows to seek vengeance on Kurdish rebels. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14170418" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: At least 14 people are killed in the latests attacks by regime forces on demonstrations in cities nationwide. More than 10,000 people are held in prisons by the regime. The demonstrations are reported to be among the largest yet in the ongoing effort to topple the government. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14168199" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/13_July_2011_Mumbai_bombings" title="13 July 2011 Mumbai bombings">13 July 2011 Mumbai bombings</a>: Indian investigators check <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CCTV" title="CCTV">CCTV</a> footage in their search for clues into Wednesday's triple bombing in <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Mumbai</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14165151" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Europe's biggest lottery jackpot, £161 million (US$260 million), is scooped by a couple from <a href="/wiki/Largs" title="Largs">Largs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ayrshire" title="Ayrshire">Ayrshire</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14161661" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows Part 2 is released in theaters as the final installment of the famous Harry Potter franchise.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>8 European banks fail <a href="/wiki/Stress_testing" title="Stress testing">stress tests</a> that could leave them open to another financial crisis, while another 16 are in a "danger zone". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14169940" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0715/banks.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> journalists strike against <a href="/wiki/Layoff" title="Layoff">layoffs</a> being forced on them by the corporation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/entertainment-arts-14152795" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_Shell" title="Royal Dutch Shell">Royal Dutch Shell</a> reveals plans to construct a 600,000-tonne <a href="/wiki/Floating_liquefied_natural_gas" title="Floating liquefied natural gas">floating liquefied natural gas</a> (FLNG) platform, a world's first for off the coast of Australia. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-13709293" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/BHP_Billiton" title="BHP Billiton">BHP Billiton</a> buys U.S. based petroleum company <a href="/wiki/Petrohawk" title="Petrohawk">Petrohawk</a> for <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">$</a>12 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/business/bhp-swoops-on-petrohawk-for-us12b-20110715-1hgph.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rebekah_Brooks" title="Rebekah Brooks">Rebekah Brooks</a> resigns as chief executive of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> as a result of the <a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/congress/murdochs-refuse-then-agree-to-be-questioned-by-uk-parliament-fbi-opens-911-hacking-review/2011/07/15/gIQAwxNTFI_story.html?hpid=z1&amp;wpisrc=al_national" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110715-uk-media-murdoch-news-international-rebekah-brooks-resigns" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France24)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/16/world/europe/16hacking.html?" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/15/rebekah-brooks-resigns-phone-hacking-scandal" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The family of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jean_Charles_de_Menezes" title="Jean Charles de Menezes">Jean Charles de Menezes</a>, killed by police bullets in London in 2005, write a letter to prime minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> calling for police actions surrounding his death to be investigated in the wake of the <a href="/wiki/News_Corp" title="News Corp">News Corp</a> <a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">phone hacking scandal</a> that has so far claimed the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14162647" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>UK prime minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> paid for his "friend", the former <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> editor <a href="/wiki/Andy_Coulson" title="Andy Coulson">Andy Coulson</a>, to stay with him at his country residence of <a href="/wiki/Chequers" title="Chequers">Chequers</a>, two months after Coulson resigned as Cameron's media chief. Coulson has since been arrested for his part in the phone hacking scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/15/david-cameron-andy-coulson-chequers-hosted" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a> meets the family of <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Milly_Dowler" title="Murder of Milly Dowler">Milly Dowler</a> and gives them what their solicitor calls a full and sincere apology. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14169731" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14169737" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Rupert Murdoch attacks former UK prime minister <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i> in his first interview on the scandal and accuses British MPs of telling lies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/15/rupert-murdoch-gordon-brown-interview" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>There are concerns over a donation believed to be at least £100,000 given by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Murdoch_(media_executive)" title="James Murdoch (media executive)">James Murdoch</a> towards <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XVI%27s_visit_to_the_United_Kingdom" title="Pope Benedict XVI's visit to the United Kingdom">Pope Benedict XVI's visit to the United Kingdom</a> last year; Murdoch was then introduced to Benedict. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/jul/15/catholicism-pope-benedict-xvi" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> reveals the advertisement Rupert Murdoch intends to run in British newspapers at the weekend apologising for "serious wrongdoing". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/interactive/2011/jul/15/rupert-murdoch-phone-hacking-apology-ad" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Les_Hinton" title="Les Hinton">Les Hinton</a>, who ran <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> from 1997 to 2005 during which the hacking took place, resigns as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CEO" title="CEO">CEO</a> of News Corp's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_%26_Co" title="Dow Jones &amp; Co">Dow Jones</a> entity. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/16/world/europe/16hacking.html?hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Technology/wireStory?id=14083348" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14170879" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The actor <a href="/wiki/Jude_Law" title="Jude Law">Jude Law</a> has filed a lawsuit against <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sun_(United_Kingdom)" title="The Sun (United Kingdom)">The Sun</a></i> over allegations of phone hacking. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/crime/the-sun-enters-frame-as-jude-law-makes-new-hacking-claims-2314496.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Horn_of_Africa_drought" title="2011 Horn of Africa drought">2011 Horn of Africa drought</a>:
<ul>
<li>Drought fleers located at camps in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a> are struck down by days of killer rain. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14165509" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> (WHO) reports that 5 million people are at risk of developing <a href="/wiki/Cholera" title="Cholera">cholera</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>, with the breakout of acute watery <a href="/wiki/Diarrhea" title="Diarrhea">diarrhea</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/07/15/us-africa-drought-idUKTRE76E2XH20110715?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=healthNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The Kenyan government announces the opening of a fourth refugee camp at <a href="/wiki/Dadaab" title="Dadaab">Dadaab</a> in the <a href="/wiki/North_Eastern_Province_(Kenya)" title="North Eastern Province (Kenya)">North Eastern Province</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/global-development/2011/jul/15/dadaab-drought-refugee-camp-kenya" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">Landslides</a> in two remote <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepalese</a> villages kill six people and injure another ten. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/feedarticle/9745122" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mount_Lokon" title="Mount Lokon">Mount Lokon</a> on <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sulawesi" title="Sulawesi">Sulawesi</a> island erupts prompting thousands of people to flee. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2011-07-15/indonesia-volcano-erupts/2796222?WT.mc_id=newsmail" rel="nofollow">(AFP via ABC News Online)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/07/15/indonesia.volcano/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Four <a href="/wiki/Pilgrim" title="Pilgrim">pilgrims</a> die when a boulder falls on them at a <a href="/wiki/Haitian_Vodou" title="Haitian Vodou">voodoo</a> festival in <a href="/wiki/Saut_d%27Eau" title="Saut d'Eau">Saut d'Eau</a>, <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ajc.com/news/nation-world/4-voodoo-pilgrims-die-1019515.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Atlanta Journal Constitution</i>)</a></li>
<li>A magnitude 6 <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> occurs off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> near <a href="/wiki/Valpara%C3%ADso" title="Valparaíso">Valparaíso</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/americas/07/15/chile.earthquake/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>A portion of the <a href="/wiki/Zendstation_Smilde" title="Zendstation Smilde">Zendstation Smilde</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hoogersmilde" title="Hoogersmilde">Hoogersmilde</a>, <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> collapses in a fire. <a class="external text" href="http://articles.cnn.com/2011-07-16/world/netherlands.tower.fire_1_television-tower-fire-crews-netherlands?_s=PM:WORLD" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Taoiseach" title="Taoiseach">Taoiseach</a> <a href="/wiki/Enda_Kenny" title="Enda Kenny">Enda Kenny</a> attacks the Vatican's approach to the child abuse scandals in the country as "absolutely disgraceful", while the <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Party_(Ireland)" title="Socialist Party (Ireland)">Socialist Party</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Joe_Higgins" title="Joe Higgins">Joe Higgins</a> tells <a href="/wiki/D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann" title="Dáil Éireann">Dáil Éireann</a> that people were "throwing their hands in the air" after the report into the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sexual_abuse_scandal_in_Cloyne_diocese" title="Sexual abuse scandal in Cloyne diocese">sexual abuse scandal in Cloyne diocese</a> was published this week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/14/vatican-child-abuse-ireland" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">United States Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> meets with <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> leaders to try to find a solution to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">Libya crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14164517" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Libyan_Republic#Recognition" title="Foreign relations of the Libyan Republic">recognizes</a> the Libyan <a href="/wiki/National_Transitional_Council" title="National Transitional Council">National Transitional Council</a> as the legitimate governing authority in Libya. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/16/world/africa/16libya.html?_r=1&amp;hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<dt>Intragalactic relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>U.S. president <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> makes a phone call to the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> (ISS) and jokes with <a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">astronauts</a> about pizza. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-14170124" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Charlie Gilmour, the son of <a href="/wiki/Pink_Floyd" title="Pink Floyd">Pink Floyd</a> guitarist <a href="/wiki/David_Gilmour" title="David Gilmour">David Gilmour</a>, is jailed for 16 months for violent disorder during the <a href="/wiki/2010_United_Kingdom_student_protests" title="2010 United Kingdom student protests">student protests against tuition fees</a> in London late last year. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-14150800" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/law-and-order/8639930/Pink-Floyd-guitarists-son-Charlie-Gilmour-jailed-for-drug-fuelled-rampage.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Italian MPs in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_Chamber_of_Deputies" title="Italian Chamber of Deputies">lower house</a> approve tough budget cuts with 314 votes in favour and 280 against. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14168914" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<ul>

<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/%C5%8Ci_Nuclear_Power_Plant" title="Ōi Nuclear Power Plant">Ohi Nuclear Power Plant</a> in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> is being shut down due a technical fault, <a href="/wiki/Fukushima_Daiichi_nuclear_disaster" title="Fukushima Daiichi nuclear disaster">Fukushima Daiichi nuclear disaster</a>. Only 18 out of 54 nuclear plants in Japan are currently producing electricity. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14171962" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/07/16/japan.nuclear.reactor/index.html?hpt=wo_c2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Nearly 5,000 people are evacuated after <a href="/wiki/Mount_Lokon" title="Mount Lokon">Mount Lokon</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> erupts. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartaglobe.com/home/4600-evacuated-in-north-sulawesi-volcano-eruption/453258" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jakarta Globe</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/news-by-industry/et-cetera/4800-evacuated-in-indonesia-volcano-eruption/articleshow/9247150.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Economic Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>Seven people are killed and two injured after a customs boat sinks near the coast of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Sumatra_Province" title="North Sumatra Province">North Sumatra Province</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/24521/7-killed-in-indonesia-boat-accident" rel="nofollow">(AFP via NewsInfo)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Quadriga_(award)" title="Quadriga (award)">Quadriga</a> is not to be awarded this year due to the backlash sustained by organisers for giving it to <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Russia" title="Prime Minister of Russia">Prime Minister of Russia</a> and former <a href="/wiki/KGB" title="KGB">KGB</a> spy chief <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a>. Among the upheaval Danish artist <a href="/wiki/Olafur_Eliasson" title="Olafur Eliasson">Olafur Eliasson</a> gave back his award and <a href="/wiki/V%C3%A1clav_Havel" title="Václav Havel">Václav Havel</a> was reported to be considering doing that too. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14173814" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,15240096,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/17/world/europe/17germany.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/16/us-germany-putin-award-idUSTRE76F1CO20110716" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/german-foundation-cancels-ceremony-to-honor-russias-putin-after-criticism-of-nomination/2011/07/16/gIQAB0nuHI_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> is set to meet with the <a href="/wiki/Dalai_Lama" title="Dalai Lama">Dalai Lama</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_DC" title="Washington DC">Washington DC</a> despite a warning from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-14171736" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://old.news.yahoo.com/s/afp/20110716/pl_afp/ustibetchinareligionpolitics" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> President <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> arrives back in <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> for <a href="/wiki/Chemotherapy" title="Chemotherapy">chemotherapy</a> treatment. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2011/07/16/Chavez-back-in-Cuba-for-chemotherapy/UPI-71351310830179/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_Foreign_and_Commonwealth_Affairs" title="Secretary of State for Foreign and Commonwealth Affairs">British Foreign Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/William_Hague" title="William Hague">William Hague</a> defends Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> following revelations he has met senior <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> executives on 26 occasions since becoming Prime Minister, and entertained <a href="/wiki/Andy_Coulson" title="Andy Coulson">Andy Coulson</a> at <a href="/wiki/Chequers" title="Chequers">Chequers</a> following his resignation as Director of Communications. Hague says he is "not embarrassed" by the extent of Cameron's dealings with News International. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14173150" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Several British newspapers run full page adverts with a signed apology from <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a> for the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a>'</i>s "serious wrongdoing" <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14170756" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daily_Telegraph" title="Daily Telegraph">The Telegraph</a></i> reports that <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police_Service" title="Metropolitan Police Service">Metropolitan Police</a> Chief Sir <a href="/wiki/Paul_Stephenson_(police_officer)" title="Paul Stephenson (police officer)">Paul Stephenson</a> stayed at a luxury health spa courtesy of a former <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> deputy editor. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/phone-hacking/8642818/Phone-hacking-Sir-Paul-Stephenson-faces-questions-of-health-spa-stay.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The funeral of <a href="/wiki/Otto_von_Habsburg" title="Otto von Habsburg">Otto von Habsburg</a>, final <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heir" title="Heir">heir</a> to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Austro-Hungarian_Empire" title="Austro-Hungarian Empire">Austro-Hungarian Empire</a>, occurs in <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a>, attended by monarchs and members of the political elite; his corpse is to be buried in the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Crypt" title="Imperial Crypt">Imperial Crypt</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14172091" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>: Ousted Egyptian leader <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> suffers stroke, falls into coma. <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/news/middle-east/ousted-egyptian-leader-mubarak-suffers-stroke-falls-into-coma-1.373744" rel="nofollow">(<i>Haaretz</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2011-07-18/mubarak-health/2798152" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a></li>

<ul>
<li>Syrian forces mass in the east of the country near the <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> border where dozens of soldiers have defected. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/18/world/middleeast/18syria.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Troops storm a town near the border with <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>, rounding up more than 500 people. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011717134540580142.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>: <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> planes destroy a military storage facility and other targets on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/2011717142844567305.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_uprising" title="2011 Bahraini uprising">2011 Bahraini uprising</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shia" title="Shia">Shia</a> al-Wafiq opposition group quits national talks aimed at ending the political crisis in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14178740" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<dt>Arts and entertainment</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Warner_Bros." title="Warner Bros.">Warner Bros.</a> has reported that <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_%E2%80%93_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 2</a></i>, the final instalment of the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)"><i>Harry Potter</i> film series</a> has broken box office records, taking $92.1m (£57m) in North America on Friday, its opening day. <a class="external text" href="http://boxofficemojo.com/news/?id=3210&amp;p=.htm" rel="nofollow">(Box Office Mojo)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> delivers aid to parts of <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> controlled by <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabab</a> militants for the first time since they ended the ban on food supplies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14175443" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A passenger bus collides with a truck near <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mashkovo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mashkovo (page does not exist)">Mashkovo</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tambov_Oblast" title="Tambov Oblast">Tambov Oblast</a> with at least 5 people dead and 17 injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2011/07/17/5-dead-17-hurt-in-Russia-bus-truck-crash/UPI-28991310877788/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mount_Lokon" title="Mount Lokon">Mount Lokon</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Volcano" title="Volcano">volcano</a> on <a href="/wiki/Sulawesi" title="Sulawesi">Sulawesi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> erupts again sending ash 3,500 metres in the air. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5huvR-GzGE23KazCtRS0g9w1yyHLw?docId=CNG.2b4f6fd7caf05132cb9f1b6338bac556.6e1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">Tropical Storm Bret</a> forms off the coast of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">Bahamas</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/nhc_storms.shtml" rel="nofollow">(National Hurricane Centre)</a></li>
<li>At least two people are killed and 35 injured due to a bus crash on <a href="/wiki/Interstate_390" title="Interstate 390">Interstate 390</a> near the US town of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bath_(town),_New_York" title="Bath (town), New York">Bath</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.democratandchronicle.com/article/20110717/NEWS01/110717009/Two-people-dead-following-tour-bus-crash-390-near-Bath?odyssey=tab%7Ctopnews%7Ctext%7CHome" rel="nofollow">(<i>Democrat and Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
<li>At the conclusion of <a href="/wiki/Ottawa_Bluesfest" title="Ottawa Bluesfest">Ottawa Bluesfest</a>, strong winds from a sudden <a href="/wiki/Thunderstorm" title="Thunderstorm">thunderstorm</a> cause one of the main stages to collapse at around 7:30 pm EDT, injuring three people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com/news/canada/article/1026329--stage-collapses-at-ottawa-bluesfest-after-sudden-storm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Toronto Star</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
