<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Home_Secretary" title="Home Secretary">British Home Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Theresa_May" title="Theresa May">Theresa May</a> will address MPs on Monday following revelations that the <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police_Service" title="Metropolitan Police Service">Metropolitan Police</a> hired former <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> deputy editor <a href="/wiki/Neil_Wallis" title="Neil Wallis">Neil Wallis</a> to give <a href="/wiki/Public_relations" title="Public relations">PR</a> advice. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14176339" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a>'s <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a> takes out a second series of adverts in Britain's Sunday newspapers apologising for wrongdoing at the <i>News of the World</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnbc.com/id/43784302" rel="nofollow">(CNBC)</a></li>
<li>Former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> Chief Executive <a href="/wiki/Rebekah_Brooks" title="Rebekah Brooks">Rebekah Brooks</a> is arrested by police investigating phone hacking and corruption at the organisation. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/UK-News/Rebekah-Brooks-Has-Been-Arrested-By-Police-Officers-Investigating-Phone-Hacking/Article/201107316032015?lpos=UK_News_Top_Stories_Header_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_16032015_Rebekah_Brooks_Has_Been_Arrested_By_Police_Officers_Investigating_Phone_Hacking" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sky News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2015677/Rebekah-Brooks-arrested-phone-hacking-scandal-News-International.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Mail Online</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14178051" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Metropolitan Police Commissioner Sir <a href="/wiki/Paul_Stephenson_(police_officer)" title="Paul Stephenson (police officer)">Paul Stephenson</a> resigns over the phone hacking affair. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14180043" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguayan</a> dictator <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mar%C3%ADa_Bordaberry" title="Juan María Bordaberry">Juan María Bordaberry</a> dies under <a href="/wiki/House_arrest" title="House arrest">house arrest</a> for <a href="/wiki/Murder" title="Murder">murders</a> committed during his time in power. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hlj3raeO_vY5PSqEupSvaHD4KJkw?docId=CNG.8fb7d35155ba255c40a5a227fc0d8daf.1251" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe" title="São Tomé and Príncipe">São Tomé and Príncipe</a> go to the polls for a <a href="/wiki/Elections_in_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe" title="Elections in São Tomé and Príncipe">presidential election</a> with a runoff election necessary with the leading candidate <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Pinto_da_Costa" title="Manuel Pinto da Costa">Pinto da Costa</a> failing to achieve an absolute majority. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110718-sao-tome-presidential-vote-set-run-off" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> wins the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FIFA_Women%27s_World_Cup_2011" title="FIFA Women's World Cup 2011">FIFA Women's World Cup 2011</a> by beating the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USA" title="USA">USA</a> 3-2 in the Penalty Shootout. <a class="external text" href="http://nbcsports.msnbc.com/id/43785995/ns/sports-soccer/" rel="nofollow">(NBC Sports)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.wsj.com/dailyfix/2011/07/17/womens-world-cup-final-live-blog-united-states-vs-japan/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> golfer <a href="/wiki/Darren_Clarke" title="Darren Clarke">Darren Clarke</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/2011_Open_Championship" title="2011 Open Championship">2011 Open Championship</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/sport/sports-fix/find/story-fn89guyk-1226096291119" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald-Sun</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Rebels claim victory in the eastern town of <a href="/wiki/Brega" title="Brega">Brega</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE76H00Q20110718?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Libya)" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs (Libya)">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Abdel_Rahman_Shalgham" title="Abdel Rahman Shalgham">Abdel Rahman Shalgham</a> says that the Libyan government was responsible for the bombing of <a href="/wiki/UTA_Flight_772" title="UTA Flight 772">UTA Flight 772</a> in 1989 over <a href="/wiki/Niger" title="Niger">Niger</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/07/18/158145.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>:
<ul>
<li>50 protesters arrested in the city of <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> are released. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14182585" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a> suspends operations at its embassy in Syria, after it was attacked by government supporters. <a class="external text" href="http://gulfnews.com/news/region/syria/qatar-embassy-suspends-mission-in-syria-1.839272" rel="nofollow">(<i>Gulf News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan (2001–present)</a>:
<ul>
<li>US General <a href="/wiki/David_Petraeus" title="David Petraeus">David Petraeus</a> hands over command of <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> forces in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> to <a href="/wiki/United_States_Marine_Corps" title="United States Marine Corps">United States Marine Corps</a> <a href="/wiki/General_(United_States)" title="General (United States)">Lieutenant General</a> <a href="/wiki/John_R._Allen" title="John R. Allen">John R. Allen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/07/18/afghanistan.petraeus.handover/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Rioting at a police station in <a href="/wiki/Hotan" title="Hotan">Hotan</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a> region of western <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> kills at least four people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14186163" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/china/Several-killed-in-police-station-attack-in-Chinas-restive-province-bordering-Pakistan/articleshow/9273172.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-07/18/c_13992884.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Nine months after a goodwill gesture <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> will commence negotiations in August on the return of more than 1,200 volumes of ancient Korean royal archives taken during <a href="/wiki/Korea_under_Japanese_rule" title="Korea under Japanese rule">Japanese rule between 1910 and 1945</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/18/64/0200000000AEN20110718002800315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>
<li>The <i><a href="/wiki/Philadelphia_Daily_News" title="Philadelphia Daily News">Philadelphia Daily News</a></i> reports that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholicism)" title="Cardinal (Catholicism)">Cardinal</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Justin_Rigali" title="Justin Rigali">Justin Rigali</a> will resign five months after a U.S. <a href="/wiki/Grand_jury" title="Grand jury">grand jury</a> accuses the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Archdiocese_of_Philadelphia" title="Archdiocese of Philadelphia">Archdiocese of Philadelphia</a> that he heads of failing to investigate claims of <a href="/wiki/Sexual_abuse" title="Sexual abuse">sexual abuse</a> of children by clergy in the diocese. <a class="external text" href="http://www.philly.com/philly/news/local/20110718_Sources__Rigali_out_as_leader_of_Philadelphia_Archdiocese.html" rel="nofollow">(Philly.com)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cisco_Systems" title="Cisco Systems">Cisco Systems</a> announces plans to cut 11,500 jobs including transfer of a plant employing 5,000 people in <a href="/wiki/Ciudad_Ju%C3%A1rez" title="Ciudad Juárez">Juarez, Mexico</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Foxconn" title="Foxconn">Foxconn</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnbc.com/id/43800031" rel="nofollow">(CNBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Eastern_United_States" title="Eastern United States">eastern United States</a> will have a <a href="/wiki/Heat_wave" title="Heat wave">heat wave</a> this week which has already commenced in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Plains_States" title="Plains States">Plains States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Midwestern_United_States" title="Midwestern United States">Midwest</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/weather/news/extremes/2011-07-17-heat-wave-to-hit-East_n.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li>The U.S. city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Phoenix_Arizona" title="Phoenix Arizona">Phoenix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a>, is hit by a <a href="/wiki/Haboob" title="Haboob">haboob</a> or dust storm. <a class="external text" href="http://www.myfoxphoenix.com/dpp/weather/wall-of-dust-moves-across-pinal-county-07182011" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Vatican</a> and <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> establish diplomatic relations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bernama.com/bernama/v5/newsgeneral.php?id=602093" rel="nofollow">(Bernama)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jd2YcSjbAvO7MmbXvW7pnL6gumIw?docId=cc386ad34caf41cbb8583c3d58c90230" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> claims to have taken control of three Iranian Kurdish <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PJAK" title="PJAK">PJAK</a> camps inside <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/07/18/158154.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President of Russia</a> <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a> commences a two-day visit to <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20110718/165254216.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">United States Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> arrives in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> for two days of talks with the Indian government. <a class="external text" href="http://ibnlive.in.com/news/hillary-to-arrive-india-for-talks-today/168276-3.html" rel="nofollow">(IBN Live)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The trial of five <a href="/wiki/Blog" title="Blog">bloggers</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> for advocating democratic reforms resumes. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011717213325459958.html?utm_content=automateplus&amp;utm_campaign=Trial5&amp;utm_source=SocialFlow&amp;utm_term=tweets&amp;utm_medium=MasterAccount" rel="nofollow">(Al-Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Somali_people" title="Somali people">Somali</a> man <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Omer_Abdi_Mohamed&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Omer Abdi Mohamed (page does not exist)">Omer Abdi Mohamed</a> pleads guilty in the US city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minneapolis,_Minnesota" title="Minneapolis, Minnesota">Minneapolis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">Minnesota</a>, to helping recruit people to travel to <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> to assist the terror group <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabab</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5iLNIVhoU2SLPSrW3CCdIdpbmIQ0w?docId=6087da778f2f4742bb0addeb2f3147fe" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_County_Superior_Court" title="San Francisco County Superior Court">San Francisco County Superior Court</a> in the US state of <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> announces plans to cut 200 jobs and close 25 out of 63 court rooms due to budget problems. <a class="external text" href="http://abclocal.go.com/kgo/story?section=news/local/san_francisco&amp;id=8253965" rel="nofollow">(ABC News America)</a></li>
<li>An <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Btselem" title="Btselem">Israeli rights group</a>, "No Minor Matter", criticises the Israeli government for jailing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> stone throwers under the age of 14. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14189730" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A new <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_Egypt" title="Cabinet of Egypt">Cabinet</a> is sworn in in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>, with half the former members being replaced due to ongoing protests since the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/2011717232716512838.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_Defence" title="Secretary of State for Defence">Secretary of State for Defence</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liam_Fox" title="Liam Fox">Liam Fox</a> announces plans to reduce the <a href="/wiki/British_Army" title="British Army">British Army</a> to its smallest size since the start of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Boer_War" title="Second Boer War">Second Boer War</a> just over a century ago. By 2020, troop numbers will be reduced from the present 101,000 to 82,000, with a greater reliability on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Territorial_Army_(United_Kingdom)" title="Territorial Army (United Kingdom)">Territorial Army</a> soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201009116032255" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/politics/2011/jul/18/liam-fox-army-cuts" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>News International scandal:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a>, cuts short a tour of <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a> due to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">News of the World phone hacking affair</a> inquiry. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/politics/2011/jul/18/david-cameron-africa-phone-hacking" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Assistant_Commissioner" title="Assistant Commissioner">Assistant Commissioner</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Yates_(police_officer)" title="John Yates (police officer)">John Yates</a> is called in for questioning for his links with former News executive <a href="/wiki/Neil_Wallis" title="Neil Wallis">Neil Wallis</a> and later resigns. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/phone-hacking/8644774/Phone-Hacking-John-Yates-facing-questions-over-Neil-Wallis-links.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14181344" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> phone-hacking whistleblower <a href="/wiki/Sean_Hoare" title="Sean Hoare">Sean Hoare</a> is found dead at his home. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/18/news-of-the-world-sean-hoare" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/LulzSec" title="LulzSec">LulzSec</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(computer_security)" title="Hacker (computer security)">hackers</a> attack <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sun_(United_Kingdom)" title="The Sun (United Kingdom)">The Sun</a></i> website posting a story about the fake death of <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/top-stories/lulzsec-hack-into-the-sun/story-e6frfkp9-1226097292750" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/18/sun-website-hacked-lulzsec" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/phone-hacking/8646558/Phone-Hacking-The-Suns-website-hacked-by-LulzSec-with-fake-story-about-Rupert-Murdochs-death.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bob_Stenehjem" title="Bob Stenehjem">Bob Stenehjem</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_Majority_Leader" title="Senate Majority Leader">Senate Majority Leader</a> in the US state of <a href="/wiki/North_Dakota" title="North Dakota">North Dakota</a>, is killed in an accident in <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.greenfieldreporter.com/view/story/f986d43ebe064582bfc98572f68c74b9/ND--Obit-Stenehjem/" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Greenfield Reporter</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dawn_(spacecraft)" title="Dawn (spacecraft)">Dawn</a> spacecraft takes its first photo of the <a href="/wiki/Asteroid" title="Asteroid">asteroid</a> <a href="/wiki/4_Vesta" title="4 Vesta">4 Vesta</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/ondeadline/post/2011/07/dawn-probe-snaps-first-close-up-of-gaint-asteroid/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> athlete and <a href="/wiki/Iran%27s_Strongest_Man" title="Iran's Strongest Man">Iran's Strongest Man</a> <a href="/wiki/Rouhollah_Dadashi" title="Rouhollah Dadashi">Rouhollah Dadashi</a> is killed in a fight which started as an argument with another driver and his passengers. Two of them are arrested by police. <a class="external text" href="http://nasehpour.blogspot.com/2011/07/iranian-athlete-ruhollah-dadashi-was.html" rel="nofollow">(Blogspot)</a></li>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 19, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-19</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_19&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Security forces shoot dead at least 10 people in <a href="/wiki/Homs" title="Homs">Homs</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.emirates247.com/news/world/10-reported-killed-in-syrian-raids-2011-07-19-1.408623" rel="nofollow">(Emirates 24/7)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jD97unh-0z8CGArL2FnVfsTaq0WQ?docId=5b439a939ee34bce9ffeb0374c8f3c49" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Forces loyal to <a href="/wiki/Guinea" title="Guinea">Guinean</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Guinea" title="List of heads of state of Guinea">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Cond%C3%A9" title="Alpha Condé">Alpha Condé</a> repel an attack by unknown assailants on his residence in <a href="/wiki/Conakry" title="Conakry">Conakry</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14197052" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A leaked <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> report suggests <a href="/wiki/War_crime" title="War crime">war crimes</a> may have been committed in <a href="/wiki/South_Kordofan" title="South Kordofan">South Kordofan</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> during a recent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Kordofan_conflict" title="South Kordofan conflict">conflict</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201171992810221479.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>:
<ul>
<li>Eight <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> employees of the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> based <a href="/wiki/American_Refugee_Committee" title="American Refugee Committee">American Refugee Committee</a> are kidnapped in southwest Pakistan near the border with <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/19/us-pakistan-kidnap-idUSTRE76I0PY20110719" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israeli_Navy" title="Israeli Navy">Israel's navy</a> confiscates a <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> yacht bound for <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a>, which departed from <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> and attempted to run the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Blockade_of_the_Gaza_Strip_(2007-present)" title="Blockade of the Gaza Strip (2007-present)">blockade</a> after repeated warnings to make for <a href="/wiki/Ashdod" title="Ashdod">Ashdod</a> instead. No casualties are reported. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hOzayaUHSvngPXpp4bza5o8_2QvQ?docId=CNG.d6302f5fdf47380d57e991a1d3bf4851.391" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A 6.1 magnitude <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Uzbekistan%E2%80%93Kyrgyzstan_earthquake" title="2011 Uzbekistan–Kyrgyzstan earthquake">earthquake</a> strikes in southern <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyzstan</a>, near the border with <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jgsH7L6hzL_qFQa_0gYZ054zdkiw?docId=c0488f2ac1464e18bd252ad1b0167863" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Ma-on_(2011)" title="Typhoon Ma-on (2011)">Typhoon Ma-on</a>, the second typhoon of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2011 Pacific typhoon season">2011 Pacific typhoon season</a>, approaches the main <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> island of <a href="/wiki/Honshu" title="Honshu">Honshu</a> leading to cancellation of air services. <a class="external text" href="http://en.apa.az/news.php?id=151778" rel="nofollow">(APA)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://search.japantimes.co.jp/cgi-bin/nn20110719a3.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Japan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2011 Pacific hurricane season">Tropical Storm Dora</a> becomes a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">hurricane</a> with a tropical storm watch issued for southwestern <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/nhc_storms.shtml" rel="nofollow">(National Hurricane Centre)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ASEAN" title="ASEAN">ASEAN</a> foreign ministers get together for their annual summit on the island of <a href="/wiki/Bali" title="Bali">Bali</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> with concerns over <a href="/wiki/Territorial_disputes_in_the_South_China_Sea" title="Territorial disputes in the South China Sea">territorial claims</a> on the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/asean-ministers-arrive-for-bali-talks-20110719-1hmn6.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14195994" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">Federal Bureau of Investigation</a> (FBI) arrests an alleged agent of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Inter-Services_Intelligence" title="Inter-Services Intelligence">Inter-Services Intelligence</a> in the US state of <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">Virginia</a> for making illegal campaign contributions. <a class="external text" href="http://firstread.msnbc.msn.com/_news/2011/07/19/7112067-fbi-arrests-pakistani-agent-for-making-political-contributions-in-us" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>Sixteen alleged members of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(computer_security)" title="Hacker (computer security)">computer hacking</a> group <a href="/wiki/Anonymous_(group)" title="Anonymous (group)">Anonymous</a> are arrested in FBI raids across several states in the US. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/CRIME/07/19/new.york.anonymous.warrants/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.justice.gov/opa/pr/2011/July/11-opa-944.html" rel="nofollow">(US Department of Justice)</a></li>
<li>A protest in the US city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Francisco,_California" title="San Francisco, California">San Francisco</a> turns violent resulting in the arrest of 35 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcbayarea.com/news/local/Bayview-Shooting-Protest-End-with-Arrests-125866423.html" rel="nofollow">(NBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Vice President of the People's Republic of China">Vice President</a> <a href="/wiki/Xi_Jinping" title="Xi Jinping">Xi Jinping</a> says the Chinese government will "smash" attempts for an <a href="/wiki/Tibetan_independence_movement" title="Tibetan independence movement">independent</a> <a href="/wiki/Tibet" title="Tibet">Tibet</a> in a speech outside the <a href="/wiki/Potala_Palace" title="Potala Palace">Potala Palace</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14205998" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.turkishweekly.net/news/119521/chinese-vp-pledges-accelerated-development-in-tibet.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Journal of Turkish Weekly</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands_Governor" title="Northern Mariana Islands Governor">Northern Mariana Islands Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Benigno_Fitial" title="Benigno Fitial">Benigno Fitial</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guam_Governor" title="Guam Governor">Guam Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Calvo" title="Eddie Calvo">Eddie Calvo</a> state that they are in serious talks to potentially merge the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._territories" title="U.S. territories">U.S. territories</a> of <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.saipantribune.com/newsstory.aspx?newsID=111145&amp;cat=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>Saipan Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li>News Corporation affair
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a> Chief Executive <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a> and his son <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Murdoch_(media_executive)" title="James Murdoch (media executive)">James Murdoch</a> appear before a select committee of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_parliament" title="United Kingdom parliament">United Kingdom parliament</a> over the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>. Murdoch Senior apologises for the scandal, but says he is not responsible for it. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/19/us-newscorp-idUSTRE76H07P20110719?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14195259" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A man attacks Murdoch during the final part of questioning with a shaving cream pie. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/entertainmentnewsbuzz/2011/07/murdochs-struggle-to-defend-themselves-before-parliament.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Appearing later at the same hearing former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> Chief Executive <a href="/wiki/Rebekah_Brooks" title="Rebekah Brooks">Rebekah Brooks</a> says NI acted "quickly and decisively" in dealing with "abhorrent" phone-hacking at the <i>News of the World</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-14209990" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Voters in the 30th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wisconsin_Senate" title="Wisconsin Senate">Senate</a> district in the US state of <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</a> go to the polls for the first <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin_Senate_recall_elections,_2011" title="Wisconsin Senate recall elections, 2011">recall election</a> for <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democrat</a> <a href="/wiki/Dave_Hansen" title="Dave Hansen">Dave Hansen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/19/us/19wisconsin.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>US budget debate
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a>, <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, endorses in principle a bipartisan proposal developed in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> to cut debt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/gang-of-six-budget-cutting-plan-gains-momentum-in-senate/2011/07/19/gIQANkdzNI_story.html?wpisrc=al_politics" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> votes to approve the "Cut, Cap and Balance Act" by 234-190 but it is unlikely to pass the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/house-pursues-balanced-budget-bill-need-for-backup-plan-acknowledged/2011/07/19/gIQAaz0vNI_story.html?wpisrc=al_politics" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://politicalticker.blogs.cnn.com/2011/07/19/breaking-house-passes-cut-cap-and-balance-bill/" rel="nofollow">(CNN Political Ticker)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Religion</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XVI" title="Pope Benedict XVI">Pope Benedict XVI</a> appoints <a href="/wiki/Charles_J._Chaput" title="Charles J. Chaput">Charles J. Chaput</a>, the current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Archdiocese_of_Denver" title="Archdiocese of Denver">Archbishop</a> of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Denver,_Colorado" title="Denver, Colorado">Denver</a>, as the head of the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Philadelphia" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Philadelphia">Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Philadelphia</a> replacing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholicism)" title="Cardinal (Catholicism)">Cardinal</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Justin_Rigali" title="Justin Rigali">Justin Rigali</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5iNDlC92H3OcwC4-atWGvzJhCWwvQ?docId=c35fcf46bd4b4aedb334e182d992bd21" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> says it has installed faster <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_centrifuge" title="Nuclear centrifuge">nuclear centrifuges</a> to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Uranium_enrichment" title="Uranium enrichment">enrich uranium</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hhGqmLVav8hMbmgNbzKqRgN6zKeQ?docId=CNG.7e4a598f9713cc3df378c520326d27b1.661" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">Space Shuttle Atlantis</a> undocks from the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> for the final time in the history of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_shuttle" title="Space shuttle">space shuttle</a> program. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nasa.gov/mission_pages/shuttle/main/index.html" rel="nofollow">(NASA)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Japan_women%27s_national_football_team" title="Japan women's national football team">Japan women's national football team</a> returns home to be greeted by thousands of fans after winning the <a href="/wiki/2011_FIFA_Women%27s_World_Cup" title="2011 FIFA Women's World Cup">2011 FIFA Women's World Cup</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/Sport/Story/STIStory_692180.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Troops surround the <a href="/wiki/Harasta" title="Harasta">Harasta</a> suburb of the capital <a href="/wiki/Damascus" title="Damascus">Damascus</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011720134034659458.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Riots erupt in <a href="/wiki/Malawi" title="Malawi">Malawi</a> in protest against the government of <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Malawi" title="List of heads of state of Malawi">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Bingu_wa_Mutharika" title="Bingu wa Mutharika">Bingu wa Mutharika</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14217148" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> <a href="/wiki/Ali_Aghazadeh_Dafsari" title="Ali Aghazadeh Dafsari">Ali Aghazadeh Dafsari</a> claims that <a href="/wiki/Army_of_the_Guardians_of_the_Islamic_Revolution" title="Army of the Guardians of the Islamic Revolution">Revolutionary Guard</a> forces shot down a <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> spy drone over the <a href="/wiki/Fordo" title="Fordo">Fordo</a> located <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Uranium_enrichment" title="Uranium enrichment">uranium enrichment</a> facility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hU-F7xlxfCBeRku76bnXREIERuxQ?docId=b83096f9ee124922aaa91980c7c98c1e" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google)</a></li>
<li>Up to 80 people, including soldiers, are arrested in <a href="/wiki/Guinea" title="Guinea">Guinea</a> after a failed assassination attempt on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Guinea" title="List of heads of state of Guinea">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Cond%C3%A9" title="Alpha Condé">Alpha Condé</a> on 19 July. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE76J0M920110720?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_people" title="British people">British</a> artist <a href="/wiki/Lucian_Freud" title="Lucian Freud">Lucian Freud</a> dies at his home in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> following a brief illness. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/22/arts/lucian-freud-adept-portraiture-artist-dies-at-88.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Horn_of_Africa_famine" title="2011 Horn of Africa famine">2011 Horn of Africa famine</a>: The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> declares a <a href="/wiki/Famine" title="Famine">famine</a> in southern <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/2011720756724143.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Ma-on_(2011)" title="Typhoon Ma-on (2011)">Typhoon Ma-on</a> hits <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>, landing in <a href="/wiki/Tokushima_Prefecture" title="Tokushima Prefecture">Tokushima Prefecture</a>; at least 47 people are injured and 1 person is left missing before the typhoon is downgraded to a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_storm" title="Tropical storm">tropical storm</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.kyodonews.jp/news/2011/07/103842.html" rel="nofollow">(Kyodo)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/Article.aspx?articleId=708119&amp;publicationSubCategoryId=200" rel="nofollow">(PhilStar)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usno.navy.mil/NOOC/nmfc-ph/RSS/jtwc/warnings/wp0811web.txt" rel="nofollow">(US NO)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2011 Pacific hurricane season">Hurricane Dora</a> strengthens to a Category 4 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">hurricane</a> as it travels towards <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/nhc_storms.shtml" rel="nofollow">(NHC)</a></li>
<li>A 6.1 magnitude earthquake occurs near the <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Fergana" title="Fergana">Fergana</a> killing 13 people in Uzbekistan and one person in <a href="/wiki/Tajikistan" title="Tajikistan">Tajikistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/21/world/asia/21briefs-Quake.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> official accuses <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> of breaking international sanctions by importing luxury goods for senior officials. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/20/0200000000AEN20110720001900315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> bans the import of <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">horses</a> from <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> following an outbreak of <a href="/wiki/Henipavirus" title="Henipavirus">Hendra virus</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://au.news.yahoo.com/thewest/a/-/world/9881273/malaysia-bans-australian-horses/" rel="nofollow">(AAP via <i>The West Australian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australian_Federal_Police" title="Australian Federal Police">Australian Federal Police</a> officers fire <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> to subdue a riot by <a href="/wiki/Asylum_seeker" title="Asylum seeker">asylum seekers</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Christmas_Island_Immigration_Reception_and_Processing_Centre" title="Christmas Island Immigration Reception and Processing Centre">Christmas Island Immigration Reception and Processing Centre</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/more-news/afp-fires-tear-gas-after-asylum-seekers-riot-on-christmas-island/story-fn7x8me2-1226098173702" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald-Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> arrests <a href="/wiki/Goran_Had%C5%BEi%C4%87" title="Goran Hadžić">Goran Hadžić</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatian</a> <a href="/wiki/Serbs_of_Croatia" title="Serbs of Croatia">Serb</a> wartime leader, indicted for alleged <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Croatian_War_of_Independence" title="Croatian War of Independence">Croatian War of Independence</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2011-07-20/serbia-war-crimes-goran-hadzic/2803266" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via ABC Online)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Supreme Court of Georgia (U.S. state)">Supreme Court</a> of the US state of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a> has agreed to the execution of <a href="/wiki/Cobb_County,_Georgia" title="Cobb County, Georgia">Cobb County</a> killer <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Grant_DeYoung" title="Andrew Grant DeYoung">Andrew Grant DeYoung</a> to be videotaped. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ajc.com/news/cobb/state-supreme-court-allows-1029058.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Atlanta Journal-Constitution</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> faces questions in <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Parliament of the United Kingdom">parliament</a> over his decision to hire <a href="/wiki/Andy_Coulson" title="Andy Coulson">Andy Coulson</a>, a former editor of the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> at the time of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/20/us-newscorp-idUSTRE76H07P20110720?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A report by the <a href="/wiki/Home_Affairs_Select_Committee" title="Home Affairs Select Committee">Home Affairs Select Committee</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_House_of_Commons" title="United Kingdom House of Commons">United Kingdom House of Commons</a> accuses the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police" title="Metropolitan Police">Metropolitan Police</a> of a "catalogue of errors" in relation to the affair. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14212485" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Australia" title="Prime Minister of Australia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Julia_Gillard" title="Julia Gillard">Julia Gillard</a> says that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_Limited" title="News Limited">News Limited</a> – the Australian arm of News Corporation – will face "hard questions" in the wake of the phone hacking scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14212954" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chinese_people" title="Chinese people">Chinese</a> <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a> player <a href="/wiki/Yao_Ming" title="Yao Ming">Yao Ming</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Houston_Rockets" title="Houston Rockets">Houston Rockets</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">National Basketball Association</a> team announces his retirement in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/sports/basketball/nba/2011-07-20-3074821903_x.htm" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Golf" title="Golf">golf</a>, the <a href="/wiki/LPGA" title="LPGA">LPGA</a> announces that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evian_Masters" title="Evian Masters">Evian Masters</a>, a tournament held in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> that is a <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_major_golf_championships" title="Women's major golf championships">major championship</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Ladies_European_Tour" title="Ladies European Tour">Ladies European Tour</a>, will become the LPGA's fifth major in 2013. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/golf/story/_/id/6786719/evian-masters-now-fifth-major-lpga-tour-2013" rel="nofollow">(AP via ESPN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">baseball</a> player <a href="/wiki/Hideki_Matsui" title="Hideki Matsui">Hideki Matsui</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Oakland_Athletics" title="Oakland Athletics">Oakland Athletics</a> hits his 500th career <a href="/wiki/Home_run" title="Home run">home run</a> in his professional career playing in both <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nippon_Professional_Baseball" title="Nippon Professional Baseball">Nippon Professional Baseball</a> in his homeland. <a class="external text" href="http://english.kyodonews.jp/news/2011/07/104124.html" rel="nofollow">(Kyodo News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The 2011 <a href="/wiki/Alzheimer%27s_Association" title="Alzheimer's Association">Alzheimer's Association</a> International Conference in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paris,_France" title="Paris, France">Paris, France</a> announces that Samantha Burnham and others at the Australian national science agency, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CSIRO" title="CSIRO">CSIRO</a>, working with several universities, have produced what may one day become a routine, valid blood test for nine hormones and proteins that, when too high, can serve as predictors of the presence of the hallmark <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beta_amyloid" title="Beta amyloid">beta amyloid</a> plaques of <a href="/wiki/Alzheimer%27s_disease" title="Alzheimer's disease">Alzheimer's disease</a>.</li>
</ul>
</td>

<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Malawian_protests" title="2011 Malawian protests">2011 Malawian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>At least eighteen people are killed during mass protests in <a href="/wiki/Malawi" title="Malawi">Malawi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.trust.org/alertnet/news/malawi-protest-death-toll-rises-to-18-official/" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>

<li>Author <a href="/wiki/Lee_Child" title="Lee Child">Lee Child</a> – creator of the <a href="/wiki/Jack_Reacher" title="Jack Reacher">Jack Reacher</a> series – wins the novel of the year award at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Harrogate_Crime_Writing_Festival" title="Harrogate Crime Writing Festival">Harrogate Crime Writing Festival</a> for his book <i><a href="/wiki/61_Hours" title="61 Hours">61 Hours</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/entertainment-arts-14246226" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Euro_zone" title="Euro zone">Euro zone</a> leaders secure a €109 billion bailout for <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> with the country going into default for a short period, but with increased powers for the main European rescue fund to assist countries that have not been bailed out, such as <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/22/business/global/European-Union-Summit-Meeting-on-Greek-Debt.html?_r=1&amp;hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>

<li>Two dozen people have died this week in a <a href="/wiki/Heat_wave" title="Heat wave">heat wave</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/22/us/22heat.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Australian_people" title="Australian people">Australian</a> radio host <a href="/wiki/Derryn_Hinch" title="Derryn Hinch">Derryn Hinch</a> is sentenced to five months <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Home_detention" title="Home detention">home detention</a> for broadcasting the names of two sex offenders. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/national/derryn-hinch-to-be-sentenced-for-contempt-of-court-today/story-e6frfkvr-1226098924136" rel="nofollow">(News.com.au)</a></li>
<li>Three <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Russia" title="Law enforcement in Russia">Russian police officers</a> are convicted for abuse of office in <a href="/wiki/Khabarovsk" title="Khabarovsk">Khabarovsk</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Far_Eastern_Federal_District" title="Far Eastern Federal District">Far Eastern Federal District</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/crime/20110721/165307145.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>Another riot occurs at <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Christmas_Island_Immigration_Reception_and_Processing_Centre" title="Christmas Island Immigration Reception and Processing Centre">Christmas Island Immigration Reception and Processing Centre</a> overnight with <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> again used to quell inmates. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/more-news/another-riot-erupts-at-christmas-island-detention-centre/story-fn7x8me2-1226098985111" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Japanese_people" title="Japanese people">Japanese</a> court sentences Tatsuya Ichihashi to life imprisonment for the <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Lindsay_Hawker" title="Murder of Lindsay Hawker">murder of British teacher Lindsay Hawker</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Lindsay-Ann-Hawker-Murder-Tatsuya-Ichihashi-Gets-Life-Sentence-For-Killing-British-Girl/Article/201107316034558?lpos=World_News_Carousel_Region_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_16034558_Lindsay_Ann_Hawker_Murder%3A_Tatsuya_Ichihashi_Gets_Life_Sentence_For_Killing_British_Girl" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/MSNBC" title="MSNBC">MSNBC</a> reports that the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Justice" title="United States Department of Justice">United States Department of Justice</a> is investigating claims that <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">News Corporation</a>'s advertising arm repeatedly <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(term)" title="Hacker (term)">hacked</a> into the computers of competitors. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43847056/ns/us_news-crime_and_courts/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>Two former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> executives have called into question certain aspects of the evidence given by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Murdoch_(media_executive)" title="James Murdoch (media executive)">James Murdoch</a> to a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_(United_Kingdom)" title="House of Commons (United Kingdom)">House of Commons</a> select Committee earlier this week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14242763" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Central_Bank_of_Iran" title="Central Bank of Iran">Central Bank of Iran</a> launches a <a class="external text" href="http://reform.cbi.ir/" rel="nofollow">website</a>, intending to poll the <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> public about <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iranian_targeted_subsidy_plan" title="Iranian targeted subsidy plan">planned economic reforms</a> and a change of <a href="/wiki/Iranian_rial" title="Iranian rial">national currency</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.tabnak.ir" rel="nofollow">(Tabnak)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">Space Shuttle Atlantis</a> lands at the <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">Kennedy Space Center</a>, concluding its <a href="/wiki/STS-135" title="STS-135">final mission</a> and marking the end of the 30-year <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_program" title="Space Shuttle program">Space Shuttle program</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/tech/science/space/2011-07-21-shuttle-atlantis-landing_n.htm" rel="nofollow">(USA TODAY)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/US/07/21/shuttle.landing/" rel="nofollow">(<i>CNN</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Team owners in the <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> have voted to approve a 10-year deal with the <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League_Players_Association" title="National Football League Players Association">National Football League Players Association</a> and to end a <a href="/wiki/2011_NFL_season" title="2011 NFL season">lockout</a> if players approve. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ajc.com/sports/atlanta-falcons/ap-source-nfl-owners-1033816.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Atlamta Journal Constitution</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/sports/nfl-lockout-owners-poised-to-approve-new-labor-deal-but-new-differences-emerge/2011/07/21/gIQA9IB2RI_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The 2000th match in the history of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Test_Cricket" title="Test Cricket">Test Cricket</a> starts at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lord%27s_Cricket_Ground" title="Lord's Cricket Ground">Lord's Cricket Ground</a> in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> between <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/England_national_cricket_team" title="England national cricket team">England</a> and <a href="/wiki/India_national_cricket_team" title="India national cricket team">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/sport/cricket/article-2017485/Nasser-Hussain-Dhoni-hands-Strauss-advantage.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.espnstar.com/cricket/international-cricket/news/detail/item644823/A-celebration-of-2000-glorious-Tests/" rel="nofollow">(ESPN Star)</a></li>

<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Norway_attacks" title="2011 Norway attacks">2011 Norway attacks</a>
<ul>
<li>An explosion damages government buildings in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oslo,_Norway" title="Oslo, Norway">Oslo, Norway</a> at 15:25; at eight people are killed and several are reportedly injured. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/07/2011722135232705239.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Explosion-At-Oslo-Government-Building-Containing-Prime-Ministers-Office-According-To-Reuters/Article/201107416035628?lpos=World_News_First_Home_Article_Teaser_Region_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_16035628_Explosion_At_Oslo_Government_Building_Containing_Prime_Ministers_Office%2C_According_To_Reuters" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>A gunman opens fire at a <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(Norway)" title="Labour Party (Norway)">Labour Party</a> camp in <a href="/wiki/Ut%C3%B8ya" title="Utøya">Utøya</a> with 69 people killed. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/video/europe/2011/07/2011722205015432143.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/23/norway-attacks" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Police arrest a Norwegian man <a href="/wiki/Anders_Behring_Breivik" title="Anders Behring Breivik">Anders Behring Breivik</a> for the shooting at <a href="/wiki/Ut%C3%B8ya" title="Utøya">Utøya</a> with reports of links to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Right-wing_extremism" title="Right-wing extremism">right-wing extremism</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctv.ca/CTVNews/TopStories/20110722/oslo-explosino-norway-blast-110722/" rel="nofollow">(CTV News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Norway-Live-Blog-Oslo-Bomb-Attack-And-Utoya-Shooting/Article/201107416035759?lpos=World_News_Carousel_Region_1&amp;lid=ARTICLE_16035759_Norway_Live_Blog%3A_Oslo_Bomb_Attack_And_Utoya_Shooting" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: Hundreds of thousands of people take to the streets after Friday prayers in cities across <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/22/us-syria-idUSTRE76L1P720110722" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Malawian_protests" title="2011 Malawian protests">2011 Malawian protests</a>: Authorities block a mass funeral for seven people killed during anti-government riots. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news24.com/Africa/News/Malawi-blocks-mass-funeral-for-riot-victims-20110722-2" rel="nofollow">(News 24)</a></li>
</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepalese</a> officials say <a href="/wiki/Monsoon" title="Monsoon">monsoon</a> rains have swollen two major rivers in the country and have increased the threat of widespread flooding. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/news/world/nepal-rivers-rising-1.1103922" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>

<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabaab</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist" title="Islamist">Islamist</a> militant group in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> says a ban on aid groups working in parts of the country remains. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/201172291538656428.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> is giving <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadian_Dollar" title="Canadian Dollar">C$</a>50 million more, in addition to the $22 million it has already donated, to aid agencies working in <a href="/wiki/East_Africa" title="East Africa">East Africa</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/world/story/2011/07/22/famine-funding.html?ref=rss" rel="nofollow">(CBC News)</a></li>

<li>British Labour MP <a href="/wiki/Tom_Watson_(Labour_politician)" title="Tom Watson (Labour politician)">Tom Watson</a> says he is contacting Scotland Yard after two former <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> executives contradicted <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Murdoch_(media_executive)" title="James Murdoch (media executive)">James Murdoch</a>'s evidence to a Parliamentary Select Committee. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/crime/mp-contacts-met-over-murdoch-claims-2318751.html" rel="nofollow"><i>The Independent</i></a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Norway_attacks" title="2011 Norway attacks">2011 Norway attacks</a>: The death toll from the shootings on <a href="/wiki/Ut%C3%B8ya" title="Utøya">Utøya</a> and bombing in Oslo reaches at least 92. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14259356" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43854355/ns/world_news-europe/" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anders_Behring_Breivik" title="Anders Behring Breivik">Anders Behring Breivik</a>, the man arrested in connection with terrorism in Norway, reveals himself as to have <a href="/wiki/Islamophobia" title="Islamophobia">anti-Muslim</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Right-wing_extremism" title="Right-wing extremism">right-wing extremist</a> views, stating that the attacks were "atrocious, but necessary." <a class="external text" href="http://www.document.no/anders-behring-breivik/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Dokument</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dagbladet.no/2011/07/20/nyheter/politikk/innenriks/auf/17367745/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Dagbladet</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2017851/Norway-attacks-gunman-Anders-Behring-Breivik-right-wing-extremist-hated-Muslims.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>: The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> says <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> forces may have committed <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a> amid the ongoing protests. <a class="external text" href="http://www.capitalfm.co.ke/news/2011/07/23/un-fears-crimes-against-humanity-in-syria/" rel="nofollow">(Capital FM Kenya)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesofoman.com/innercat.asp?detail=48048&amp;rand=" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of Oman</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>: Rebels claim to have fired rockets at a meeting of senior <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Gaddafi</a>-regime officials in the capital <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/20117238472925170.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Mumbai_bombings" title="2011 Mumbai bombings">2011 Mumbai bombings</a>: The death toll from the attacks rises to 22. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jX8604DBbUhwAOP1k_COK4nf1rgw?docId=CNG.78170485c209b06fff87142edb44c459.531" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/city/mumbai/Mumbai-blasts-toll-climbs-to-22/articleshow/9334535.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gatluak_Gai" title="Gatluak Gai">Gatluak Gai</a>, a key <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudanese</a> rebel leader who signed a peace deal with the <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> government this week, is killed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14261525" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unicef" title="Unicef">Unicef</a> states that a child dies from malnutrition every six minutes (250 a day) in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thesun.co.uk/sol/homepage/news/3710240/Child-dies-every-six-minutes-in-Somalia-famine.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sun</i>)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Asylum_seeker" title="Asylum seeker">Asylum seekers</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scherger_Immigration_Detention_Centre" title="Scherger Immigration Detention Centre">Scherger Immigration Detention Centre</a> near <a href="/wiki/Weipa,_Queensland" title="Weipa, Queensland">Weipa</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> start harming themselves in protest. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-national/detainees-start-self-harm-in-qld-protest-20110723-1htxc.html" rel="nofollow">(AAP via <i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>
<ul>
<li>Claims of phone hacking at the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mirror" title="Daily Mirror">Daily Mirror</a></i> and other <a href="/wiki/Trinity_Mirror" title="Trinity Mirror">Trinity Mirror</a> publications are made by former <i>Mirror</i> journalist <a href="/wiki/James_Hipwell" title="James Hipwell">James Hipwell</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/media/press/hacking-was-endemic-at-the-mirror-says-former-reporter-2319039.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14259180" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/jul/23/phone-hacking-piers-morgan-mirror" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A gunman fatally shoots six people, including himself, and wounds four others in a shooting in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grand_Prairie" title="Grand Prairie">Grand Prairie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/jul/24/gunman-texas-birthday-party" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daryoush_Rezaei" title="Daryoush Rezaei">Daryoush Rezaei</a>, an Iranian scientist, is shot dead outside his home in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a>. It was reported that the scientist had links to the country's nuclear programme. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-14263126" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Nearly 4,000 employees of the US <a href="/wiki/Federal_Aviation_Administration" title="Federal Aviation Administration">Federal Aviation Administration</a> are <a href="/wiki/Furlough" title="Furlough">furloughed</a> due to <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">Congressional</a> authorisation for its programs lapsing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.faa.gov/news/updates/?newsId=64216" rel="nofollow">(FAA)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a> go to the polls for <a href="/wiki/Elections_in_Sri_Lanka" title="Elections in Sri Lanka">local elections</a>, with one person dying in clashes between supporters of rival parties in the <a href="/wiki/Anuradhapura" title="Anuradhapura">Anuradhapura</a> district. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-14259705" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Latvian_parliamentary_dissolution_referendum,_2011" title="Latvian parliamentary dissolution referendum, 2011">Latvian parliamentary dissolution referendum</a> with 95 per cent of voters supporting dissolution of the <a href="/wiki/Saeima" title="Saeima">Saeima</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/E/EU_LATVIA_REFERENDUM?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT&amp;CTIME=2011-07-23-16-42-44" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>General <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_M._Shalikashvili" title="John M. Shalikashvili">John M. Shalikashvili</a>, a Polish-American former <a href="/wiki/Chairman_of_the_Joint_Chiefs_of_Staff" title="Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff">Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff</a> under President Bill Clinton during the Post-Cold War years and the Bosnian conflicts who had suffered a major stroke several years ago, dies.</li>
<li>South Vietnamese premier and general Nguyễn Cao Kỳ dies at age 80 in Kuala Lumpur, Malaysia.</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/CERN" title="CERN">CERN</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Large_Hadron_Collider" title="Large Hadron Collider">Large Hadron Collider (LHC)</a> produces notable fluctuations in search for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Higgs_Boson" title="Higgs Boson">Higgs Boson</a> particle. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-14258601" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Australian_people" title="Australian people">Australian</a> cyclist <a href="/wiki/Cadel_Evans" title="Cadel Evans">Cadel Evans</a> wins the right to wear the <a href="/wiki/General_classification_in_the_Tour_de_France" title="General classification in the Tour de France">yellow jersey</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Champs-%C3%89lys%C3%A9es_stage_in_the_Tour_de_France" title="Champs-Élysées stage in the Tour de France">final stage</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Tour_de_France" title="2011 Tour de France">2011 Tour de France</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/national/cadel-evans-wins-the-tour-de-france/story-e6frfkvr-1226100568298" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li>The world footballing body <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> bans former presidential candidate <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mohamed_Bin_Hammam" title="Mohamed Bin Hammam">Mohamed Bin Hammam</a> for life over claims he tried to buy presidential votes. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/football/14262937.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_24&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_Thai_Armed_Forces" title="Royal Thai Armed Forces">military</a> <a href="/wiki/Helicopter" title="Helicopter">helicopter</a> crashes near the <a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a> border, the third in a week, with three people feared dead in the latest crash. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/43870208" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> port of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a> kills at least eight <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_Yemen" title="Military of Yemen">Army</a> soldiers and wounds scores. <a class="external text" href="http://www.winnipegfreepress.com/world/breakingnews/126078163.html" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press via <i>Winnipeg Free Press</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Television_in_Japan" title="Television in Japan">Japanese television</a> switches totally to <a href="/wiki/Digital_television" title="Digital television">digital television</a> from midday. <a class="external text" href="http://search.japantimes.co.jp/cgi-bin/fd20110724pb.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Japan Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Timothy_Geithner" title="Timothy Geithner">Timothy Geithner</a>, the United States <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Secretary_of_the_Treasury" title="Secretary of the Treasury">Secretary of the Treasury</a>, says that President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> will not invoke the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Constitution" title="United States Constitution">United States Constitution</a> to raise the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Debt_ceiling" title="Debt ceiling">debt ceiling</a> unilaterally. The idea has been under consideration due to the <a href="/wiki/Fourteenth_Amendment_to_the_United_States_Constitution" title="Fourteenth Amendment to the United States Constitution">14th amendment</a> requiring that "the validity of the public debt of the United States [...] shall not be questioned." <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/24/us-usa-debt-geithner-idUSTRE76N15C20110724" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic Party</a> leaders call for the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_Committee_on_Ethics" title="United States House Committee on Ethics">United States House Committee on Ethics</a> to investigate claims that Rep <a href="/wiki/David_Wu" title="David Wu">David Wu</a> of <a href="/wiki/Oregon" title="Oregon">Oregon</a> had <a href="/wiki/Sexual_assault" title="Sexual assault">sexually assaulted</a> a teenager. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/blogs/the-fix/post/democratic-leaders-call-for-ethics-investigation-of-david-wu/2011/07/24/gIQANN4bXI_blog.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/2011_Tour_de_France" title="2011 Tour de France">2011 Tour de France</a> finishes in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cyclist" title="Cyclist">cyclist</a> <a href="/wiki/Cadel_Evans" title="Cadel Evans">Cadel Evans</a> becoming the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Australian_people" title="Australian people">Australian</a> to win the event. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/sport/tour-de-france/cadel-evans-to-become-first-australian-to-win-the-tour-de-france/story-fn8s9i81-1226100674840" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110724-sport-cycling-australia-cadel-evans-wins-tour-de-france" rel="nofollow">(AP via France24)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a> 3-0 in the finals of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2011 Copa América">2011 Copa América</a>, capturing their 15th title and becomes the nation with most Copa América titles. <a class="external text" href="http://nbcsports.msnbc.com/id/43873985/ns/sports-soccer/" rel="nofollow">(AP via NBC Sports)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Tevatron" title="Tevatron">Tevatron</a> collider near <a href="/wiki/Chicago" title="Chicago">Chicago</a> produces results similar to recent results from the <a href="/wiki/Large_Hadron_Collider" title="Large Hadron Collider">Large Hadron Collider (LHC)</a> in the on-going search for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Higgs_Boson" title="Higgs Boson">Higgs Boson</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-14266358" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>Police revise the death toll from the attack down to 76. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/norway/8661257/Norway-killings-police-revise-Norway-death-toll-to-76.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> court decides to try former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President of Egypt</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> and Interior Minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Habib_al-Adly" title="Habib al-Adly">Habib al-Adly</a> together on charges relating to the death of protesters in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">2011 Egyptian revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.maannews.net/eng/ViewDetails.aspx?ID=408391&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Maan News)</a></li>
