<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> cancels fundraising dinners due to the ongoing debt crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://politicalticker.blogs.cnn.com/2011/07/24/obama-cancels-fundraisers-amidst-debt-situation/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>President Obama gives a televised address to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> warning of "incalculable damage" if the debt limit is not raised. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/obama-to-warn-of-incalculable-damage-20110726-1hxj7.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> <a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="Speaker of the United States House of Representatives">Speaker of the United States House of Representatives</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Boehner" title="John Boehner">John Boehner</a> puts forward a plan based on spending cuts. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/house-senate-leaders-unveil-dueling-debt-limit-plans/2011/07/25/gIQApnm1YI_story.html?hpid=z1" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Canada's <a href="/wiki/Leader_of_the_Official_Opposition_(Canada)" title="Leader of the Official Opposition (Canada)">Leader of the Opposition</a> <a href="/wiki/Jack_Layton" title="Jack Layton">Jack Layton</a> announces that he will take a medical leave of absence and an <a href="/wiki/Interim_leader" title="Interim leader">interim leader</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Democratic_Party_(Canada)" title="New Democratic Party (Canada)">New Democratic Party</a> will be appointed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctv.ca/CTVNews/TopStories/20110725/ndp-jack-layton-announcement-110725/" rel="nofollow">(CTV News)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_Administration" title="Obama Administration">Obama Administration</a> released a Strategy to Combat Transnational Organized Crime <a class="external text" href="http://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2011/07/25/remarks-white-house-release-strategy-combat-transnational-organized-crim" rel="nofollow">(whitehouse.gov)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Truong_Tan_Sang" title="Truong Tan Sang">Truong Tan Sang</a> becomes the new <a href="/wiki/President_of_Vietnam" title="President of Vietnam">President of Vietnam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia-pacific/vietnam-announces-new-president-as-country-wrangles-with-economy-china/2011/07/25/gIQArnb8XI_story.html" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a></li>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 26, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-26</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_26&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_26&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_26&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Police in <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a> begin naming the victims of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Norway_attacks" title="2011 Norway attacks">2011 Norway attacks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14300086" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Reserve_Bank_of_India" title="Reserve Bank of India">Reserve Bank of India</a> increases <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Interest_rates" title="Interest rates">interest rates</a> to 8% in an effort to contain <a href="/wiki/Inflation" title="Inflation">inflation</a> which is currently at 9.44%. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14287444" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Britain's <a href="/wiki/Trinity_Mirror" title="Trinity Mirror">Trinity Mirror</a> reviews its editorial guidelines in light of the <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking affair</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://finance.yahoo.com/news/Mirror-to-review-practices-apf-3849737525.html?x=0&amp;.v=1" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo News)</a></li>
<li>U.S. Senator <a href="/wiki/Al_Franken" title="Al Franken">Al Franken</a> of <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">Minnesota</a>, in a letter to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Justice" title="United States Department of Justice">Justice Department</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Communications_Commission" title="Federal Communications Commission">Federal Communications Commission</a>, demands that they block the effort of telephone giant <a href="/wiki/AT%26T" title="AT&amp;T">AT&amp;T</a> to buy rival <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/T-Mobile_USA" title="T-Mobile USA">T-Mobile USA</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/26/us-tmobile-att-antitrust-idUSTRE76P7BV20110726" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Moroccan</a> military transport plane <a href="/wiki/2011_Royal_Moroccan_Air_Force_Lockheed_C-130_Hercules_crash" title="2011 Royal Moroccan Air Force Lockheed C-130 Hercules crash">crashes</a> into a mountain in the south of the country killing 78 of 81 on board. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14290795" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/07/2011726103840621483.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Senior <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> diplomat <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kim_Kye_Gwan" title="Kim Kye Gwan">Kim Kye Gwan</a> heads to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> for discussions on reopening the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Six_party_talks" title="Six party talks">six party talks</a> on his country's <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">nuclear weapons program</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/26/0200000000AEN20110726005400315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Senegal" title="Senegal">Senegalese</a> rapper and government critic <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Omar_Toure&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Omar Toure (page does not exist)">Omar Toure</a> is arrested. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14288491" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Sri_Lanka" title="Law enforcement in Sri Lanka">Sri Lankan police</a> hunt for 20 local television actresses alleged to be part of a <a href="/wiki/Prostitution" title="Prostitution">prostitution</a> ring. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/entertainment/2011-07/26/c_131010170.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A shootout at a prison in <a href="/wiki/Ciudad_Ju%C3%A1rez" title="Ciudad Juárez">Ciudad Juárez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>, leaves 17 dead. <a class="external text" href="http://latino.foxnews.com/latino/news/2011/07/26/17-inmates-die-in-shootout-at-prison-in-mexican-border-city/" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
<li>David Cecil, an unemployed truck driver, is charged with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Computer_crime" title="Computer crime">hacking</a> into <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Platform_Networks&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Platform Networks (page does not exist)">Platform Networks</a>'s network. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kansascity.com/2011/07/26/3038902/man-charged-with-hacking-into.html" rel="nofollow">(Kansas City Star)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/stories/2011/07/26/ap/asia/main20083884.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/nation/hacker-accused-of-threat-to-national-broadband-network/story-e6frg6nf-1226102794463" rel="nofollow">(The Australian)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nguyen_Tan_Dung" title="Nguyen Tan Dung">Nguyen Tan Dung</a> is re-elected <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Vietnam" title="Prime Minister of Vietnam">Prime Minister of Vietnam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.gov.vn/Home/VNs-Prime-Minister-reelected/20117/11147.vgp" rel="nofollow">(Government Web Portal of Vietnam)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Wu" title="David Wu">David Wu</a> resigns as a member of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> following allegations of an unwanted sexual encounter with an 18-year-old. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/aponline/2011/07/26/us/politics/AP-US-Wu-Sex-Scandal.html?_r=1&amp;emc=na" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Luis_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Luis Gutiérrez">Luis Gutiérrez</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Illinois" title="Illinois">Illinois</a> member of the United States House of Representatives, is arrested outside the <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_D.C." title="Washington D.C.">Washington D.C.</a> during protests calling for immigration reform. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rollcall.com/news/gutierrez_arrested_during_immigration_protest-207724-1.html" rel="nofollow">(Rollcall)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Dog" title="Dog">dog</a> is discovered carrying the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hendra_virus" title="Hendra virus">hendra virus</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> near the town of <a href="/wiki/Beaudesert,_Queensland" title="Beaudesert, Queensland">Beaudesert</a>. It is the first time the virus has been detected in a species other than <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flying_fox" title="Flying fox">flying foxes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">horses</a> or <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">humans</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/national/dog-near-beaudesert-believed-to-be-the-first-of-species-detected-with-the-hendra-virus/story-e6frfkvr-1226102106856" rel="nofollow">(AAP via News Limited)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_27&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Norway_attacks" title="2011 Norway attacks">2011 Norway attacks</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Norway" title="Law enforcement in Norway">Norwegian police</a> start releasing the names of the victims of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Norway_attacks" title="2011 Norway attacks">2011 Norway attacks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/world/oslo-police-release-names-of-norway-bomb-and-massacre-victims/story-e6frfkz9-1226102486916" rel="nofollow">(AP via News Limited)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Norway" title="Prime Minister of Norway">Prime Minister of Norway</a> <a href="/wiki/Jens_Stoltenberg" title="Jens Stoltenberg">Jens Stoltenberg</a> promises to set up a security review. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110727-norway-pm-vows-security-review-after-massacre-mourning-stoltenberg" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan (2001–present)</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ghulam_Haidar_Hameedi" title="Ghulam Haidar Hameedi">Ghulam Haidar Hameedi</a>, mayor of <a href="/wiki/Kandahar" title="Kandahar">Kandahar</a>, is killed in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bombing" title="Suicide bombing">suicide bombing</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://gulfnews.com/news/world/afghanistan/kandahar-mayor-killed-in-suicide-attack-afghan-police-1.843633" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Gulf News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> intervenes in the <a href="/wiki/North_Kosovo_crisis" title="North Kosovo crisis">border clashes</a> between <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14303165" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Australian_dollar" title="Australian dollar">Australian dollar</a> reaches a post-float record against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">United States dollar</a> based on higher than expected <a href="/wiki/Consumer_price_index" title="Consumer price index">consumer price index</a> figures and concerns over a US <a href="/wiki/Default_(finance)" title="Default (finance)">default</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://au.finance.yahoo.com/news/-A-breaks-post-flat-record-aap-4291307119.html?x=0" rel="nofollow">(AAP via Yahoo Finance)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Seventeen people are killed in <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">landslides</a> in <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> caused by heavy rain including eight in the town of <a href="/wiki/Chuncheon" title="Chuncheon">Chuncheon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/27/81/0200000000AEN20110727003700315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/A/AS_SKOREA_LANDSLIDE?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/World_Food_Programme" title="World Food Programme">World Food Programme</a> prepares an airlift to <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a> in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> to help relieve the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Horn_of_Africa_famine" title="2011 Horn of Africa famine">2011 Horn of Africa famine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110727-un-readies-aid-airlift-mogadishu-0" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France24)</a></li>
<li>At least seventeen people are dead and 25 missing after <a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2011 Pacific typhoon season">Severe Tropical Storm Nock-ten (Juaning)</a> hits the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-07/27/c_131013786.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_storm" title="Tropical storm">tropical storm</a> watch is issued for <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Don_(2011)" title="Tropical Storm Don (2011)">Tropical Storm Don</a> in the US state of <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> between <a href="/wiki/Port_Mansfield,_Texas" title="Port Mansfield, Texas">Port Mansfield</a> north to <a href="/wiki/San_Luis_Pass" title="San Luis Pass">San Luis Pass</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/text/refresh/MIATCPAT4+shtml/272053.shtml" rel="nofollow">(National Hurricane Centre)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/news/specials/hurricane/" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Government of the United Kingdom">Government of the United Kingdom</a> expels <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> diplomats loyal to <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> from the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> and recognises the <a href="/wiki/National_Transitional_Council" title="National Transitional Council">National Transitional Council</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com/news/world/as-libya-settles-into-stalemate-the-west-grasps-for-a-way-out/article2112337/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Globe and Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli_army" title="Israeli army">Israeli army</a> arrests two men involved in running the Freedom Theatre founded in <a href="/wiki/Jenin" title="Jenin">Jenin</a> by murdered Israeli actor <a href="/wiki/Juliano_Mer-Khamis" title="Juliano Mer-Khamis">Juliano Mer-Khamis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.maannews.net/eng/ViewDetails.aspx?ID=408710" rel="nofollow">(Ma'an)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4100943,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynet)</a></li>
<li>An unruly crowd riots on <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Boulevard" title="Hollywood Boulevard">Hollywood Boulevard</a> outside <a href="/wiki/Grauman%27s_Chinese_Theatre" title="Grauman's Chinese Theatre">Grauman's Chinese Theatre</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hollywood,_California" title="Hollywood, California">Hollywood</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> after being refused admission to a documentary on the <a href="/wiki/Electric_Daisy_Carnival" title="Electric Daisy Carnival">Electric Daisy Carnival</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://losangeles.cbslocal.com/2011/07/27/unruly-crowds-setting-fires-vandalizing-police-cars-near-graumanns/#.TjDe2hikvVI.tweet" rel="nofollow">(CBS Los Angeles)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbclosangeles.com/news/local/Cancelled-Movie-Promps-Crowd-Disturbance-on-Hollywood-Boulevard-126297928.html" rel="nofollow">(NBC Los Angeles)</a></li>
<li>Two men are convicted in <a href="/wiki/St._John%27s,_Antigua_and_Barbuda" title="St. John's, Antigua and Barbuda">St John's</a>, <a href="/wiki/Antigua" title="Antigua">Antigua</a> of the 2008 <a href="/wiki/Antigua_honeymoon_murders" title="Antigua honeymoon murders">murders</a> of <a href="/wiki/British_people" title="British people">British</a> <a href="/wiki/Honeymoon" title="Honeymoon">honeymoon</a> couple Ben and Catherine Mullany. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/centralamericaandthecaribbean/antiguaandbarbuda/8667067/Antigua-honeymoon-murders-two-men-found-guilty.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>
<ul>
<li>Former <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mirror" title="Daily Mirror">Daily Mirror</a></i> editor <a href="/wiki/Piers_Morgan" title="Piers Morgan">Piers Morgan</a> says comments he made in 2009 on <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_4" title="BBC Radio 4">BBC Radio 4</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Desert_Island_Discs" title="Desert Island Discs">Desert Island Discs</a></i> do not suggest he printed stories obtained through illegal reporting. In the programme, he had spoken of "running the results" of work by third parties who did "rake through bins... tap people's phones". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14311382" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>An 18 year old man in the <a href="/wiki/Shetland" title="Shetland">Shetland</a> Islands of <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a> is arrested on suspicion of launching multiple <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Distributed_denial_of_service" title="Distributed denial of service">distributed denial of service</a> attacks in association with <a href="/wiki/LulzSec" title="LulzSec">LulzSec</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anonymous_(group)" title="Anonymous (group)">Anonymous</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14315442" rel="nofollow">(BCC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republicans</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> announce they will delay a vote on extending the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Debt_ceiling" title="Debt ceiling">debt ceiling</a> until Thursday due to concerns over level of proposed savings not being sufficient. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/boehner-presses-debt-plan-opposed-by-democrats-imf-urges-raise-in-debt-limit/2011/07/26/gIQA0s3taI_story.html?wpisrc=al_national" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spanish_people" title="Spanish people">Spanish</a> protesters known as the "Indignants" begin a march from <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a> to <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> in <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> to protest at cuts in government expenditure in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14302607?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least seven <a href="/wiki/Philippine_Army" title="Philippine Army">Philippine Army</a> soldiers are killed and 21 injured in a confrontation with <a href="/wiki/Abu_Sayyaf" title="Abu Sayyaf">Abu Sayyaf</a> militants on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jolo_Island" title="Jolo Island">Jolo Island</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.monstersandcritics.com/news/asiapacific/news/article_1653620.php/Seven-soldiers-killed-in-fighting-in-southern-Philippines" rel="nofollow">(DPA via Monsters and Critics)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> accuses <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a> of attempting to bomb an <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> summit in <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14335752" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Assassination" title="Assassination">Assassins</a> kill the military commander of <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>'s <a href="/wiki/National_Transitional_Council" title="National Transitional Council">National Transitional Council</a> General <a href="/wiki/Abdul_Fatah_Younis" title="Abdul Fatah Younis">Abdul Fatah Younis</a> and two other officers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/29/world/africa/29libya.html?_r=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan (2001–present)</a>:
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> attack in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Uruzgan" title="Uruzgan">Uruzgan</a> province kills 21 people including a <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> reporter <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ahmed_Omed_Khpulwak" title="Ahmed Omed Khpulwak">Ahmed Omed Khpulwak</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/asia/afghanistan/8669677/BBC-reporter-among-21-killed-in-Afghanistan-attacks.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Swiss</a> bank <a href="/wiki/Credit_Suisse" title="Credit Suisse">Credit Suisse</a> announces plans to cut 2,000 jobs due to poor profit results. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/28/us-creditsuisse-idUSTRE76R0MI20110728?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> electronics company <a href="/wiki/Sony" title="Sony">Sony</a> reduces sales and profit forecasts due to the <a href="/wiki/2011_T%C5%8Dhoku_earthquake_and_tsunami" title="2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami">2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(computer_security)" title="Hacker (computer security)">computer hacking</a> attack and slowing demand in the US and Europe. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-07-28/sony-trims-full-year-net-income-forecast-by-25-lowers-outlook-for-sales.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Asiana_Airlines_Flight_991" title="Asiana Airlines Flight 991">Asiana Airlines Flight 991</a> crashes in the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>, near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jeju_Island" title="Jeju Island">Jeju Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>, killing 2 onboard. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110728-asiana-airlines-cargo-plane-crashes-off-skorea" rel="nofollow">(France24)</a></li>
<li>At least 57 people are dead and 12 are confirmed missing in the <a href="/wiki/Seoul" title="Seoul">Seoul</a> and <a href="/wiki/Siheung" title="Siheung">Siheung</a> region of <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> due to <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">landslides</a> caused by heavy rain. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctv.ca/CTVNews/World/20110728/mudslide-aftermath-search-korea-110728/" rel="nofollow">(CTV News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/world/torrential-rains-kill-36-in-south-korea/story-e6frf7lo-1226103249578" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theweathernetwork.com/news/storm_watch_stories3&amp;stormfile=scores_dead_or_missing_after_280711" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Weather Network</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 17 people are killed and 30 injured after a truck collides with a bus in the <a href="/wiki/Bogra_District" title="Bogra District">Bogra District</a> of <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-07/28/c_131015146.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Horn_of_Africa_famine" title="2011 Horn of Africa famine">2011 Horn of Africa famine</a>: <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> peacekeepers launch a major offensive against <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al-Shabaab</a> militants in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, Somalia, in order to reduce threats to relief efforts. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-14323426" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Authorities in the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> say more than 100 people are feared dead after two boats collided on <a href="/wiki/Tshuapa_River" title="Tshuapa River">Tshuapa River</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2011/07/28/more-than-100-feared-dead-in-congo-boat-accident/" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> resumes sending food aid to <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> to assist with chronic food shortages. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/28/38/0200000000AEN20110728002600315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap News)</a></li>

<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>:
<ul>
<li>Police tell the mother of murder victim <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Sarah_Payne" title="Murder of Sarah Payne">Sarah Payne</a> that her mobile phone details have been found in notes made by private investigator <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Mulcaire" title="Glenn Mulcaire">Glenn Mulcaire</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-14332689" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lord_Justice" title="Lord Justice">Lord Justice</a> <a href="/wiki/Brian_Leveson" title="Brian Leveson">Leveson</a> sets out some of the details of the forthcoming <a href="/wiki/Leveson_Inquiry" title="Leveson Inquiry">inquiry into the phone hacking affair</a>, which will begin in September. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14325466" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>In a legal milestone, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_Court_of_England_and_Wales" title="High Court of England and Wales">High Court of England and Wales</a> rules that <a href="/wiki/BT_Group" title="BT Group">BT Group</a> must block access to <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Newzbin_2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Newzbin 2 (page does not exist)">Newzbin 2</a>, a members-only website providing links to pirated movies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/technology-14322957" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_England_and_Wales" title="Supreme Court of England and Wales">Supreme Court of England and Wales</a> grants veterans involved in <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapons_tests_in_Australia" title="Nuclear weapons tests in Australia">Britain's nuclear weapons tests during the 1950s</a> leave to appeal in their fight for compensation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14320465" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Tunisia" title="President of Tunisia">President of Tunisia</a> <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a> is sentenced to 16 years in absentia for corruption and property fraud. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/middle-east/Ex-Tunisian-President-Ben-Ali-given-16-years-for-corruption/articleshow/9402875.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Boehner" title="John Boehner">John Boehner</a> delays a vote on the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_U.S._debt_ceiling_crisis" title="2011 U.S. debt ceiling crisis">debt ceiling legislation</a> with the issue deferred until at least Friday. <a class="external text" href="http://thecaucus.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/07/28/house-delays-budget-vote/?emc=na" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/house-gop-leader-no-vote-tonight-on-debt-limit-bill/2011/07/28/gIQA1Gt5fI_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Astronomers using the <a href="/wiki/Wide-field_Infrared_Survey_Explorer" title="Wide-field Infrared Survey Explorer">Wide-field Infrared Survey Explorer</a> telescope identify a <a href="/wiki/Trojan_asteroid" title="Trojan asteroid">Trojan asteroid</a>, calling it <i><a href="/wiki/2010_TK7" title="2010 TK7">2010 TK<sub>7</sub></a></i>, orbiting on the same path as the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Earth_(planet)" title="Earth (planet)">Earth</a> around the <a href="/wiki/Sun" title="Sun">Sun</a>. The rock poses no danger to the Earth since it sits in a what is termed a gravitational "sweet spot". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-14307987" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nature.com/nature/journal/v475/n7357/full/nature10233.html" rel="nofollow">(Nature)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Swimming_(sport)" title="Swimming (sport)">swimming</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Lochte" title="Ryan Lochte">Ryan Lochte</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_at_the_2011_World_Aquatics_Championships" title="United States at the 2011 World Aquatics Championships">United States</a> sets a new world record in the 200-meter <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Individual_medley" title="Individual medley">individual medley</a> in winning a gold medal at the <a href="/wiki/2011_World_Aquatics_Championships" title="2011 World Aquatics Championships">2011 World Aquatics Championships</a> in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a>. Lochte becomes the first person to set a long-course world record since <a href="/wiki/FINA" title="FINA">FINA</a> banned rubberized swimsuits in 2010. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/gameon/post/2011/07/lochte-beats-phelps-with-world-record-time/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">soccer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bob_Bradley" title="Bob Bradley">Bob Bradley</a> is dismissed as manager of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men's national soccer team">United States men's national soccer team</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/sports/soccer/news/_/id/6812931/bob-bradley-dismissed-us-men-soccer-national-team-coach" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_uprising" title="2011 Syrian uprising">2011 Syrian uprising</a>
<ul>
<li>An oil pipeline near the city of <a href="/wiki/Homs" title="Homs">Homs</a> is blown up by "saboteurs", according to the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Arab_News_Agency" title="Syrian Arab News Agency">state news agency</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/29/us-syria-deaths-idUSTRE76S75820110729?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FworldNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+International%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Syrian forces kill at least 20 civilians in attacks on several pro-democracy demonstrations across <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/29/us-syria-deaths-idUSTRE76S75820110729?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FworldNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+International%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_uprising" title="2011 Bahraini uprising">2011 Bahraini uprising</a>: <a href="/wiki/King_of_Bahrain" title="King of Bahrain">King</a> <a href="/wiki/Hamad_bin_Isa_Al_Khalifa" title="Hamad bin Isa Al Khalifa">Hamad bin Isa Al Khalifa</a> approves parliamentary reforms, which are rejected by opposition groups. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201172955558583141.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Tunisian_revolution" title="2011 Tunisian revolution">2011 Tunisian revolution</a>: Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Tunisia" title="President of Tunisia">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a> is sentenced <i><a href="/wiki/Trial_in_absentia" title="Trial in absentia">in absentia</a></i> to 16 years imprisonment for corruption. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-07/29/c_131018174.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Johnson_%26_Johnson" title="Johnson &amp; Johnson">Johnson &amp; Johnson</a> announced that it will lower the maximum daily <a href="/wiki/Dose_(biochemistry)" title="Dose (biochemistry)">dosage</a> of one of its signature products, Extra Strength <a href="/wiki/Tylenol_(brand)" title="Tylenol (brand)">Tylenol</a>, in order to reduce the risk of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liver_damage" title="Liver damage">liver damage</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/29/us-tylenol-idUSTRE76S52220110729" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Pay-TV company <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BSkyB" title="BSkyB">BSkyB</a> secures a seven year deal to share the United Kingdom broadcasting rights of <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> racing. From March 2012 half the races will air on Sky, while the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> retains the right to show the other half. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-07-29/bskyb-to-show-formula-1-races-in-deal-that-takes-exclusivity-from-bbc.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Polish</a> report into the <a href="/wiki/2010_Polish_Air_Force_Tu-154_crash" title="2010 Polish Air Force Tu-154 crash">2010 Polish Air Force Tu-154 crash</a> that killed <a href="/wiki/President_of_Poland" title="President of Poland">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Lech_Kaczy%C5%84ski" title="Lech Kaczyński">Lech Kaczyński</a> blames the Polish crew and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> air traffic controllers for the accident. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2011/07/29/Report-spreads-blame-for-Polish-jet-crash/UPI-42551311938571/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_South_Korea" title="Prime Minister of South Korea">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kim_Hwang-sik" title="Kim Hwang-sik">Kim Hwang-sik</a>, calls for an overhaul of disaster management following the death of 59 people in floods and landslides caused by heavy rain in recent days. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/07/29/0200000000AEN20110729003200315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li>At least twenty <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coal_mine" title="Coal mine">coal miners</a> are killed and seventeen are missing following <a href="/wiki/2011_Ukraine_mine_accidents" title="2011 Ukraine mine accidents">two accidents</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctv.ca/CTVNews/World/20110729/ukraine-mining-accidents-110729/" rel="nofollow">(CTV News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hsEW7iINVQ1vvOi97F0wLYw8wPGw?docId=4ac382e84c3d40d08ff8ccf02b0107ae" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> joins the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> as its 54<sup>th</sup> member. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehindu.com/news/international/article2305415.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hindu</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> threatens to dispose of <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> assets at the jointly-run <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/K%C5%ADmgangsan_Tourist_Region" title="Kŭmgangsan Tourist Region">Mount Kumgang resort</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/07/29/uk-korea-north-kumgang-idUSLNE76S01820110729" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The Chief of the armed forces along with the heads of the army, navy and air force all resign in <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-14346325" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ajmal_Kasab" title="Ajmal Kasab">Ajmal Kasab</a>, the last surviving gunman from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Mumbai_terrorist_attacks" title="2008 Mumbai terrorist attacks">2008 Mumbai terrorist attacks</a>, launches an appeal against his death sentence in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/india/Kasab-appeals-death-sentence/articleshow/9406042.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/home/world-news/article/16039587" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>
<ul>
<li>The legal team representing <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Mulcaire" title="Glenn Mulcaire">Glenn Mulcaire</a>, the private investigator at the centre of claims of phone hacking, says that he "acted on the instructions of others". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14346083" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>MPs on the <a href="/wiki/Culture,_Media_and_Sport_Committee" title="Culture, Media and Sport Committee">Culture, Media and Sport Committee</a> vote not to recall <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Murdoch_(media_executive)" title="James Murdoch (media executive)">James Murdoch</a> after his evidence was called into question by two senior <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> executives. However, he may have to appear again later after more evidence is heard. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14336691" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peta_Buscombe,_Baroness_Buscombe" title="Peta Buscombe, Baroness Buscombe">Baroness Peta Buscombe</a> announces her intention to step down as Chair of the <a href="/wiki/Press_Complaints_Commission" title="Press Complaints Commission">Press Complaints Commission</a> following criticism about the way she handled the scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14342217" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Broadcaster <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BSkyB" title="BSkyB">BSkyB</a> announces its intention to return $1bn to shareholders angered by the recent fall in its share prices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-14338032" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Appearing in court, protester Jonathan May-Bowles admits to throwing a foam pie at <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Murdoch" title="Rupert Murdoch">Rupert Murdoch</a> as he gave evidence to a Parliamentary Committee. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-london-14339271" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Christopher Jefferies, an early suspect in the <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Joanna_Yeates" title="Murder of Joanna Yeates">investigation into the murder of Joanna Yeates</a>, accepts "substantial" libel damages from eight British newspapers after they published details of his private life. <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sun_(United_Kingdom)" title="The Sun (United Kingdom)">The Sun</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mirror" title="Daily Mirror">Daily Mirror</a></i> are also fined for <a href="/wiki/Contempt_of_court" title="Contempt of court">contempt of court</a> in their reporting of the investigation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14342766" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>UK based Internet blogger Bilal Zaheer Ahmad is sentenced to 12 years imprisonment after admitting using his blog to solicit the murder of MPs who voted for the <a href="/wiki/Iraq_War" title="Iraq War">Iraq War</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-14344199" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A U.S. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Court_of_Appeals" title="Court of Appeals">Court of Appeals</a> holds that isolated DNA is "markedly different" in its chemical structure from the DNA within chromosomes, and thus is not simply a product of nature but of human ingenuity. According, the court upholds two <a href="/wiki/Patent" title="Patent">patents</a> held by <a href="/wiki/Myriad_Genetics" title="Myriad Genetics">Myriad Genetics</a> against challenge. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/30/business/gene-patent-in-cancer-test-upheld-by-appeals-panel.html" rel="nofollow">(New York Times)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> votes to increase the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_public_debt" title="United States public debt">debt ceiling</a> but the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">Senate</a> rejects it. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wtsp.com/news/article/203483/250/House-passes-Senate-rejects-debt-bill" rel="nofollow">(WTSP)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Spain" title="Prime Minister of Spain">Prime Minister of Spain</a> <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Rodr%C3%ADguez_Zapatero" title="José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero">José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero</a> calls an early election for November 20 rather than 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://latino.foxnews.com/latino/politics/2011/07/29/spanish-elections-moved-up-to-november/" rel="nofollow">(EFE via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/J%C3%BCrgen_Klinsmann" title="Jürgen Klinsmann">Jürgen Klinsmann</a> is named head coach of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men's national soccer team">United States men's national soccer team</a>, one day after <a href="/wiki/Bob_Bradley" title="Bob Bradley">Bob Bradley</a> was relieved as coach. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/sports/soccer/news/_/id/6815761/juergen-klinsmann-hired-coach-us-men-soccer-national-team" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 30, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-30</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_30&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_30&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_30&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_Civil_War" title="2011 Libyan Civil War">Libyan Civil War</a>:
<ul>
<li>(<a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> claims to have destroyed three television distribution facilities in an airstrike on <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://nitv.hq.nato.int/index.php?getit&amp;username=c73ccd0ec219a79bead2878113b28c89&amp;password=15cca983242ee1f410590585b30ae430&amp;dirId=78616" rel="nofollow">(NATO)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least thirteen people are killed when gunmen open fire at passengers near a bus stop in <a href="/wiki/Quetta" title="Quetta">Quetta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-07/30/c_131019424.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Suspected <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_the_Philippines" title="Communist Party of the Philippines">Communist Party of the Philippines</a> <a href="/wiki/New_People%27s_Army" title="New People's Army">New People's Army</a> forces attack a police station in <a href="/wiki/Agusan_del_Sur" title="Agusan del Sur">Agusan del Sur</a> killing a civilian and wounding two police officers. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-07/30/c_131019428.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zara_Phillips" title="Zara Phillips">Zara Phillips</a>, granddaughter of <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a>, marries <a href="/wiki/England_national_rugby_union_team" title="England national rugby union team">England rugby union international</a> <a href="/wiki/Mike_Tindall" title="Mike Tindall">Mike Tindall</a> in a ceremony at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canongate_Kirk" title="Canongate Kirk">Canongate Kirk</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Edinburgh,_Scotland" title="Edinburgh, Scotland">Edinburgh, Scotland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-scotland-edinburgh-east-fife-14344093" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 17 people are killed in a fire at a shoe factory in the <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnamese</a> city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hai_Phong" title="Hai Phong">Hai Phong</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-14352275?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/News_International_phone_hacking_scandal" title="News International phone hacking scandal">News International phone hacking scandal</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police_Service" title="Metropolitan Police Service">Metropolitan Police</a> launches <a href="/wiki/Operation_Tuleta" title="Operation Tuleta">Operation Tuleta</a> to investigate allegations of computer hacking by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_International" title="News International">News International</a> journalists. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-14351004" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_people" title="Mexican people">Mexican</a> media reports that hitman <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jose_Antonio_Acosta_Hernandez" title="Jose Antonio Acosta Hernandez">José Antonio Acosta Hernández</a>, associated with the <a href="/wiki/La_L%C3%ADnea_(gang)" title="La Línea (gang)">La Línea</a> gang, is arrested in <a href="/wiki/Chihuahua_(state)" title="Chihuahua (state)">Chihuahua</a> in connection to killing <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> consular official and murders at a <a href="/wiki/Ciudad_Ju%C3%A1rez" title="Ciudad Juárez">Juarez</a> birthday party. <a class="external text" href="http://www.elpasotimes.com/ci_18581826" rel="nofollow">(<i>El Paso Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Four people are shot and one killed after a <a href="/wiki/George_Clinton_(musician)" title="George Clinton (musician)">George Clinton</a> concert in the US city of <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">Cleveland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.19actionnews.com/story/15180524/ems-four-people-shot-during-george-clinton-concert-at-e116th-and-kinsman" rel="nofollow">(19 Action News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Mixed_martial_arts" title="Mixed martial arts">mixed martial arts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dan_Henderson" title="Dan Henderson">Dan Henderson</a> defeats fellow former <a href="/wiki/Pride_Fighting_Championships" title="Pride Fighting Championships">Pride Fighting Championships</a> title holder <a href="/wiki/Fedor_Emelianenko" title="Fedor Emelianenko">Fedor Emelianenko</a> via <a href="/wiki/Knockout" title="Knockout">knockout</a> in the first round of their bout at <i><a href="/wiki/Strikeforce:_Fedor_vs._Henderson" title="Strikeforce: Fedor vs. Henderson">Strikeforce: Fedor vs. Henderson</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sherdog.com/news/news/Henderson-Stops-Fedor-in-First-34398" rel="nofollow">(Sherdog)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/2011_AFL_season#Round_19" title="2011 AFL season">Round 19 of the Australian Football League season</a>, <a href="/wiki/Geelong_Football_Club" title="Geelong Football Club">Geelong</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Football_Club" title="Melbourne Football Club">Melbourne</a> by a near-record 186 points; the loss results in <a href="/wiki/Dean_Bailey" title="Dean Bailey">Dean Bailey</a> being sacked as coach of the latter team the following day. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/sport/dean-bailey-sacked-as-melbourne-coach/story-e6frg7mf-1226105585751" rel="nofollow">The Australian</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> July 31, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-07-31</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_31&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_July_31&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 9 people including a suspect are killed and 28 others are injured in a knife attack in <a href="/wiki/Kashgar" title="Kashgar">Kashgar</a>, west <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>, marking the second attack of the month in Xinjiang. <a class="external text" href="http://english.cri.cn/6909/2011/08/01/1781s651239.htm" rel="nofollow">(CRI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-07/31/c_131020413.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia-pacific/7-dead-22-injured-in-northwest-china-after-knife-bearing-men-hijack-truck-and-attack-crowd/2011/07/31/gIQA1AbRkI_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ramadan_Massacre" title="Ramadan Massacre">Ramadan Massacre</a>:
<ul>
<li>At least 121 people are killed in a <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> tank raid on the town of <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> and over 150 people are reportedly killed across the country. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/201173143432348733.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/07/2011731183142996341.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Jazeera)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://english.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/07/31/160188.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Arabiya)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least seven people drown after a collision between a pleasure boat and a barge in central <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://themoscownews.com/local/20110731/188886418.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Moscow News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=231733" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>No-one was killed when a <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Airlines" title="Caribbean Airlines">Caribbean Airlines</a> Boeing 737 plane crashed and split in two at the Cheddi Jagan International Airport, <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.tt/news/2011/07/31/huge-scare-163-aboard-cal-aircraft" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Trinidad Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexican</a> <a href="/wiki/Federal_Police_(Mexico)" title="Federal Police (Mexico)">Federal Police</a> say suspected cartel leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jose_Antonio_Acosta_Hernandez" title="Jose Antonio Acosta Hernandez">José Antonio Acosta Hernández</a>, who was arrested on Friday, has confessed to ordering the murder of 1,500 people in the country's northern state of <a href="/wiki/Chihuahua_(state)" title="Chihuahua (state)">Chihuahua</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-14360288" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_U.S._debt_ceiling_crisis" title="2011 U.S. debt ceiling crisis">2011 U.S. debt ceiling crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senate of the United States</a> fails to pass legislation lifting the debt ceiling with compromise talks continuing. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/POLITICS/07/30/debt.talks/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/08/01/us/politics/01FISCAL.html?_r=1&amp;hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, the <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a>, and <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">Congressional</a> leaders reach a deal on extending the debt ceiling. <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/international-business/barack-obama-and-congressional-leaders-strike-a-deal-for-raising-us-debt-limit/articleshow/9437937.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Economic Times</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/reid-signs-off-on-debt-deal-hopes-for-vote/2011/07/31/gIQALCW4lI_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_US_debt_ceiling_crisis" title="2011 US debt ceiling crisis">2011 US debt ceiling crisis</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Financial_crisis_of_2007%E2%80%932010" title="Financial crisis of 2007–2010">Global financial crisis</a>

</ul>
